# 高上神霄玉清真王紫书大法

**High Supreme Daoist Scripture of the Celestial Palace: The *Zishu* Scripture of the High Supreme Daoist Sovereign of the Jade Purity**

**Author Unknown**, composed approximately in the late Northern Song or early Southern Song dynasty.
A scripture of the **Shenxiao** Daoist sect. Twelve volumes.
Source of the base text: *Zhengtong Daozang* Canon, First Proper Division.

**Preface to the *Zishu* Scripture of the High Supreme Daoist Sovereign of the Celestial Palace**

In antiquity, before the **Great Void** (*Taikong*) was formed and the **original *qi*** (*yuánqì*) emerged,
the **Original Beginning Heavenly Sovereign** (*Yuánshǐ Tiānwáng*), as progenitor of the **vast and boundless Great Brahman** (*hàománg dàfán*), condensed his spirit and conceived a form, named it **Hundun** (混沌).
When **Hundun** was dispersed, the **original *qi*** of heaven and earth, within and without, was manifest—then called **Hunxu** (混虚).
The **Original Beginning Heavenly Sovereign**, through his transformative power, unfolded the cosmic pattern.
His golden visage shone like the sun, his jade likeness radiated like the heavens.
He nurtured the **wondrous essence** (*miàojīng*), partitioning the **Heavenly and Earthly** (*qiánkūn*).
Thus, descending from the **Jade Capital** (*Yùjīng*) mountain and ascending through the celestial realms,
he encountered the **Primordial Mother of Ten Thousand *Qi*** (*Tà Xuán Yùjí Yuánjǐng Zìrán Jiǔtiān Shàng Xuán Yùqīng Shénmǔ*), the **Great Ancestral Mother of the Nine Heavens**,
and practiced the **Dao of the Great Cavern of the High Supreme Purity** (*Shàngqīng Dàdòng Cīxióng Sānyī Hùnhuà*), the **triune unity of yin and yang**,
and bore eight children.

The eldest was the **Long-Lived Sovereign of the Southern Extremity** (*Nánjí Chángshēng Dàdì*), also known as the **Great Sovereign of the Nine Dragons and the Fuxi Sun Palace** (*Jiǔlóng Fúsāng Rìgōng Dàdì*), also known as the **High Supreme Daoist Sovereign of the Jade Purity** (*Gāoshàng Shénxiāo Yùqīng Wáng*).
One body, three names—his holiness is singular.

The **High Supreme Daoist Sovereign of the Celestial Palace** (*Shénxiāo Zhēnwáng*), with his spirit condensed at the **Golden Gate** (*Jīnquè*),
reflected upon the world and all beings,
the **three calamities and eight hardships** (*sānzāi bānàn*) of all suffering,
the **nine abyssal prisons and the Green Anticipation** (*jiǔyōu quánchéng*), where all guilty souls endure retribution,
the endless torments that never cease day or night,
the **cyclic wheel of birth and death** (*shēngsǐ wǎnglái*).
Now, with my **divine powers** (*shéntōnglì*), I pity all beings in the **Three Realms** (*sānjiè*),
and thus proceed to the **Jade Purity Heaven** (*Yùqīng Tiān*), beneath the **Golden Gate of the Original Beginning Heavenly Sovereign** (*Yuánshǐ Shàngdì Jīnquè*).
With reverent offerings, I beseech the **Purple Microstar Celestial Palace** (*Zǐwēi Shànggōng*), the **Purple Jade and Precious Orchid** (*Zǐyù Qióngruǐ*) scriptures,
and within the **Nine Heavens Treasure Register** (*Jiǔxiāo Bǎogǔ*), I request the **Secret Dao of the High Supreme Sovereign** (*Shénxiāo Zhēnwáng Mìfǎ*), three volumes in total,
all composed of **Brahmanic *qi*** (*fánqì*), the **scriptures of the Nine Heavens’ Great Primordial Clouds and Mist** (*Jiǔtiān Tà Xuán Yúnxiá*).
The **uppermost** (*shàng*) conceals the **prohibitions of the Ten Thousand Heavens** (*wàn tiān zhǐjìn*);
the **middle** (*zhōng*) conceals the **Dao of immortality spanning Ten Thousand Years** (*shénxiān wànián fǎ*).

The **lower** (*xià*) reveals the **Dao of governing humanity and pacifying ghosts**—securing the state and bringing peace to the family.

The **Original Beginning Heavenly Sovereign** thus decreed to the **Supreme Lord of Ten Thousand Blessings, the True Prince** (*Tàihuáng Wànfú Zhēnjūn*), to transmit the **High Supreme Sovereign’s Secret Dao of the Jade Pure Palace for Long Life and Protection of Life** (*Gāoshàng Shénxiāo Yùqīng Wáng Chángshēng Hùmìng Fǎ*) to the mortal realm, first instructing me to propagate it among those in the world who seek the **Dao**, so that they may **wear the law and cultivate**, making it a lasting treasure for their bodies.

Above, it **defends emperors and kings**, stabilizing the land and ensuring a reign of **ten thousand years**.
Below, it **benefits the people**, extending life and delivering them from calamity, so that those who study the **Dao** may attain its truth.

With **face-bowed reverence to the True King**, one **drives away the Six Heavens** and **subdues demons and spirits**.
It is used to **issue talismans and edicts**, summoning and binding ghosts and gods.

As the **High Supreme Sovereign** has commanded, and as the **hundreds of millions of ancestors**—the **lineage of the sacred lineage and kindred spirits**—have ascended beyond suffering, one’s **single body is blessed**, and **ten thousand generations enjoy honor**.

Next, it enables the practitioner to **attain the Dao**, achieving **corporeal ascension and hidden transcendence**, ensuring its transmission through generations, with the **law safeguarded** so that the **Dao may flourish**.
Those who **leak, reveal, or grow lax**—facing the **Wind Knife Trial**—shall not be pardoned even after **ten thousand kalpas**.
Scholars who practice this must **strictly adhere** to it.

---
**The Great Dao Source of the Supreme Law**
**Volume One of the Purple Scripture Great Law of the High Supreme Sovereign of the Jade Pure Palace**

Within the **Great Luo Purple Treasury of the Nine Heavens**, there exist **all the celestial bureaus**.
The **assemblies of the Celestial Emperors**, the **Heavenly Sovereign’s Gate**—with **twelve thousand eight hundred** subordinate domains, each with its officials—**examine the virtues and transgressions of mortals**, recording none in official registers, yet all as **retribution or reward**.
Thus, **poverty and wealth, nobility and ignominy, longevity and early death** are not granted or withheld by decree, but arise entirely from **one’s own karmic summoning and response**.

These bureaus and gates **acknowledge the Jade Emperor of the Boundless Heaven as their sovereign**.
Yet the **High Supreme Sovereign of the Jade Pure Palace**, now commissioned by the Jade Emperor as the **Human Sovereign**, oversees the **Jade Pure Bureau of the High Supreme Sovereign**.
Moreover, he governs **all earthly mountain and ghostly spirits**, differing from the **edicts of the Great Emperor of the Northern Pole, the Purple Microstar**, and is not the **mixed primal virtue of the Supreme Emperor’s Three Heavens Exalted Teaching and Auxiliary Dao Master’s secret scriptures**.

Now, the **celestial officials of the High Supreme Sovereign’s Jade Pure Bureau** oversee the **seals of the earthly ghosts and spirits**, along with the **Spirit Officials and celestial attendants**, the **messengers and generals**, the **diverse-named Jade Officials**, and the **summoned spirit texts**.
This law must be practiced on the **third day of each lunar nine-day period**, when the **celestial officials of the High Supreme Sovereign’s Palace descend to the mortal assembly**. One must **abstain from meat, alcohol, and carnal desires**, observing strict fasting—**this must be observed with utmost care**.

**On the Scriptures**
The **Seven Stages of the High Supreme Sovereign’s Dao Scriptures** are now transmitted to the mortal world.

Since ancient times, it has never descended to manifest itself. Now those who obtain it shall **exalt their bodies and preserve their lives**, **cross calamities and extend their years**. Those who revere it shall receive blessings from the **celestial officials**, **dispel calamities and avert misfortune**. Those who practice it shall **repel and extinguish malevolent spirits**, **severely punish demons**. The **worthy and virtuous** must first **pledge allegiance to the Dao of the Spirit Palace**, **petition the High Supreme Sovereign**, and await the **divine response** before they may **revere and practice it**. They must not **transgress or recklessly employ** it. It is most fitting to **strictly adhere to its precepts**.

**On the Secret Keys**
The **Spirit Palace’s Dao Scriptures**, the **Jade Pure Bureau’s Secret Keys**, encompass **all matters without exception**, **all beings without fail**. If one **preserves oneself and upholds them faithfully**, then **sitting in stillness, all wonders manifest**; **standing, all spirits obey**. In **tranquility and motionless repose**, one **feels and attains communion**—this is unlike all other **Dao laws**, and no **seal scriptures** compare to it. If the **worthy and virtuous** encounter this **transmission across the eons**, with **fate and fortune** aligned, **boundless and eternal**, how can they not **strive with utmost sincerity** to **invoke the True One’s blessings**? If they **begin with diligence but falter at the end**, **speaking falsely while harboring deceit**, the **Spirit Officials and celestial attendants** within the **Dao laws** shall **record their merits and demerits without fail**. At that time, the **Three Officials** shall **severely judge** them with their **divine tablets**. They must not **reveal these to the unworthy**—is this not something to be **held in utmost reverence**? **Exhortation and warning** are given.

**On the Wondrous Intent**
The **Spirit Palace’s Secret Scriptures**, the **Jade Officials’ Wondrous Intent**, are **profound mysteries**, difficult to fathom. Though there are **secret scriptures** to be studied and practiced according to their **prescribed methods**, there are no **essential keys or core principles**—like garments **cut but never sewn**, how could they be worn? The **key** is the **sewing**. Now, the **eternal secret scriptures** are revealed to the **learned and true**. If one **persists with unwavering resolve**, **aligns their heart with the Dao**, **uses the scriptures to sever malevolence**, and **returns to the True Path**, the **celestial soldiers** shall **assist and follow**. Day by day, month by month, one may **ascend to the Spirit Palace’s realm**. When **merits are fulfilled and name is established**, they shall **rise to the House of Boundless Eons**. Now these are **laid out to the left**—how can one not **ponder deeply and follow them with conviction**?

**On the Dao Law**
The **Spirit Palace’s Dao Law** was **hidden within the Jade Hall**, never revealed to the mortal world. Now, in the **auspicious cycle of the Jia-Xin years**, when the **Dao Sovereign** assumes **human leadership**, the **mysteries of the Dao** are **unveiled in this era**, and the **spirit scriptures** are **bestowed upon the treasure seals**, regardless of rank, for **reverence and practice**. Though **investigated and expounded**, they **differ from all other Dao laws**, and no **seal scriptures** are alike. But if one **sincerely invokes** with **unfailing devotion**, **peacefully practices** while **awaiting divine response**, the **merits and rewards** shall be **equal to the deeds**. They must not **arbitrarily invoke guilt from ghosts and spirits**. If they **follow the precepts and treat accordingly**, they may **rely on their merits and virtues** to **redeem themselves**, so that **both the living and the dead** may **all benefit from their virtue**. How could this be called **a minor supplement**?

**Oath and Ritual Procedure**
For those who practice this **Dao law**, on the **third day of each lunar nine-day period**, when the **celestial officials of the Spirit Palace** descend to the world, they must **use three lamps**, **twelve sheets of yellow paper**, and **compose a petition** to be **sealed with the Jade Seal** and **enclosed**. The words shall be **offered to the High Supreme Sovereign**. After burning the words, they must **prepare incense, tea, alcohol, and fruits**, **offering them with utmost sincerity**, then **extinguish the lamps and collect the ashes**. If they **receive a divine response**, then they may **practice the law**. The **Heavenly Sovereign of the Primordial Beginning** declares: *"I save the Supreme Sovereign of the Ten Thousand Blessings, opening the **Nine Pure Eons of the Purple Sky** and the **Ninefold Mysteries of the Spirit Palace**. I entrust them to the **Heavenly Sovereign’s eldest son**, so that he may **unveil the heavenly winds**, **transmit and guide the world’s people**, and **point them toward the True Dao**. Those who obtain it shall **ascend to the Celestial Realm** themselves. The **Ninefold Radiance of the Primordial Qi** has **eighty-one repetitions**, which is the **cycle of the Great Sun**. The **Sovereign of the Great Sun’s Ninefold Radiance and the Mulberry Tree of the East** accumulates **qi into the Spirit Palace’s True Sovereign**. He also **leads the duties of the Southern Pole**, together with **Han the Official of the Furnace**, in **molding the Heavenly People**, all **attaining the Nine Heavens**. Thus, they obtain the **Spirit Palace’s Forbidden Seal Scriptures** and the **Heavenly Seal of the Spirit Palace**, and on the appointed day, they **ascend to the Spirit Palace**."*

The **"Scripture of the Jade Hall"** comprehensively records **treasures that lead to ascension**, containing **ten grades of methods**. If one encounters this **scripture**, they shall **register their name in the Eastern Jade Hall**, and on the appointed day, they shall **ascend to the True Realm**. This **scripture** is **guarded by ten thousand Golden Spirit Children** and **one thousand Heavenly Pure Consorts**, who **constantly protect it**. When **incense is burned and scriptures are scattered**, they **record merits and demerits**. If there is **any slight transgression**, even the **Seven Ancestors** shall **suffer the divine punishment of the Spirit Prison**. The **transmitters** shall **deliver it with a Golden Dragon and Jade Fish’s Forbidden Brocade Seal**, **pledging allegiance to the Ten Heavens**. If one **breaks the fast or recklessly reveals** it, both **master and disciple** shall **share the same guilt**, and the **Seven Ancestors** shall **enter the Northern Capital**, where **ten thousand laws** shall **not pardon them**. This is the **pledge and warning** for the **worthy**.

**The Heavenly People’s Fasting with Rice Gruel**
The **hundred grains and five flavors** enter the **spleen and stomach**. The **five viscera** are **calmed and at peace**, and the **corporeal demons** are **dispelled and annihilated**. The **Seven Ancestors** ascend to **Heaven**, and the **minor worthy** attain **ascension**. **Long life** is **achieved within the Nine Pure Eons**, and **enduring vision** is **communed with the Holy Wisdom**. **Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **High Supreme Spirit Palace’s Eastern Jade Ascension Sovereign** decrees: *"This law is taken from the **Eastern Jade Qi**. Again, the **qi is blown**, harmonizing the **hundred bones and nine orifices**, and **dispelling the Three Corpses and Nine Worms**."*

**The Heavenly People’s Hair-Combing Method**
The **mud pellet at the Jade Vertex** and the **precious essence of the Vermilion Chamber and Mysterious Palace**—the **Heavenly Sovereign’s divine countenance** is **eternally preserved**, and the **divine light of the Sage Forest** is **manifested**. The **right** is the **Hidden Moon**, and the **left** is the **Hidden Sun**. The **six directions are purified**, and the **hundred spirits are transformed**. **Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **High Supreme Spirit Palace’s Great Sovereign** decrees: *"This law is to be practiced **facing the direction of the Heavenly Qi**. One must **blow the qi** and then **combine the hair**. The **white strands become qi**, bringing **great auspiciousness and prosperity**."*

**The Heavenly People’s Washing and Adorning with Headgear**
The **Heavenly Pure Jade Crown** and the **Cloud Robes with Glow of the Morning Mist**—the **Tiger Skirt subdues demons**, and the **Golden Elixir is refined**. The **five turbidities** are **rapidly dispelled**, and the **eight scenes** are **radiant**. The **ministers receive their blessings**, and their **guilt is erased while their fortune is enhanced**. They **ascend with the Spirit Palace**, **equally attaining the True and Holy**. **Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Five Sovereigns of the High Supreme Spirit Palace** decree: *"This law is to be practiced **from the month of the Heavenly Pure Maiden downward**, with **Jade Boys standing in attendance**. One must **blow the Heavenly Qi** into the **water** before **washing and adorning**."*

**The Heavenly People’s Mouth and Hand Washing**
The **Heavenly Pure and Earthly Bright**, the **Sun and Moon radiant in the morning**—they **purify my five senses**, and the **light shines upon the Jade Pure**.

The **Qi** does not receive defilement; the **five viscera** flourish in splendor.
Guilt vanishes from the **Northern Capital**, calamity is extinguished in the **Nine True Regions**.
Evil and malevolence are subdued and hidden; fortune connects with the **Upper Pure**.
Today’s **refined bathing**—all receive blessings.
The body generates **feathered robes**, ascending into the **Imperial Court**.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Southern Pole Long-Life Great Emperor** decrees.

**The Ritual:**
Close your eyes, and visualize the **Immortal’s Five-Colored Cloud Robes**, the **Four Beasts—Lion, White Crane**—before you. Let the radiance of the **Sun and Moon** enter the water.
Knock the teeth **thirty-six times**, face east, and draw the **Qi**, blowing it into the water.
First, swallow one mouthful, then use it.

---

**The Heavenly People’s Entry and Exit Ritual**
Serve and assist the **Jade Pure**, donning the **Paramartic Tiger**.
Exit with the **Sun**, enter with the **Moon**, opening the **Eight Scenes of Clarity**.
The **Six Jia** follow the **Divine**, the **Six Ding** march in attendance.
You align with the **Heavenly and Earthly**, supporting the **Hook-and-Arrow** constellations.
The **Seven Stars** guard and protect; a hundred blessings ensure **Long Life**.
The **Five Thunder Armies** stand with the **Ranks of Pure Immortals**.
Knives, swords, water, and fire **depart from your form**.
If you violate this **Heavenly Decree**, the **Kui and Gang** will act.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Highest Jade Pure Exorcising-Demon Emperor** decrees.

**The Ritual:**
Early, draw in the **Sun’s Light**; late, draw in the **Moon’s Light**—one mouthful each—blowing it to the left and right.
Ward off **evil, calamities, and malevolent people**; sever **slanderous curses**.

---

**The Heavenly People’s Undressing Ritual**
Receiving the **Heavenly Emperor’s Command**, ascending to the **Nine Heavens**.
A hundred spirits take their positions, arrayed in attendance upon the **Immortal**.
**Soul and vital essence** harmonize and soften; the **five viscera** flourish in abundance.
A hundred limbs generate **vital fluids**; the **Seven Essences** fill with luminosity.
The **Fire Order** radiates brilliance, vanquishing ghosts and dispelling misfortune.
Above, you aspire to the **Spirit Palace**, the **Divine Storehouse of Eternal Truth**.
For **countless kalpas**, you roam in splendor, bold and boundless.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Highest Taiwei Heavenly Emperor** decrees.

**The Ritual:**
Knock the **Heavenly Bell** three times with the left hand, the **Heavenly Chime** three times with the right, and strike the **Law Drum** three times in the center.
Undress, visualizing the **Taiwei Void Sovereign’s Chamber**, then lie down.
This will make the body **vital and healthy**, free from illness, with auspicious responses.

---

**The Heavenly People’s Outer Exorcism Spell**
Heaven has **nine stars**, Earth has **nine palaces**.
I have **nine orifices**, ten thousand spirits follow.
The **Three Corpses** are subdued and extinguished; the **five viscera** flow freely.
The **Three Fields and Four Limbs** move and rest in the **Center**.
The **Eight Trigrams’ Dragons and Tigers** come to attend my body.
Demons, spirits, and a hundred evils **do not dare approach**.
The **True Officials** maintain solemnity; **evil dreams** do not intrude.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Highest Spirit Palace Exorcising-Demon King** decrees.

**The Ritual:**
Draw the **Long-Life Vital Qi** from the **Cao**, swallow it, and strike the **Law Drum** three times, then cast it outward at will.

---

**The Heavenly People’s Illness and Medicine Spell**
Respectfully summon the **Highest Spirit Palace’s Eastern Hua Five Spirits**, calling forth the **Heavenly Physician, the True God Bian Que**, and their **clerks—fifty each**.
When the **small talisman** is taken with medicine, the body **separates from illness**; the illness swiftly departs.
Riding the **Kui** and **Gang**, ascending to the **Nine Heavens**.
Counting through the **Nine Earths**, **lifespan and fortune** both flourish.
**Long Life and eternal vision**, never dying in sorrow.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Highest Spirit Palace Long-Life Emperor** decrees.

**The Ritual:**
Draw the **Cao** and take the **Spirit Palace Qi**, blowing it over the medicine before giving it to the person.
This will **remove illness and calamity**, dispel chronic ailments.
It will **extend life and increase years**, always in accordance with this.

---

**The Heavenly People’s Entry into Filth and Darkness Ritual**
Left: **Virtue of the Pure Spirit**; Right: **Command of the Heavenly True**.
Left: **Lady of the Earthly Officials**; Right: **Five Ding of Exorcising Filth**.
Order my **death register** to be erased, and my **name** recorded in the **Jade Registry**.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Highest Spirit Palace Thunder Department’s Exorcising-Evil King** decrees.

**The Ritual:**
When arriving at filth, first raise your left hand to support the **Sun and Moon**, visualizing the **Five Ding Officials**, knock the teeth **seven times**, draw the **Northern Qi**, blow it upon yourself, then enter the **dark and filthy place**.

---

**The Ten-Thousand-Word Exorcising-Demon Spell of Wisdom**
The **Spirit Palace’s Green Emperor** refines truth in the **Eastern Well**.
The **Dan Palace’s Primordial Immortal** guards and preserves in unity.
The **nine orifices** flow freely; the **Linglang** extinguishes the **Sun**.
The light penetrates the **Azure Depths**; the **Mystic Mystic** communicates across distances.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—invoking the **Mahasattva of the Sun and Moon Wind**, as the **Eastern Well Emperor** decrees.

**The Talisman:**
Used on a **Wuwu day**, grind **Dan** with **play pearl blood**, facing east while reciting the spell, written on **yellow paper**.
Chew **Gulu** daily, swallowing it with **Eastern Well water**.
After a hundred days, the mind opens.
Recite the **Ten-Thousand-Word Spell** daily; **Heaven-born wisdom** emerges.
The **divine mind** wanders not; **inner clarity** is revealed.

---

**The Cold Filth Talisman**
Decree to the **Azure Sky’s Purple Mist Primordial Awakening Spirit General**, aiding my **True Qi** to sever all inauspiciousness.
**Li’s Emperor** arrives, carrying out the decree to subdue.
**The Talisman:**
Sever and dispel **ten thousand filths and a thousand evils**, either worn or affixed.
If **evil, malevolence, or pests** are present, swallow it for immediate effect.
Take the **Qi from the Dipper** and inscribe it.
If **official disputes or slander** threaten, or if **malevolent people plot harm**, wearing it will grant immunity.

---

**The Transforming Spirit Spell**
Highest True Salvation, donning the **Star and Jade**.
Left: **Thunder**; Right: **Lightning**; riding the **Dragon and Tiger**, the **wicked are annihilated**, the **virtuous nurtured**.
Reverently offering to the **Jade Emperor**, the **form and spirit transform swiftly**.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Highest Spirit Palace Jade Pure King** decrees.

**The Ritual:**
After reciting the spell, cast the **seal**.
Visualize the **Jade Boys and Girls** on either side, their **inner and outer golden light** enveloping your body, transforming you into an **Immortal Official**.
First, swallow a mouthful of **Spirit Palace Qi**, blow it upon your body, then knock the teeth **seven times**, seal the **Spirit Palace Seal**, and silently draw the **Cao**.
For **driving dragons, subduing ghosts, or submitting petitions**, this method is used.

---

**The Divine Light Talisman**
**Heavenly Thunder of the Spirit Palace**, **Earthly Thunder of the Nine Fortifications**.
**Water Thunder of the Abyssal Caverns**, **Wind Thunder of the Eastern Tree**.
**Ghost Thunder of the Mountains and Valleys**, a hundred valleys facing the **Sun**.
The **Great One’s Edict** commands: **"Burn the Ghost Fire."**
The **Thunder** is swift across **Heaven and Earth**; a hundred evils have no deceit.
Descending into the **viscera**, it flows smoothly and harmoniously.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Great One’s Decree** commands.

**The Talisman:**
On a day when **thunder sounds**, face the **cardinal direction** while reciting the spell.
**Heavenly Thunder**: write in **yellow** on **green** paper;
**Earthly Thunder**: write in **white** on **red** paper;
**Water Thunder**: write in **black** on **white** paper;

**Wind Thunder**: write in **blue-green** on **black** paper;
**Ghost Thunder**: write in **white** on **black** paper.
**Absorbing qi**: nine breaths from **Heaven**, ten from **Earth**, five from **Water**, three from **Wind**, one from **Ghost**—swallow while facing the cardinal direction.

Swallow the talisman for one day, and a hundred evils will flee in terror, their cries like urgent thunder, all meridians harmonized and flowing.
For infantile convulsions or possession by flying corpses, deploy **black qi** and the child will be at ease.

**Talisman of the True Yin and Yang Qi of Heaven and Earth**
Heaven and Earth’s eight and nine, humanity and spirit’s six and seven.
Pure and turbid, gold clears and separates—
Enter my divine fields, the **Great Granary** receives blessings.
The **Cavern Palace** is pure and clear, foul vapors dare not touch.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Supreme Sovereign of the Celestial Clarity’s Edict** commands.

This talisman: on **Winter Solstice** and **Summer Solstice**, face **west** and swallow **Earth qi** eighteen times.
On **Summer Solstice**, face **east** and swallow **Heaven qi** nineteen times.
Recite the spell and exhale the talisman.
On **yang days**, write in **red**; on **yin days**, write in **black**.
Swallow it, and the limbs will be attuned, a hundred ailments repelled.

**Talisman of the Nine Qi of Solar and Lunar Eclipses**
The **Roaming Moon’s True Essence**, the **Great Yin’s waxing and waning**.
Cold departs, heat arrives—the **Great Sun’s** fullness and decline.
Within, the **Three Corpses** reside, a hundred **passes** arrayed.
One breath of true qi enters, and the corpse-worms scatter and perish.
**Swiftly, swiftly**—as the **Supreme Sovereign of the Celestial Splendor’s Edict** commands.

This talisman: on days of the **Sun’s fullness** and **Moon’s fullness**, use the tongue to exhale and emit.
Nine breaths of the **Sun**, ten breaths of the **Moon** form the talisman.
Wear it swallowed, banishing the **Three Corpses** and **Nine Worms**.
Exhaled qi dissolves poison, blown upon ghosts—ghosts vanish.

**Talisman of the Eastern March Wood Official (Muxia)**: write in **yellow** on **blue-green** paper;
**Talisman of the Southern Pole’s Han Sizhang**: write in **yellow** on **red** paper.

「**Talisman of the Western Ling Gold Mother (Jinmu)**: write in **yellow** on **white** paper;
**Talisman of the Northern Xuanjun**: write in **yellow** on **black** paper;
**Central Yellow Old Official’s Talisman (Huanglao)**: inscribed with the **Sacred Edict of the Dragon Chapter (Yuzhang Shenghao)** and the **Sacred Edict of the Dragon Chapter (Longzhang Tian Shu)**.

This script emerged from the era of **Red Brightness (Chiming)** and the **Great Void (Haojie)**, sealed and entrusted to the **Eight Celestial Children (Bazi)** to subdue the **Celestial Palace (Tian Gong)**.
Hidden in the **Divine Azure Heaven’s (Shenxiao Tian)** Hall of Ultimate Truth, **three ten thousand heavenly maidens (Yunü Tianxian)** perpetually guard the text.

Should calamities of **water** and **fire** arise, inscribe in **red**, and cast into the midst of the water and fire—it shall not harm the **august body (zhaoshēn)**.
Should one carry or swallow this talisman, then **a hundred evils (bāi xié)** shall flee, **all diseases (wàn bìng)** shall be dispelled, **water demons (shuǐguài)** shall retreat in form, and **fiendish dragons (yāolóng)** shall hide beneath.

If one seeks to **transcend and guide (chāodù)** the **Seven Ancestors of the Nine Void Realms (Jiǔxuān Qīzǔ)**—suffering, tormented, and destitute spirits—then, as prescribed, inscribe on **yellow paper with red ink**, and entrust to the **Three Officials (Sānguān)**, and they shall immediately be **transcended and transformed (chāohuà)**. Ascending to the **Celestial Hall (Tiāntáng)**, they shall receive **all pleasures (zhū kuàilè)**.

This script is not to be passed to the **common folk (xiàshì)**.
If there are those who practice and study, with **one-hearted devotion (yīxīn)** receiving it, they may attain **supplementation to the Heavenly Maidens (Tiānxiān)**.

**Heedless disclosure or negligence shall bring death into the Northern Court of Punishment (Běifēng)**.

**Of Old, the Great Primordial Transformation**
The Primordial One, with the **Vajra-Qi Ancestral Mother**, performed the **Great Cavern Yin-Yang Union**, blending winds and merging, condensing **eighty-one measures of pure yang qi**, and birthing the **First Son, the Celestial Constellation King**. Next, condensing **seventy-two measures of pure yang qi**, the **Second Son, the Jade Flower Lord**, was born. Next, condensing **sixty-three measures of true yang qi**, the **Third Son** emerged. Next, condensing **fifty-four measures of Vajra-yang qi**, the **Fourth Son** was born. Next, condensing **forty-five measures of flourishing yang qi**, the **Fifth Son** appeared. Next, condensing **thirty-six measures of luminous yang qi**, the **Sixth Son** was born. Next, condensing **twenty-seven measures of rosy yang qi**, the **Seventh Son** emerged. Finally, condensing **eighteen measures of treasure yang qi**, the **Eighth Son** was born.

All were born from the **Great Cavern Union**, the **Primordial Father and Mysterious Mother**, through **nine transformations of yin-yang**, merging into **one**. **Nine yangs as one qi**. Congealing mist into spirit, blending wind into ether, forming **one imperial infant**, giving rise to the **Nine Emperors**.

The **seven nines of the Dao**, ten thousand transformations.

All the **Highest Celestial Jade Emperors** are but different titles of the **Eight Kings**. Thus, the **Nine Yang Heavenly Truths** all emanate from the **Thirty-Nine Chapters of the Great Cavern**.

The **Union of Blended Winds** is the **Dao of the One Emperor**. How could one, knowing this Dao, ascend to heaven in broad daylight, while those who lose it forever sink into the abyss?

Reflect upon this: the **Jade Saints and Ten Thousand Emperors** attain **True Reality** only by never departing the **Great Cavern**. How much more so for mere insects and corpses, ignorant of the **True One**, yet claiming to become **perfected sovereigns of marvelous Dao**?

**The Nine Masters of Celestial Constellation**
In antiquity, when the **Celestial Constellation descended**, the **Three Masters** convened in the **Azure Constellation Heaven**. **Disasters** are under the authority of the **Highest Heavenly Jade Sovereign Emperor**.
**The Patriarchal Master**, the **Highest Celestial Constellation Jade Purity True King of Long Life and Life-Preservation**, oversees **clear weather and rain**.

**The True Master**, the **Nine-Heaven Beneficent Calculation Command-of-Life Auspicious-Generating Khan Lord-in-Law True Sovereign of Life-Preservation**, governs **soul transmission and ether capture**.

**The Six Outer Masters** each hold their own orthodox laws, governing as follows:
**The Spirit Master**, the **Responding Primordial Recorded True Sovereign of Command**, wields the **Thunder Decree Tablet**, commanding **thunderous harmonies**.
**The Mysterious Master**, the **Life-Preserving Transformation-Generating True Sovereign of Life-Preservation**, oversees **the Five Peaks, rivers, lakes, Huai Sea, and cavern dragons**.
**The Saintly Master**, the **Commanding and Supervising True Sovereign of Ten-Thousand Security**, governs **soul capture, transmigration, exorcism of malevolent spirits, and suppression of demons**.
**The Treasure Master**, the **Primordial Life-Preserving True Sovereign of Auspicious Reserve**, administers **celestial laws of the Nine Exaltations**, overseeing **thirty-six kinds of untimely deaths**.
**The Heavenly Master**, the **Law-Master Recorded True Sovereign of Agriculture**, wields the **Thirty-Six Celestial Constellation Vajra-Qi True Talismans**, specializing in **Dao cultivation and official ascension**.

There is also the **Thunder Enclosure Divine Master**, the **Decree-Descending True Sovereign of Auspicious Gathering**, who governs **demons of the world, mountain-valley five calamities, and the five unrighteous gods**.

When the **Saintly Master** encounters **fasting and exorcism rites**, he should be invoked as the **Life-Preserving Transformation-Salvation Sovereign**.

Each of the **Nine Masters** has their own **inner principles**. If an official seeks the **Celestial Constellation lineage**, he must first prioritize **five-viscera essence-qi-spirit talismans**. Once inner essence is exhausted, how can one restore the original **divine qi** without relying on the **Primordial Vajra-Qi** to supplement what is lacking?

One must first **nurture internally**—only then will the **Celestial Constellation Dao** manifest as **ten thousand spirits**. Our **Celestial Constellation** is the **great essence of the exalted heavens**; it does not wander as the **Primordial Spirit**.

The **Highest Celestial Kings descend true talismans**.

**Morning Ritual Procedures**
Each time one practices, upon encountering the Ninth Days or Days of Descent, burn incense and, facing the northwest, bow nine times to the Three Pure Ones of Supreme Holiness, the Ten Extremes of High Perfection, the Celestial Sovereign of the Vault of Heaven, and the Daoist Patriarch Emperor, Lord of the Teaching.

Next, facing due south, bow nine times to the Ancestral Master, the Emperor of the Southern Extremity of Eternal Life, the Celestial Lord Who Preserves Life, and the True Master, the Beneficent Lord of the Nine Heavens, Master Han the Elder.

Next, facing due east, bow nine times to the Patriarchal Master, the Emperor of the Northern Extremity of Verdant Clarity, the Celestial Lord Who Saves Suffering from the Great Void.

Next, facing southeast, bow nine times to the Highest Celestial True Sovereign and all the True Saints and Immortal Officials within the Divine Treasury.

Offer three incense sticks, kneel facing east, and recite:
*"I am of the rank [state one’s Daoist position], surname [state surname]. With deepest reverence, I prostrate and kneel, bowing twice. I humbly report to the True Saints of the Highest Celestial Palace:*
*Today, I sincerely follow the practice of the Celestial Constellation’s Great Method, devoting my heart to pray that all my countless ancestral spirits may swiftly ascend to the celestial realms. May my own body be secure, my blessings and longevity extended. May I attain Dao and become an immortal, paying homage to the Celestial Constellation and soaring through the Golden Gates.*
*Thus spoken. Nine bows in retreat.*

If aged, infirm, or weak and unable to bow physically, a mental bow suffices."

**Adopting the Black Practice of the Celestial Constellation**
Each morning at sunrise, face southeast while studying. Mentally bow thirty-six times, strike the teeth thirty-six times, and gather true *qi* to form the Celestial Constellation Emperor. Visualize the thirty-six heavens’ golden light and jade platform’s verdant *qi*. Within its radiance, behold the Celestial Constellation True Sovereign, with the sun to the left and moon to the right. As the True Sovereign exhales verdant *qi*, inhale eighty-eight times (sixty-four breaths), distributing them to the Upper Dan Field, forming a solar wheel. Then inhale thirty-six breaths into the Middle Dan Field, forming a green pearl as if an emperor dwells within water.

When complete, bow seven times and recite the incantation:
*"Emperor of Verdant Clarity, True Sovereign of the Celestial Constellation, the Sun Emperor of the Eastern Red Pine, the Moon Sovereign of the Western Extremity—Four Truths, Three *Qi*—bind the verdant luminous light. Settle the Three Fields, internally harboring the True Emperor. Swallow the sun’s essence, ascending golden light. Internally circulate sun and moon, the alchemical hall’s jade chamber. Exhale to form a jade body, inhale the lustrous radiance. Demons and ghosts depart, the Three Corpses perish. Three nines make seven; face the Immortal King. Swiftly, as the decree of the Highest Celestial Constellation True Sovereign."*

This method, practiced for a hundred days, grants the way of *shixie* (corpse dissolution). This *qi* can subdue a thousand ghosts and a hundred demons, dispelling plagues and epidemics.

When traveling far or entering mountains, tigers and wolves retreat. Avoid blades, weapons, and plagues. Above, I confront the Celestial Constellation; golden light shines in all ten directions. Swiftly, as the decree of the Celestial Constellation Sovereign."*

**The Method:**
When practicing, draw a talisman on the ground to form an altar. Malevolent ghosts and demonic spirits cannot intrude, making it a blessed site. This is the realm of the thirty-six heavens; diligently cultivate merit to ascend to the Celestial Constellation’s sky. The talisman may be carried during fasting or placed in a quiet chamber. Spread upon the ground, it transforms into a golden palace with jade gates, divided into thirty-six portals, naturally generating golden hues and jade light that spirals about. It dispels evil; even if placed on the earth, ten thousand spirits dare not approach.

**The Thirty-Six Heavens of Highest Purity and True Life-Preservation**
The Highest Celestial Constellation comprises thirty-six heavens, each with thirty-six layers below, governed by the Thirty-Six Fortifications. Each possesses nine solar *qi* to correspond with the thirty-six *qi* of the year. Every ten days, one *qi* ascends, aligning with one heaven ruled by an emperor who governs that *qi*. The deeds of heavenly immortals, spirits, and ghosts are recorded by their respective heavens. The virtuous are inscribed in their heavenly registers; the wicked are imprisoned in their heavenly jails. The lowest are consigned to the Thirty-Six Fortifications, where the Sovereign reports to the Divine Treasury for investigation.

If one seeks to subdue ghosts and spirits, use the heavenly talisman to summon and notify the Sovereign and the heavenly and earthly deities, who shall promptly appear. Present them with the *Wheel of Heaven Diagram*; do not reveal it recklessly. Should ghosts or spirits bring calamity, or dragons and monsters cause disaster, or fire and water bring affliction, pinch the *heavenly eyes* (third eye), place the talisman below, and call in the direction:
*"Heavenly Emperor, swiftly arrive! Dispatch them at once."*

To summon, first fast for ninety days, liberating the souls of the deceased, and inform them below—they shall then ascend. This shall be inscribed in cinnabar on yellow paper and distributed with the appropriate *qi*.

**Method for the Thirty-Six Talismans:**
The thirty-six talismans are inscribed in *seal script* (篆) with *jade* (碧玉), encased in a *golden box* (黄金为函). They reside within the *Divine Treasury Palace* (神霄宫府), in the *crimson chambers* (朱房) and *jade rooms* (玉室), beneath the *Precious Forest Pavilion* (琼林紫石芝英宝阁), guarded by eight hundred *Highest Purity Jade Maidens* (太和玉女). These are the *primordial mystic texts* (太初玄古之文) of the *Supreme Sovereign* (皇天).

They emerge from *ten thousand kalpas* (万劫), revealing natural wondrous principles (妙理). The *Emperor’s Purple Script* (紫字) is the *Divine Treasury’s* decree (契贤之旨).

The *Supreme Sovereign of the Eastern Celestial Palace* (东华上相青童仙君) seals the *Dao/Way* within these thirty-six heavens and the *Nine Celestial Mansions* (九霄宫), circulating eternally through ten thousand kalpas without decay, and remaining fresh through countless ages (亿载). Those who encounter them bear the *ancient mystic name* (宿挺玄名).

They can avert the *threefold demonic calamities* (三对之魔) and avoid the *fivefold sufferings* (五苦之劫). They transcend the souls of the *Northern Peak* (北岳), issuing commands to the myriad deities (万神). They ascend to release the *seven ancestral souls* (七祖之魂) and descend to disperse the *Nine Yin grudges* (九阴之仇).

Without this talisman, one may only labor in vain over refining the *essence* (精), yet how could they attain self-liberation in the *Southern Celestial Abode* (南轩)? Those who attain this shall possess *refined spirit* (爽灵), and the *One Dao* (雌一) shall manifest its response.

With the *Thirty-Six Talismans*, one may naturally become an immortal (自仙矣), and all calamities and punishments (祸考) shall be extinguished.

They may be *received* (受), *worn* (佩), *swallowed* (吞), or *ingested* (服). The names of a hundred immortals (百仙书名) are inscribed, and the *Yin Capital* (阴都) shall erase its records (削字).

In a *pure chamber* (净室), facing east, perform nine prostrations (九拜), clap teeth thirty-six times (叩齿三十六通), swallow saliva seven times (咽液七遍), and recite the incantation:

*"Highest and Supreme Divine Treasury,
Greatly Holy and Pure Jade Maidens.
Spirit talismans liberate souls,
Preserve form and guard spirits.
Three refineries, nine transformations,
The six directions naturally respond.
Forever depart from the Northern *Yin Tribunal* (北酆),
Release all sufferings (万苦).
My body attains liberation,
Ascending to the Jade Treasury of immortals.
Inscribed on azure tablets,
Listed among the Highest Sovereigns.
With jade seals and cinnabar texts,
I ascend to Dao/Way and immortality.
The three luminaries align,
The nine emperors share the same hall.
Ascending in the purple chariot,
I am ranked among the Han Celestial.
Blessings flow to the seven ancestors,
All attain the highest immortality.
Swiftly, as the decree of the Highest and Supreme Divine Treasury King (神霄王)."*

Upon completing the incantation, inscribe it in cinnabar on yellow paper (朱书黄上), swallow the saliva twenty-four times (咽津二十四过), visualize the *five-colored clouds and mists* (五色云霞) ascending from your body, and let *flames of fire* (火光) envelop you. Swallow it with pure water (以净水吞之).

Practice this for three years, and the *Emperor-Immortal* (帝仙) shall descend. When nine years have passed and the merit is complete, you shall ascend to the *Divine Treasury Court* (神霄).

Then pinch the *Supreme Sovereign’s Dao/Way secret* (掐上帝诀), extract the *stellar qi* (辰气), inscribe and recite the *Universal Incantation* (都咒). Facing the *eastern-southern direction* (东南) with utmost sincerity (至诚祷祝), pray to the *associated celestial emperors and immortal assemblies* (所属天帝仙众), beseeching them to descend their *true qi* (真气) into your body.

This shall cure all illnesses (治万病). If confronted by malevolent spirits (凶邪), you may also inscribe and affix the talisman. It shall avert the calamities of *water and fire* (水火之灾).

The *Divine Treasury Palace* (神霄) of the *Highest and Supreme Jade-Purity King* (玉清王府) spans its domain (分域之境), known as the *Divine Treasury Heaven* (神霄天). Within it are the thirty-six heavens (三十六天), each presided over by a *Dragon Deity* (龙神), who summon thunder and bring forth benevolence to subdue violence (兴雷生善伐暴). None escape their jurisdiction (罔不由之).

The efficacy of these thirty-six talismans is profound and secret, forged by *accumulated jade and refined gold* (流金积玉成文). Their texts can penetrate the *underworld tribunal* (闻冥曹) and reach the *Three Heavens* (三天).

Swallow one talisman daily, and within a hundred days, your face shall radiate with *jade light* (玉光), your countenance with *golden mists* (金霞). After nine years of practice, the *cloud-borne palanquin* (云軿) shall descend upon you. One talisman corresponds to one *Heavenly Sovereign* (天主); three years suffice to ascend into the *Jade Treasury* (玉府).

**Method for the *Sun-Soul Talisman* (日魂符) and *Sun-Soul Incantation* (日魂咒):**
At noon, when the *Sun Deity* (日君) is summoned (司命天君), the nine emperors align (九帝齐景), and the three luminaries share the same palanquin (三光同軿). They ascend with me, soaring to the Three Heavens (高奔三天).
Swiftly, as the decree of the Divine Treasury Jade-Purity King (神霄玉清王律令).»

This talisman is inscribed by extracting *stellar qi* (辰气) with the *left hand’s two upper fingers* (左手二指上节), facing east-south at sunrise (日出), and visualizing *golden light at noon* (想日中金光), channeling it into the talisman.

Men who ingest it shall, within a hundred days, radiate *purple mists and crimson light* (紫霞红光); women who ingest it shall manifest *golden and jade forms* (金玉成形), bearing noble children (生贵子).

**Method for the *Moon-Soul Talisman* (月魄符) and *Moon-Soul Incantation* (月魄咒):**
At the moment of the moon’s fullness (月中方盈), when the *Moon Emperor* (月帝元君) is invoked, the eight *divine manifestations* (八景) are arrayed, and *precious light* (宝光) sustains the form. The body generates *jade essence* (玉液), purifying internally and externally (内灌外清).
Swiftly, as the decree of the Highest and Supreme Divine Treasury Jade-Purity King (神霄玉清王律令).»

This talisman is inscribed by extracting *qi* (气) with the *left hand’s five fingers pinching the Yin-stellum* (左手五指掐酉文), facing west-north at moonrise (月出), and visualizing *jade light within the moon* (想月中玉光), channeling it into the talisman.

Gather *thousand truths* (千真) to refine it, and let your body radiate with *jade light* (身有玉光).

**Additional Method:**
At sunrise or moonrise, close your eyes (闭目), clap teeth eighty-one times (叩齿八十一通). Facing east or west, inscribe in yellow and white paper (以黄白书), and cast into water (投水中). Draw *stellar qi* through your nostrils thirty-six times (鼻引气三十六口), retain the *qi*, swallow the talisman, and rinse with pure water (以净水盥漱), washing your ears and eyes. Thus, your face shall radiate with *gold and jade light* (兆面有金玉光), reversing aging and restoring youth (反老回童). This shall cure chronic illnesses (治夙病).

If women drink it, they shall bear noble children (生贵子). The *Divine Water* (神水) flows harmoniously, and the hundred *meridians* (脉) shall be tranquil (百脉安然). This practice ensures the *high ascent of the sun and moon* (日月高奔).

The **High Ascension of the Dao/Way: Secret Instructions of the Long-Living Jade Purity King of the Celestial Heights**

On the days of *Jiazi* (甲子) and *Gengshen* (庚申), inscribe it upon yellow silk (书之於黄罗上).
Wear it at your left flank (佩於左胁), and the myriad deities shall guard you.
Unless it is the morning of the Celestial Court’s audience (非朝帝), you must not wear it.
If ghosts and spirits do not submit (如鬼神不伏), with the *arrow script* (箓) fire, burn the talisman (化), clap teeth twelve times (叩齿十二通), face southeast (望东南), and invoke the True King (请真王).
When he arrives (立到), all demons shall be subdued (万魔克伏).

**The Stellar Dao/Way of the Nine Suns: The High Ascension of the Dao/Way’s First Sun**
*The talisman of the mixed* [cosmic] *origins* (一阳混□□瑝之炁) *of the Right*
On the day of the Winter Solstice (冬至之日), at midnight (夜半), face north (面北), and inscribe with black script upon dark paper (玄书苍上).
Clap teeth three times (叩齿三通), and recite the incantation:
*"The Dao/Way’s First Sun, descending from the Nine Heavens (神霄一阳，出自九天).
The mixed origins of the celestial chariot, faintly extending (混元轩舆，□瑝微延)."*
The talisman shall govern the left kidney (符镇左肾), ascending to the Jade Chariot (上升玉轩).
**Method:** With the left hand’s ring finger root (左手无名指根), draw *west-north qi* (西北炁), swallow it.
In nine years (九年), you shall bear the *Imperial Mushroom of the Jade Flower* (生皇芝玉英), ascending in broad daylight (白日飞升), and your spirit shall wander the Golden Gate (神游金阙).

**The Stellar Dao/Way of the Second Sun: The Dao/Way’s Overflowing Purple Microcosm**
*The talisman of the right* (二阳泛华紫微之炁)
On the day of the Spring Equinox (立春之日), at the Hour of Ox (丑时), face northeast (面东北), and inscribe with black script upon green paper (玄书青上).
Clap teeth five times (叩齿五通), and recite the incantation:
*"The Dao/Way’s Second Sun, descending from the Nine Heavens (神霄二阳，出自九天).
Overflowing brilliance of the Grand Primordial, faintly extending in the Purple Microcosm (泛华太素，紫微微延)."*
The talisman shall govern the right kidney (符镇右肾), ascending to the Jade Heaven (上升玉天).
**Method:** With the left hand’s middle finger root (左手箔中指), draw *east-north qi* (取东北炁), swallow it.
In nine years (九年), golden light shall descend upon your body (金光降身), commanding the myriad deities (役使万神), and the Purple Sovereign shall be born in the Imperial Mansion (紫皇生府注名), ranking among the Celestial Officials (位列仙公).

**The Stellar Dao/Way of the Third Sun: The Dao/Way’s Heavenly Hall and Phoenix Chariot**
*The talisman of the right* (三阳天娄凤车之炁)
On the day of the Spring Equinox (春分之日), at the Hour of Tiger (寅时), face east (面东), and inscribe with green script upon green paper (青书青上).
Clap teeth nine times (叩齿九通), and recite the incantation:
*"The Dao/Way’s Third Sun, descending from the Nine Heavens (神霄三阳，出自九天).
The Heavenly Hall of the Jade Pavilion, faintly extending in the Phoenix Chariot (天娄玉阁，凤车微延)."*
The talisman shall govern the *Gate of Life* (命门), ascending to the Nine Heavens (上升九天).
**Method:** With the left hand’s middle finger’s second joint (左手箔二指根), draw *east-north qi* (取东北炁), swallow it.
In seven years (七年), at night you shall see the *Phoenix Clouds and Jade Chariot* descending with edicts (夜有凤云玉车下诏), welcoming you into the Dao/Way’s High Ascension (迎入神霄).

**The Stellar Dao/Way of the Fourth Sun: The Dao/Way’s Midwife’s Light and Exorcism**
*The talisman of the right* (四阳中女辟邪之炁)
On the day of the Summer Equinox (立夏之日), at the Hour of Dragon (卯时), face the sun (面来), and inscribe with white script upon red paper (白书赤上).
Clap teeth seven times (叩齿七通), and recite the incantation:
*"The Dao/Way’s Fourth Sun, descending from the Nine Heavens (神霄四阳，出自九天).
The midwife’s light, faintly extending in exorcism (中女养光，辟邪微延)."*
The talisman shall govern the *Vermilion Palace* (绛宫), ascending to the *Cinnabar Heaven* (丹天).
**Method:** With the left hand’s middle finger’s second joint (左手箔二指中节), draw *east-south qi* (取东南炁), blow it in.
In three years (三年), your bodily ailments shall depart (身疾患去), and no demon shall dare approach you (万邪不干).

**The Stellar Dao/Way of the Fifth Sun: The Dao/Way’s Grand Primordial’s Faint Extension**
*The talisman of the right* (五阳太皇微延之炁)
On the day of the Summer Solstice (夏至日), at the Hour of Snake (辰时), face south (面南), and inscribe with red script upon red paper (赤书赤上).
Clap teeth fourteen times (叩齿十四通), and recite the incantation:
*"The Dao/Way’s Fifth Sun, descending from the Nine Heavens (神霄五阳，出自九天).
The Grand Primordial’s faint extension in the Jade Emperor (太皇玉帝，微微延延)."*
The talisman shall govern the *Spleen Palace* (脾宫), ascending to the *Primordial Beginning* (上升始玄).
**Method:** With the left hand’s ring finger, pinch the *Hour of Snake* script (掐二指辰文), draw *perverse qi* (巽炁), and swallow it.
In five years (五年), the Yellow Emperor shall record your name (黄帝书名), and no hundred diseases shall harm you (百病不伤).
If taken on the first day of the fifth month (以五月一日服之), it shall subdue serpents, centipedes, and scorpions (制伏蛇虫蜈蚣).
Tigers, wolves, and fierce beasts shall not dare harm you (虎狼猛兽，不敢伤人).
Throughout the year (并一年之中), no hundred demons shall intrude (百怪不侵), and your body shall radiate with jade light (身有玉光).

In seven years (七年), your blood shall be invigorated and your essence replenished (活血补精), your white hair shall depart (去白发), and your youthful visage shall not age (变童颜不老).
Your body shall be light and luminous (轻身体，有光明), and no demon shall dare approach you (万邪不敢近也).

At night you shall have myriad divine lights (夜有神光万道), and no hundred ghosts or demons shall dare approach you (百鬼万邪，不敢近也).

**The Stellar Dao/Way of the Eighth Sun: The Dao/Way’s Heavenly Truth and the Edict of Immortality**

**The Stellar Dao/Way of the Ninth Sun: The Dao/Way’s Grand Primordial’s Silent Primordial**
*The talisman of the right* (九阳太皇寂玄之炁)

*"The Dao/Way’s Ninth Sun, the sun’s nine *qi* (神霄九阳，太阳九炁).
Eighty to obtain one, the Grand Primordial’s Jade Chamber (八十得一，太皇玉室).
Silent entry into the Primordial Void, ascending to the Jade Chamber of the Celestial Court (寂入无元，上朝玉室)."*
**Method:** With the left hand’s five fingers’ nails (左手拾五指甲下), draw the sun’s *qi* eighty-one times (取太阳炁八十一口), inscribe the seal script with your tongue (舌书篆文), and swallow it.
In nine years (九年), your body shall dissolve and transform (身形解化), ascending to the Jade Emperor of the Celestial Court (上朝玉帝).

**The Secret Instructions of the Jade Purity King of the Celestial Heights, Preserved in the True Transformation Diagram**
The *brain talisman* (书脑符咒) is inscribed within the *arrow script* (箓).

The *brain talisman* (脑君泥丸赤文), the *Mixed Void Lord* with whispered incantations (混洞君嘘嘘摄).
All *solar qi* shall gather (众阳宗集), and the hundred *marvels* shall be illuminated (百会图明).
Ascend to the unity of the entire body’s *primordial* (上全一体之元), descend to the five *palaces* of the senses (下闰五官之府).
*The talisman of the right*, inscribed with white script upon red paper (白地赤书), pinch the *Hour of Snake* script (掐辰文), and draw the *qi* from above (取上方炁).
Store the spirit within its *palace*, and release the *primordial light* to envelop your body (存神在其官，放元光罩身).
This talisman nourishes the brain (此符补脑), and you shall have no headaches (不头疼).
In a hundred days (百日), all deities shall bow in reverence (诸神朝拱).

**Kidney Talisman (肾符咒):**
*The Spirit of the Kidney* (肾神大渊), whose name is *Lord of the Seeking* (君字求都).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity* (玉清敕), *"Swiftly descend the Primordial *qi* and complete it"* (速降元炁成).
**Activating the Talisman:**
*The Lord of the Kidney* (肾君), *Spirit of the Kidney* (肾神大渊), whose name is *Lord of the Seeking* (君字求都摄).
It is the master of the body (为身之主), and the root of all life (总命之元).
It dwells in the *Water Palace* (居水府), and remains pure and clear (以洁清).
Ascend to the *Separate Palace* (升离官), and achieve completion (而既济).
**Right Talisman:** Inscribed in *qi*-script upon white paper (白地炁书), with the left hand pinching the root of the middle finger (左手掐中指根), drawing the *qi* from the north (取北炁), and storing the *mysterious* *qi* to fill the room (存玄炁满室).
It strengthens the essence and vitality (益精壮元), and the *yang* shall not falter (阳不倦). Deep roots and firm foundations (深根固蒂), it generates the *flowering* *qi* (生华萼).

**Yin Talisman (阴符咒):**
*The Spirit of the Yin* (阴神续命), whose name is *Lord of the First Strong* (君字伯强).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity* (玉清敕), *"Swiftly descend the Primordial *qi* and complete it"* (速降元炁成).
**Activating the Talisman:**
*The Lord of the Yin* (阴君), *Spirit of the Yin* (阴神续命), whose name is *Lord of the First Strong* (君字伯强摄).
It is the secret chamber of the spirit (精神之秘府), and the origin of life and vitality (性命之本源).
The cause of eternal life and purity (长生清净之缘), it blocks all thoughts of licentiousness (杜绝邪淫之念).
**Right Talisman:** Inscribed in *qi*-script upon red paper (炁地朱书), with the left hand pinching the root of the middle finger (左手掐中指根), then drawing upward to the central joint (引上掐中节), gathering the *qi* from the northwest (取西北炁), and writing it thus. Store the spirit within the *three-colored clouds* (存神三色云中).
Ingest it thus, and it shall cause the five *palaces* to generate the *flowering* *qi* (五脏生华萼), and vitalize the blood to grow flesh (活血生肉).

**Uterus Talisman (胞符咒):**
*The Spirit of the Uterus* (胞神元常), whose name is *Lord of Autumnal Husband* (君字秋夫).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity* (玉清敕), *"Swiftly descend the Primordial *qi* and complete it"* (速降元炁成).
**Activating the Talisman:**
*The Lord of the Uterus* (胞君), *Spirit of the Uterus* (胞神元常), whose name is *Lord of Autumnal Husband* (君字秋夫摄).
It is the origin of birth (生身之本), and the beginning of transformation (化形之初).
It conceals the *Primordial* *qi* (藏元炁), and makes it the spirit (以为神).
It protects the *Palace of Life* (翼命宫), and gathers in rectitude (而集正).
**Right Talisman:** Inscribed in red script upon white paper (白地朱书), with the left hand pinching the middle finger’s central joint (拾中指中节), drawing the *qi* from the southeast (取东南炁), and taken in three swallows (当三呼，服之).
Store the spirit within the *three-colored clouds* *qi* (存神，存三色云炁之中), and blend harmoniously with all spirits, who shall dwell within your body (混合百神皆在其身).

**Fetus Talisman (胎符咒):**
*The Lord of the Fetus* (胎君), *Spirit of the Fetus* (胎神含生), whose name is *Lord of the Auspicious Harmony* (君字寅和).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity* (玉清敕), *"Swiftly descend the Primordial *qi* and complete it"* (速降元炁成).
**Activating the Talisman:**
*The Lord of the Fetus* (胎君), *Spirit of the Fetus* (胎神含生), whose name is *Lord of the Auspicious Harmony* (君字寅和摄).
It is borne by the heavens and earth (天地所载), and the *yin* and *yang* align in harmony (阴阳顺宜).
It bestows life and vitality (赋唱), and manifests to the myriad spirits (演於万神).
It cradles the nascent life (怀生), and achieves completion in due order (成而有序).
**Right Talisman:** Inscribed in white script upon yellow paper (黄地白书), with the left hand pinching the *Hour of Tiger* script (掐辰文), drawing the *qi* of the *Primordial Spirit* (取元神之炁), and facing the five directions (向五方之炁), ingesting it thus. Store the spirit within the *three-colored clouds* *qi* (存神三色云炁之中).
Ingest it over time, and you shall transcend the mortal to attain the sacred (久而服之，能超凡入圣).

**Sealing Talisman (结符咒):**
*The Spirit of the Seal* (结神九华), whose name is *Lord of the Auspicious Flight* (君字彦遐).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity* (玉清敕), *"Swiftly descend the Primordial *qi* and complete it"* (速降元炁成).
**Activating the Talisman:** *The Lord of the Seal* (结神)...」

**Sealing the Lord and Spirit of Nine Flowers (九华):**
The Lord of the Seal, *Yánhuá* (彦遐), binds the spirit.
Coiling and winding, curving and encircling—
It sinks filth and turbidity, lightening the body.
It clarifies purity and fragrance, nourishing the flesh.

**Right Talisman:** On red ground with *qi*-script (炁书), the left hand pinches the *Hour of Tiger* script, drawing the *Primordial Spirit qi* from three breaths (三口), facing northeast, and inscribing it.
Ingesting it shall extinguish thought and gather the spirit.

**Sealing the Aroma-Spirit Talisman (节神香皓):**
The Lord of the Seal, *Kōngyóu* (空猷), whose name is *Aroma-Spirit*.
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity*, *"Swiftly descend the Primordial qi and complete it."*
**Activating the Talisman:**
The Lord of the Seal, *Kōngyóu*, binds the spirit.
He governs muscles and bones, harmonizing sinews and framework.
In accordance with the shifting of seasons, he opens the *Primordial Essence* (元精).
**Right Talisman:** On yellow ground with white script, pinch the left middle finger’s root, drawing upward to the middle joint, taking *qi* from the northwest, and inscribe it.
Long-term ingestion shall vitalize the blood and bloom the complexion.
At the time, store the spirit and emit a vast luminous canopy around the body.

**Sealing the Blood Talisman (血符咒):**
The Blood-Spirit of *Zhōngyōu* (中幽), whose name is *Liángbì* (良弼).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity*, *"Swiftly descend the Primordial qi and complete it."*
**Activating the Talisman:**
The Blood-Lord and Blood-Spirit of *Zhōngyōu*, *Liángbì* binds the spirit.
It circulates as one body, spreading freely through the four limbs.
It possesses the function of movement, cutting off stagnant ailments.
**Right Talisman:** On blue ground with red script, the left hand pinches the middle finger’s root, drawing upward to the middle joint, facing the *Kingly Direction* (王方) with three invocations.
Ingesting it shall ensure the hundred vessels’ *qi* and blood flow without obstruction—success in a hundred days, with immediate efficacy.

**Sealing the Essence Talisman (精符咒):**
The Spirit of *Yuánchú* (元除), whose name is *Zhùzhù* (祝祝).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity*, *"Swiftly descend the Primordial qi and complete it."*
**Activating the Talisman:**
The Essence-Lord and Spirit of *Yuánchú*, *Zhùzhù* binds the spirit.
The great form borrows its foundation; the Primordial *qi* supports it.
It shall achieve the function of supplementing the brain, eternally aiding the marvel of nourishing the spirit.
**Right Talisman:** On blue ground with red script, the left hand forms the *zi* script (子文), taking *qi* from true north, storing the *Mysterious qi* (玄炁), with three invocations.
Ingesting it shall, in a hundred days, complete its function—supplementing deficiencies, enriching marrow and brain.

**Sealing the *Qi* Talisman (炁符咒):**
The *Qi*-Spirit of *Wúyáng* (无央), whose name is *Yìjiā* (义嘉).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity*, *"Swiftly descend the Primordial qi and complete it."*
**Activating the Talisman:**
The *Qi*-Lord and *Qi*-Spirit of *Wúyáng*, *Yìyì* (义义) binds the spirit.
Dispersing as firm and upright, it generates the vast and boundless.
Filling the four limbs, it brings peace and honor.
Filling the hundred bones, it aligns with ease.

**Right Talisman:** On yellow ground with white script, the left hand pinches the middle joint of the middle finger, drawing downward from the upper joint, taking *Chén qi* (辰炁), with three invocations toward the northwest. Ingesting it for a hundred days shall invigorate the spirit and replenish *qi*, rendering it inexhaustible.

**God-Symbol Talisman (神符咒):**
The God-Spirit born of Heaven, *Língfù* (灵父).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity*, *"Swiftly descend the Primordial *qi* and complete it."*

**Activating the Talisman:**
The God-Lord and God-Spirit born of Heaven, *Língfù* binds the spirit.
With *qi* as form and essence as substance,
Manifesting the virtue of the numinous, to dwell in tranquility.
Illuminating the body with radiance, revealing itself naturally.

**Right Talisman:** On blue ground with red script, the left hand pinches the middle finger, taking *Xùn qi* (巽炁).
Ingesting it for a hundred days shall complete its function—clarifying the spirit, refreshing *qi*, harmonizing essence and vitality, with no discontent remaining.

**Life-Symbol Talisman (命符咒):**
The Life-Spirit of *Zhèngzhōng* (正中), *Chángshēng* (长生).
I follow the *Edict of Jade Purity*, *"Swiftly descend the Primordial *qi* and complete it."*

**Activating the Talisman:**
The Life-Lord and Life-Spirit of *Zhèngzhōng*, *Chángshēng* binds the spirit.
Where there is life, there is form.
Where there is response, there is spirit.
Knowing the myriad transformations of form,
Revealing the utmost nobility of the human body.

**Right Talisman:** On white ground with blue script, the left hand pinches the upper joint of the middle finger, taking *Xùn qi*, with three invocations.
Ingesting it for a hundred days shall complete its function—achieving longevity, preserving life, transcending the mundane, and entering sainthood.

**The Above True Talismans:**
When sealing *qi* and nurturing the spirit, recite the incantation and inscribe the talisman.
Ingesting it for a hundred days shall illuminate the inner and outer self, radiating clarity throughout the body.
Preserving the vision of the hundred spirits merging, the Great Cavern shall open of its own accord, granting longevity as the hundred spirits descend upon the body.
Diligently practicing this, one may command the myriad spirits—where shall one not go?

**Explanation of the True Form of the Godly Sovereign (神霄真形图说):**
The True Form’s nine *qi* are the eighty-one true yangs of the *Purple Cloud Jade Light* (紫霞玉光) of the Great Sun, condensed into *Lánglié Jié Lín* (琅结璘) form.
The Nine-Heaven Secrets, held in awe by the Celestial Sovereign, are not revealed to mortals.
Only those who have seen the True Form of the Jade Emperor, the Host of Primordial Bones, and recorded it before the kalpa,
Shall inscribe it on white jade with golden script.
Wearing it into the mountains, wolves and tigers retreat.
Within a hundred *li*, nobility and wealth flourish, free from calamities of blades, war, fire, or water.
Avoiding misfortune and violent harm.

If peril arises, burn incense and pray sincerely—
The True King dispatches the Great God of Removing Calamities with ten thousand troops,
Jade Boys and Jade Girls, guarding against all misfortune.
Wearing it for a hundred days, mountain and river immortals, the Six Heavenly spirits and earthly deities,
Shall escort one at the hour of *Zǐ* (子).
In nine years, one ascends in broad daylight.
Ever preserving the True King in the Celestial Court,
Foreknowing the future.
Daily worshipping, visualizing the True Form.
Ingesting it for a hundred days shall harmonize with Heaven’s will,
Entrusting one to the Dao of natural longevity.
Preserving it ensures immortality; ingesting it prevents illness.
Leaking it to others invites calamity—all spirits detest it.
*Zǐsī* kept this secret.

**Department of the Great Cavern General under the Jade Purity King:**
- *Qīyī* General: ten thousand troops.
- *Qīyī* Boy Officer: ten thousand.
- *Xióngyī* General: ten thousand troops.
- *Xióngyī* Boy Officer: ten thousand.
- Great Cavern General: ten thousand troops.
- Great Cavern Boy Officer: ten thousand.

**The Method:**
Each is inscribed with *Chén* script, taking *Xùn qi*, and the talisman is written to summon them.
The *Qīyī* General bears a jade case,
The *Qīyī* Boy Officer presents the incense burner,
The *Xióngyī* General wields an axe,
The *Xióngyī* Boy Officer plays the jade flute,
The Great Cavern General wields an axe,
The Great Cavern Boy Officer carries the *fánhuā* banner and flags.
All wear five-colored robes, riding five-colored clouds.
These generals are of supreme power—
Do not summon them lightly, nor invoke them carelessly.
Each follows the *Yīn-Yáng* principle of unity.
Recite the *Thirty-Seven Chapters of the Great Cavern True Scripture*,
First using the talismans of the Great Cavern *Yīn-Yáng* Boy Officers and Generals for the Six Paths.
Each time the Great Cavern talisman and the Thirty-Seven Chapters are ingested,
Burn the summoning talisman to have them attend to the body.

**Additional Officers:**
- Yellow Chamber General: ten thousand troops.
- Yellow Chamber Boy Officer: ten thousand.

- White *Xiá* Boy Officer: ten thousand.

- Hidden Path Boy Officer: ten thousand.
- True Taboo General: ten thousand troops.
- True Taboo Soldiers: ten thousand.
- Left Upper General: ten thousand troops.
- Left Upper Soldiers: ten thousand.

The **Right Talisman**—all of them clad in gold armor, with multicolored weapons—each accompanied by **one hundred twenty attendants**, all riding upon **verdant, variegated clouds**. When summoned, they may be dispatched toward the **Xùn direction**, invoking the **Xùn qi** and pressing the **Chén characters**.

**Right Upper General**: ten thousand troops.
**Right Upper Soldiers**: ten thousand.

The **second Right Talisman**, pressing the **Chén characters** and invoking the **Xùn qi**, burned to summon them:
One as a **General**, bearing a banner, with **one hundred twenty attendants**.
One as a **soldier**, wielding a bow, with **one hundred twenty attendants**.

**Front Division Tiger General**: ten thousand troops.
**Rear Division Tiger General**: ten thousand troops.

The **second pair of Right Talismans**, pressing the **Chén characters** and invoking the **Xùn qi**, inscribed and summoned:
The **Generals**, all resembling generals in form, each wielding a sword, with **one hundred twenty attendants** each.

**Dragon Cavalry General**: ten thousand troops.
**Phoenix Chariot General**: ten thousand troops.

The **second pair of Right Talismans**, pressing the **Chén characters** and invoking the **Xùn qi**, inscribed and summoned:
The **Dragon Cavalry General**—
His appearance like a **gold-armored warrior**, commanding **one hundred thousand gold-armored soldiers**, riding upon **Dragon-Phoenix chariots**.
The **General** bears **variegated banners**, commanding **ten thousand** who ride upon **Phoenix chariots**.
**Drum-and-Flute Division Officers**: ten thousand.
**Bell-and-Gong Division Soldiers**: ten thousand.

The **second pair of Right Talismans**, pressing the **Chén characters** and invoking the **Xùn qi**, inscribed and summoned:

For those who wish to practice the **Great Cavern Thirty-Seven Chapters Mixed Hundred Deities Talisman Method**, first inscribe the **Yin-Yang Great Cavern Boy Officers and Generals Six Talismans**, burning them to summon them. One must then **purify the mind**, arrange the **Three Officials**, align the form, and harmonize the **ten thousand qi**.

All facing east, strike the teeth **thirty-nine times**.

The **Incantation** reads:

*"O Jade Talisman of Sacred Sound, abide in eternal command over life.
The Three Caverns’ Precious Truth, rooted in the Jade Flower.
The Three Officials overflowing, ascending to fill the **Níwán** [1].
Thirty-nine nodes, **qi** bound and transformed to birth.
Change and transformation manifesting Truth, ascending to the **Imperial Dawn** [2].
Liberated by the Seven Ancestors, reborn in the **Southern Hall** [3].
Soaring in the **Great Cavern** [4], receiving **liberation** [5] with joy.
As swift as the **High Above Sacred Cavern Jade Purity King’s** decree.
Swallow the saliva **thirty-nine times**, then write the talisman with pen.
The **Mixed Hundred Deities Talisman**—Right Talisman:
Yellow ground, purple script, inner stars marked in black script.
Sit upon the talisman, then recite the preceding incantation and **purify** [6] it with the **Thirty-Nine Chapters Talisman**.

**High Above Sacred Cavern Jade Purity True King’s Purple Script Great Law Volume the Second** ends.
**High Above Sacred Cavern Jade Purity True King’s Purple Script Great Law Volume the Third**—**Great Cavern Subtle Mysteries**:

*"By decree: The **Great Cavern True Mysteries Cavern Chapter Flying Void Secret Talisman**,
must be inscribed on this day, the **Pure Dawn**,
with **cinnabar script** on **blue paper**,
and **purified** with clear water—then the **mind and spirit** shall be at ease.
Every **sixty-year cycle (jiǎzǐ)**, **Gēngshēn** [7], **natal day**, **Eight Nodes**, or **auspicious day**,
follow the above method to inscribe and **purify** it.
For mortals with **defiled qi**,
**purify** it for **one hundred days**—the **Long-Life Divine Spirits** shall descend upon your **embodiment** [8].
Use this to treat illnesses—none shall fail to respond.
**Incantation**:
'O Jade Talisman’s decree, the **Great Cavern** self-illuminates.
White Clouds spread across the heavens, the **Great Cavern Generals**.
Bound to the talisman’s dispersal, sickness flees with the **qi** at peace.
Long-Life Immortals, their **divine spirits** descend upon the body.
As swift as the **High Above Jade Purity Great Harmony King’s** decree.'

**Right Method**—Again, take the **Heavenly Gate Qi-Blowing Talisman**,
with the **Great Cavern Yin-Yang Yellow Chamber White Cloud Generals** and **Boy Officers**,
each **ten thousand** to guard it.
Do not reveal it recklessly—**secrecy and prohibition** are most grave.
Examine the **transgressions of the disciples** [9].
