**Method of Transformation, Mixing, and Divine Spirits’ Wondrous Generalship**:

*"For those who wish to **ascend to the Primordial** and enter **tranquility**,
walk the **Flying Void Pole** [10],
face north,
with a **pure cloth** held in one hand,
and offerings of **rice wine and food** in one portion,
strike the teeth **nine times**.
The **Five Zang** and **Hundred Passages** [11],
emit **White Qi**—**dense and lingering**.
After some time, the **qi** transforms and manifests as:
**One General of Yin** and **ten thousand Boy Officers**.

Again, retain the **Five Zang** and **Hundred Passages**,
emit **Yellow Qi**—**dense and lingering**.
After some time, the **qi** transforms and manifests as:
**One General of Yang** and **ten thousand Boy Officers**.

Again, retain the **Five Zang** and **Six Fu** [12],
as well as the **Three Dantian** [13],
with **Golden Chamber Jade Portal**,
emit **Purple Qi**—transforming into the **Great Cavern Generals**, **ten thousand**.
Again, retain the **Níwán Yellow Chamber**,
descend to the **Lower Element Yellow Court** [14],
emit **Yellow Qi**—transforming into the **Yellow Chamber Boy Officers**, **ten thousand**.

Again, retain the **nose** and emit **White Qi**—forming the **White Cloud General**.
Again, retain the **ears** and hear the **Boy Officers’ speech**,
with **drums and gongs** resounding, their voice shaking heaven and earth.
After some time, they enter the **Níwán**.
The **Golden Palace**,
sees **ten thousand troops**—transformed into a **precious pearl**,
its light like the **sun and moon**.
You then swallow it with your mouth,
entering the **Lower Dantian**,
transforming into a **small child**,
as though newly born, seeing the **Three Corpses Five Desires’ spirits**,
emerging from the **Jade Phallus**.
Inhale the **qi** with one breath,
and absorb it into the **heart** [15].
After some time, a **great light** appears in the heart,
exiting through the mouth—
transforming into the **Hidden Dao General**, **ten thousand**,
who draw bows and wield swords,
beheading the **Three Corpses** and their heads falling—
transforming into the **True Name Boy Officers**.
Close your eyes—the **crown** emits **White Qi**,
along with the **Generals and soldiers**.
Again, your **form** transforms into your own likeness,
riding upon **White Clouds**.
With your mouth, call upon the **left and right officers and soldiers**,
ascending to the **Jade Palace**,
and bowing in homage to the **Jade Emperor** [16].
The **various Generals** then transform into **Golden Light**,
swallowed in an instant—
only then does this method take effect.
If you wish to **summon spirits and laborers**,
first inscribe the **Summoning Truth and Inviting Spirits Talisman**,
as well as the **Calling upon the Functional Officials and Commanding Officers**,
and the **assembled soldiers and laborers**—this is most wondrous.

---
**Grasp the Key Principles**:
The **Tàiwéi Pole** [17]."

---
[1] **Níwán (泥丸)**: The upper dantian, a vital energy center in Daoist cosmology.
[2] **Imperial Dawn (帝晨)**: Likely refers to the **Dawn of the Jade Emperor (玉皇)** or the celestial realm.
[3] **Southern Hall (南轩)**: A Daoist term for the **Lower Dantian (下丹田)**, the energy center below the navel.
[4] **Great Cavern (太玄)**: A celestial or immortal domain, often associated with the **Highest Daoist Realms**.
[5] **Liberation (度)**: Here, a Daoist term for **transcendence or spiritual attainment**.
[6] **Purify (服)**: In this context, refers to **reciting and activating the talisman**.
[7] **Gēngshēn (庚申)**: A specific day in the **sixty-year cycle (甲子)**, often considered auspicious in Daoist practice.
[8] **Embodiment (兆身)**: The physical or spiritual form inhabited by the divine.
[9] **Disciples (察子)**: Likely refers to **students or practitioners** of the Daoist method.
[10] **Flying Void Pole (飞空罡)**: A Daoist **pole-star or energy pathway** for ascension.
[11] **Five Zang and Hundred Passages (五脏百关)**: The **Five Zang organs (心、肝、脾、肺、肾)** and their associated **meridians or energy passages**.
[12] **Six Fu (六腑)**: The **Six Fu organs (胃、胆、小肠、大肠、膀胱、三焦)** in Traditional Chinese Medicine.
[13] **Three Dantian (三田中)**: The **Three Vital Energy Centers**—**Upper (上丹田)**, **Middle (中丹田)**, **Lower (下丹田)**.
[14] **Lower Element Yellow Court (下元黄庭)**: The **Lower Dantian (下丹田)** or **Lower Elixir Field**, associated with **Yang Qi** and **vitality**.
[15] **Heart (心)**: Here, refers to the **Middle Dantian (中丹田)** or the **spiritual heart**.
[16] **Jade Emperor (玉皇)**: The supreme **Daoist deity**, equivalent to the **Celestial Sovereign**.
[17] **Tàiwéi Pole (太微罡)**: A **Daoist pole-star or constellation**, often linked to **celestial navigation and ascension**.

**The Ascension of the Spirit and the Great Roundness of the Dao**

**The Pole-Star of the Dao’s Flight Through the Void**
The heavens round, the earth square—**the Great Cavern’s Five Qi** blend as one.
Sit in silence, gathering the spirit—**restrain the soul and vital essence**.
Hold firm the **Elixir Foundation**, swallow the saliva to harmonize the **qi**.
The **Five Spirits** merge—all ascend to the **Primordial Origin**.
No **evil** disturbs the **True One**; ten thousand ailments never take root.
**Seal the Essence** at the **Command Gate**—eternal life, boundless years.
**Everlasting vitality and keen vision** lie within the **Celestial Court**.

**The Supreme Sovereign of the One**
The **One Supreme Deity** dwells in the **Néihuán Palace**,
Spouting the radiance of sun and moon from his mouth.
**Tiānpéng** appears as an infant,
**Sìmìng** as oneself, in **crimson robes and golden crown**.
**Táokāng** as oneself, in **yellow robes**,
The **Néihuán Prince** in **green robes**, like a noble lord.
The **White Primordial Deity** in **white robes**, like a noble lord.

If the **heart is restless**, fearing calamity’s approach,
Press the left hand to the chest and chant:
*"O **Central Sovereign of the Celestial Court, Master of Life**,
Extend my disciple’s years—bind me with golden cords,
That I may endure **thousands of autumns, tens of thousands of springs** without end."*
Recite seven times—**restlessness dissolves**.

**Incantation to Purge Illness**
*"O **One Supreme Deity**,
Return all schemes to their source.
Drive away the **hundred maddenings**, sweep away all **evil impurities**."*
Recite seven times—**if the *qi* is discordant, the Essence unnurtured**, it shall be cured.

**Nurturing the Essence-Baby**
With prolonged cultivation, **spring and autumn stirrings** arise.
Fear the **leakage of fluids**, the loss of control—
Invoke **Táokāng**, grasp the **Heavenly Sovereign’s Symbol**, and chant:
*"O **Gate of Life, Lord of the Peach, Child of the Dao’s Safety**,
Merge and prolong the **Essence-Qi**, ascending to the **Néihuán Palace**!
Let any **demonic evil** dare assail the **True Law**—
Molten gold and fire shall shatter the **Chamber of the Cavern**!"*
Thus, the **illness of fluid leakage** is averted.
**Avoid meat, blood, and carrion.**

**Healing All Ailments, Nurturing the Spirit-Essence.**

Recite the incantation and stabilize the *qi*, then the spirit shall be clear and the *qi* shall be refreshed.
**Malicious dreams and demonic trials**, invoke the spirit’s name,
preserve the **Five Spirit Awakenings**,
and chant thus:

*"O **True Sovereign of the Great Cavern**,
Extend and refine the **Three Spirits**!
The **first spirit**, swiftly bind the **Seven Ghostly Attachments**;
The **second spirit**, swiftly guard the **Néihuán Palace**;
The **third spirit**, under the **Heavenly Sovereign’s** command,
Swiftly summon the **Sovereign of the Three Highest**!
Should any **inauspicious dream** arise,
the **Seven Ghostly Attachments** shall wander as a **corpse-spirit**,
conspiring with **evil sources** in the east,
urgently invoke **Táokāng** to protect and destroy,
the **root of malevolence**,
reverse **misfortune** into **auspiciousness**,
and **life and death** shall have no **obstacle**—
**Seal the *qi* of command**, and there shall be no dreams at all.

**The Method of Removing the Three Corpse-Spirits**
Upper Corpse-Spirit, Middle Corpse-Spirit, Lower Corpse-Spirit—rightward affix the **symbol**.
On days **Jiazi** and **Gengshen**,
write in **cinnabar**,
take at the hour of **human stillness**,
and ingest it.
Seven times, the **corpse-worms** shall depart on their own.
Again, at **dawn and dusk**, with the left hand
caressing the heart and reciting the incantation,
they shall not dare to harm.
The incantation:

*"Nine Heavens’ Supreme Sovereign, Four Gates and Eight Spirits!
Seven Celestial Officials and Two Mysteries, Three Pure and Nine Azure.
**Táokāng of the Great One**, ascending to the **Three Pure Ones**.
I beseech the **Imperial Sovereign**,
to seize and contemplate the **Yellow Peace**!
At dusk, summon the **Seven Ghostly Attachments**;
at dawn, call upon the **Three Spirits**!
When the spirit is **suppressed** and the *qi* is **refreshed**,
should any **inauspiciousness** arise,
the **Seven-Star Divine Soldiers**,
but summon the **True Spirit**!
Let **filth flow** and **refine the form**,
**sever and destroy** the **demonic essence**!
The **Three Spirits** in harmony and gentleness,
the **blood-corpse** and **depraved spirit** shall sink.
The spirit returns to its **scarlet abode**,
facing **auspiciousness and rectitude**!
Grant me **harmony with the immortals**,
long preserve my **spirit’s vitality**!
As swift as the **Highest Sovereign’s** decree from the **Celestial Jade Purity**!"

Another incantation:
*"Nine Heavens’ Jade Sovereign, Four Pure and Eight Sceneries!
Seven Dawns and Two Mysteries, Three Pure and Other Gates—
**Táokāng** merges and prolongs,
I beseech and summon the **Three Spirits**!
Ascending to the **Celestial Jade Purity**,
the spirit returns to the **Golden Official**,
to **banish all inauspiciousness**!
Should any dare to resist,
**fire-armored soldiers** shall be raised!
The **immortals** command me,
long preserve the **First Year**!
As swift as the **Highest Sovereign’s** decree from the **Celestial Jade Purity**!"

**The Great Cavern True Person’s Method of Refining Jade Essence to Nourish the Body**
First, on a **Gengshen** day at dawn,
knock the teeth **seventy-two times**,
and take the **play of *qi* from the southeast**—
**play of *qi* from the southeast**—
into the **Lower Elixir Field**,
transforming into a **baby**.
Having completed the recitation,
use the tongue to press the **upper palate**,
stirring the **inner and outer mouth**,
and **jade essence** shall spontaneously arise.
Rinsing fully, swallow it into the **stomach of the upper baby**.
Its spirit dwells beneath the heart;
when the **Imperial Sovereign** opens his eyes,
it shall then be directed.
In ten days, the face shall radiate **jade light**,
the body shall lose its **wrinkles**,
and **all ailments** shall not arise.
The incantation:

*"O **Sovereign of the Great One** and **True Person of Command**,
The **Han Palace refines the spirit**, the **Southern Court receives its name**.
The **Three Platforms** condense their **luminous essence**,
and I begin to be born.
**Jade essence** pours into the **Golden Spring**,
the **Golden Spring** returns to the **Azure True Person**.
In the **white day**, ascending to heaven,
I meet the **Jade Sovereign**.
As swift as the **Highest Sovereign’s** decree!"*

**The Heavenly Sovereign’s Bestowal of the Southern Court’s Method of Refining the Body by the Celestial Jade Official**
*"Heavenly, Heavenly! Pay me my **original spirit**!
**Li** shall have few **ailments**,
**Kàn** shall have no **form-spirit**!
Sever the **hundred demonic barriers**,
sweep away the **flames of the One True**!
I command with **reverent virtue**,
the **Heavenly Court’s Azure Water**!
Cooked and refined with fire,
**roasted** into the **womb of the embryo**!
I practice this method,
and **fire-light flows through my form**!
The **Five Sovereigns** guard me,
and I ascend to the **Heavenly Dawn**!
As swift as the **Southern Court’s** decree by **Han Lord’s** father-in-law!"*

Rightward, at **six Yang times**,
facing **south** and reciting the incantation,
**absorb and bind the One *qi*** with the mouth,
and swallow it—**twenty-one times** as the measure.

**The Method of Restraining the Three Spirits**
The method states:
On the **third, thirteenth, and twenty-third** of each month,
that evening, the **Three Spirits** shall abandon the body and wander outside.
Those who seize them
should recline on their back,
remove the pillow,
extend the feet,
and cross the hands over the heart.
Close the eyes,
seal the *qi* for **three breaths**,
knock the teeth **three times**.
Preserve in the heart a **red *qi****, like a **chicken egg** emerging from within and exiting the mouth.
The *qi* shall be like fire,
enveloping the body all around—
when aware, the body shall feel slightly warm.
Call upon the **Three Spirits**.
The incantation:

The **Celestial Palace of Taiwei**, within the **Central Yellow**—
beginning with **Azure Primordial**.
**Refine the Three Spirits within**,
nurturing the **Embryonic Light** in tranquility.
The **Divine Treasure Chamber of Jade**—
born with me, never straying.
**Do not move recklessly**—
the **Yellow Court** watches over the **Spirit Sovereign**,
the **Supreme Spirit** guards in vigilance.
If you wish to **ascend and soar**,
only to the **Jade Purity** you shall go.
**Hunger and thirst?**—
swallow and drink the **Jade Crystal**.

**Urgent as the True Person of Taiyi, the Three Platforms Jade Emperor’s Edict.**

**The Spirit-Binding Talisman**
This talisman:
**Strike the Heavenly Drum seventy-two times**,
inscribed in **white on two sheets**.

Another talisman:
**Ring the Golden Bell thirty-six times**,
inscribed in **crimson on yellow**.

Another talisman:
**Sound the Jade Chime twenty-four times**,
inscribed in **black on white**.

---

**The Method of Restraining the Seven Souls**
On the **first, fifteenth, and thirtieth** of each month,
or the **twenty-first and nineteenth** in short months,
the **Seven Souls** wander and conspire with ghosts.
**To bind the Spirits and return the Souls:**

On this day, recline on your back, extend your feet,
cover both ears with your palms, pressing fingers to the crown.
Close your eyes,
seal the *qi* for **seven breaths**,
knock the teeth **seven times**.
Focus in the heart—
a **white *qi*,** the size of a **mung bean**, grows,
gradually expanding through the **nine layers** of the body.
Suddenly, it transforms into **two Azure Dragons** in the eyes,
a **White Tiger** in the nostrils,
a **Vermilion Bird** over the heart,
a **Spirit Serpent** at the left foot,
and a **Azure Tortoise** at the right.
Two maidens in **brocade robes**, bearing **flames of light**, stand at the ear gates.

Swallow the saliva **seven times**,
and call the **Seven Souls** by name:
**Shi Gou, Fu Shi, Que Yin, Tun Zei, Fei Du, Chu Zui, Chou Fei.**
The incantation:

*"The Nine Returns of the Pure *Qi*, restraining the Souls, repelling deceit.
The Heavenly Marshal guards the gate, the maiden holds the pass.
Refine the Souls to gentleness, let them dwell with me in harmony.
Do not move recklessly—
watch over the **Source of Form**.
If hunger or thirst arises, allow the **Yellow Elixir** to be consumed."*

**Incantation before sleep:**

At the time of retiring to bed, the **Four Beasts** shall emerge to guard the body.
The **Azure Dragon** issues from my liver, residing at my left.
The **White Tiger** issues from my lungs, residing at my right.
The **Vermilion Bird** issues from my heart, residing before me.
The **Spirit Serpent** issues from my kidneys, residing behind me.

You, the **Four Beasts**,
grind your teeth and sharpen your blades,
dwelling at my left, right, front, and rear—
repelling all malevolent spirits and wicked ghosts,
keeping them a thousand leagues distant,
so they dare not come near
and disturb my **Jade Chamber**.

Sleep soundly and peacefully,
free from evil dreams and spectral illusions.
**Swiftly, swiftly, as the commandments decree.**

**Incantation for Preserving the Spirit:**
The liver stores the **Soul** (*hun*),
the lungs store the **Soul** (*po*),
the heart stores the **Spirit** (*shen*),
the spleen stores the **Will** (*zhi*),
the kidneys store the **Essence** (*jing*).

The **Azure Dragon** returns to my liver,
the **White Tiger** returns to my lungs,
the **Vermilion Bird** returns to my heart,
the **Spirit Serpent** returns to my kidneys.
The **Yellow Dragon** (*Huang Long*) steadies my spleen,
to fortify my **abdomen** (*real venter*).

No malevolent spirits or wicked ghosts
shall dwell below.
**Swiftly, swiftly, as the commandments decree.**

Another method:
When lying down, place your hand upon your heart
and pray:
*"May the **Heavenly Spirit** (*Tian Ling*) and **Vital Nodes** (*Jie Rong*) flourish,
granting me eternal life.
O **Five Zang** (*visceral sovereigns*), may you now rest in tranquility.
If a man recites this seven times,
or a woman recites it twenty-four times,
it will ensure longevity and freedom from illness."*

**Method for Warding Off Evil Dreams:**
If an evil dream arises, do not speak.

**Morning Ritual for Warding Off Evil Dreams:**
At dawn, spit upon the water facing east. Recite the incantation:
*"May evil dreams cling to grasses and trees,
and auspicious dreams become precious jade."*

**Method for Calming the Five Zang:**
On the night of the new moon, when all is still, lie with your head facing north. Place your left hand upon your heart and recite:
*"O sovereigns of the Five Zang,
divine manifestations of Dao and virtue,
the Sun is your lord, the Moon your lady—
all now guard the True Person [Name].
Men recite seven times, women recite fourteen times,
to prolong life and enhance longevity."*

**Method for Safe Travel:**
Before setting out, keep the *Dou Gang* (Big Dipper’s handle) in mind above your head, silently reciting without pause. Thus, you shall not encounter malevolent spirits, and all paths shall be auspicious.
If going to war, hold the *Dou Bing* (Big Dipper’s handle) before you, pointing at the enemy—great fortune shall follow.
Incantation:
*"The primal power of Heaven, beneficent and unyielding,
swiftly, as the commandments decree."*

**Method for Subduing Demons:**
When sleeping, or walking in darkness, or encountering stubborn, malevolent spirits causing mischief, steady your body and mind, casting aside all distractions. Recite:
*"At the tip of a single hair,
the Jewel King’s realm appears.
Seated in motes of dust,
the Great Dharma Wheel turns.
Extinguishing all sentient beings,
piercing the veil of dusty labor.
Within your subtle awareness,
as wind extinguishes flame.
Like a blade cutting water—
no contact remains.
You are like boiling water,
they are like solid ice.
As warm *qi* approaches,
they shall soon perish."*

**Method for Ceasing Ear Ringing:**
If ear ringing persists, focus your mind and recite:
*"Spirit is present, spirit is present, spirit is present."*

**Incantation to Banish Sleep:**
*"Om! Jidi Yidi Pige Na Dan Di Po Sa Ba He!"*
The master should step onto the left foot upon ascending the bed, clacking the teeth seventy-seven times, preventing sleep.
This practice, when maintained, is supremely refined.

**Method for Warding Off Calamities:**
When the master fears disaster by day or night, or encounters the Three Calamities and Nine Adversities, recite:
*"I take Heaven as my father,
Earth as my mother.
Within them, I dwell as an innocent child.
The Sun is my clerk, the Moon my scribe.
Thunderer and Lightning Mother stand at my sides,
Wind Lord and Rain Master at my fore and aft.
The Six Jia talismans encircle me.
The Azure Dragon supports my left,
the White Tiger attends my right.
The Vermilion Bird guides my front,
the Dark Warrior follows my rear.
The Northern Dipper covers my head,
the Celestial Ganges points to my hands.
The Azure Serpent coils at my feet,
to annihilate my misfortunes.
Within the Elixir Chamber I reside,
Taiyi as my consort.
Three on the left, seven on the right,
wearing Nine above, stepping One below.
Two and four as shoulders,
six and eight as feet.
Within this, I dwell—
my abdomen fortified.
Now I command ten thousand ghosts and spirits:
Return to your proper stations.
Those who oppose me shall die,
those who betray me shall perish.
Flee swiftly, hide in obscurity!
Heaven’s mighty enforcers,
behead all inauspicious omens!
Swiftly, as the Highest Celestial Jade Purity True King’s decree."*

This incantation repels a hundred evils and the Five Plague spirits, banishing all unrighteous ghosts and deities.
The practitioner should visualize and recite it within a purified space.

**Method for Restoring the Spirit:**
On the fifteenth and last days of each month, first speak inwardly: *"Spirit, spirit."*
Then, with the left hand pressed upon the heart, whisper:
*"Spirit, spirit, dwell in my palace.
Enter my hall, abide with me.
Speak with me—
never depart from my side."*

「The Yellow **Qi** guards the center and transforms into the **Dao/Way**-form.
*Photah! Photah!* Swiftly, as the decree.
Recite three times to the right—then the **Dao/Way**-form guards the body,
and a hundred evils and myriad illnesses cannot enter.

**Method for Illuminating the Eyes:**
At the time of the rooster’s crow,
visualize within the eyes that each contains a person,
three inches tall, clad in black robes, standing upright.
Respectfully recite the incantation:
*"Left Eye, Right Moon—restored to the **Dao/Way**-form of **Xuanlang** (玄朗).
Grant me piercing vision—
all matters a thousand *li* distant shall be seen.*
Recite twenty-one times.
Or if one has afflictions,
it shall prevent their revelation.

**Method for Self-Solving Sorrows:**
If the practitioner’s eyes blink involuntarily,
ears ring, heart races, or face grows hot—
a **Dao/Way**-form sorrow is approaching,
and misfortune is certain.
Silently recite the incantation:
*"The **Dao/Way**-form Master of Life and Heavenly Communication,
bind my fate with a golden thread—
grant me eternal prosperity, endless years.*
Recite three times, and it shall cease.

**Incantation for Preventing Hair Loss from Combing:**
Upon the **Dao/Way**-form’s crown,
the **Xuanhua** (玄華) **Baojing** (寶精) resides.
The left is the **Yinyi** (隐日) Eye,
the right is the **Yuegen** (月根) Moon.
Today’s refinement shall benefit a hundred **Dao/Way**-forms.
After completion, comb the hair—
it shall never fall again.
The **Dao/Way**-form’s brilliance is revealed.

**Dongguan (洞觀) Division**.»

**Qingwei (清微) Section:**

**Yu Yu (禹余) – Supreme Red (太赤) Right Talisman:**
On the *Year-End Night*, if sudden calamity arises, this shall dissolve it.
Write on **yellow paper with black ink** and carry it—
or, if inscribed on **red on yellow**, swallow it twice at **midnight (between 11 PM and 2 AM)**.
Its divine power is potent; swallow saliva and seal the *qi*.
Within one month, the **Six Ding (六丁)** shall obey your command.
Naturally, your mind shall foreknow fortune and misfortune—
report it in advance.

**Six Jia (六甲) True Taboo Right Talisman:**
Face **east in spring, south in summer, west in autumn, north in winter, south after midnight, north before dawn**.
Sit upright, strike teeth **thirty-six times** to circulate *qi*, then seal the breath while reciting the incantation and gargle saliva **nine times**.
After **one hundred days**, a jade-like radiance shall appear on your face,
and the hundred spirits shall guard your body—
you shall foreknow all fortune and misfortune.

**Northern Dipper (北斗七星) True Taboo Right Talisman:**
Write in **red ink**, place in a **bamboo tube**, seal with wax, and hide in a **chicken coop**.
After **seven times seven days**, swallow it with **east-flowing water**.
Your spirit shall brighten, and you shall recite **ten thousand words daily**.

**Southern Dipper (南斗六星) True Taboo** [incantation omitted].

「Natural knowledge of fortune and misfortune shall arise—
it is fitting to foretell them beforehand.

**True Taboo of the Six Jia (六甲真讳):**
Right method: In spring, face east; in summer, south; in autumn, west; in winter, north; at midnight, south; before dawn, north.
Sit upright, strike teeth **thirty-six times** to circulate *qi*,
then seal the breath while reciting the incantation and gargle saliva **nine times**.
After **one hundred days**, a jade-like radiance shall appear on your face,
and the hundred spirits shall guard your body—
you shall foreknow all fortune and misfortune.

**True Taboo of the Northern Dipper (北斗七星真讳):**
Right method: Write in **red ink** on a **yellow paper talisman**,
burn it beneath a lamp, and observe if a **purple cloud** and **strange fragrance** appear.
If a **white-clothed god** with a sword is seen within the lamp, it is an omen of misfortune;
if a **divine figure in a crown and simple attire** appears, it is an omen of fortune.
This may avert death and bring rebirth.
**Avoid**: filial sons, monks, chickens and dogs, menstruating women, and omens of ill fortune.
By this method, swallow the talisman to dispel **malevolent spirits** and **preserve life**.

**Supreme Purity Divine Method: The Right Talisman for Dispelling Evil Spirits (上清妙行真人辅正破祟符):**
Enter a **pure chamber**, focus the spirit, and gather the *qi* of the **five directions** and **heaven, earth, sun, and moon**.
Blow upon the brush and inscribe the talisman.
For major matters, use **Jiazi divination**, invoke a certain deity,
and according to the **imperial edict**, channel the **true *qi*** into the talisman for a specific purpose.
Incantation:
*"Northern Dipper Spirit Child (北斗灵童), one call, a hundred respond.
Supreme Unity (太一) Communing with Spirits, one call, a hundred respond."*
The **Dharma Master** recites this **seven times**,
then blows and sprinkles the talisman in water to be swallowed by the afflicted.
Gather the *qi* of the **five directions** into the talisman,
and summon the **Five Star Spirits of Imperial Response (五星灵应帝君)**,
to harmonize and extend the lifespan of a certain person.
**Swiftly, swiftly, as the Primordial Sovereign (元始天尊) decrees to the True Lord of the Dharma (本师真君).**
Inscribe one talisman and wear it on the head.
Inscribe three more and swallow them.
At night, inscribe one more.
Use **five-colored paper money** as a substitute for the person’s body,
and with **seven parts tea wine**, under the open sky,
face the **Northern Dipper and its myriad stars**,
and set up an incense altar with lamps and candles to worship as prescribed.
The **Dharma Master** and **fasting officials** shall fully confess all sins committed in life.
In silence, pray to:
**Northern Dipper Supreme of the Dark Vault (北斗玄穹上帝),**
**Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper (北斗七元星君),**
**Left Minister and Right Minister Stars (左辅右弼星君),**
and the **Divine Marshal of the Northern Dipper (北斗中神仙将吏).**
For **so-and-so**, whose parents have suffered prolonged illness,
and who is also imprisoned by public litigation, unable to resolve it,
**so-and-so** now offers their **lifespan and years of fortune**,
to prolong and protect the lives of their parents.
After the prayers conclude,
under the **Northern Dipper’s stars**, burn the **five-colored paper money**—
a substitute for the person’s body—
and present the **paper money petition**.
Thus, for every **first offense of the month**, three times,
fortune and benefit shall be attained.

**Three days constitute one divination (算),**
**one year constitutes one lifespan (寿),**
**twelve years constitute one cycle (纪).**
The **Jiazi divination**, repeated **seven times**, shall confirm the efficacy of the incantation.

**Right Method of the Daoist Master’s Practice:**
At night, when going to sleep, the **Northern Dipper’s stars** shall be observed for omens of response.
Arrange the **divine formations (罡)** on the mat,
lie down, and recite the **Northern Dipper incantation**,
preserving the body as a **White Crane Immortal (白鹤仙人)**,
gazing upward at the Dipper to await **Heaven’s decree**.
Before sleep, recite the **Great Protective Body Incantation** once more.
Those who receive the **Great Dao** shall daily preserve their spirit,
reciting it **ten times**, or even **thousands and millions of times**—
its merit is beyond description.

Incantation:
*"The Great Sovereign descends, malevolence is suppressed,
favor emanates from the **Supreme Purity’s Nine Heavens (上清九天)**.
Deploying the **Divine Marshal**, the **Five Sacred Peaks** are subdued,
ranked formations welcome the **Ten Thousand Leagues**.
Winds and clouds unite, all mountains’ grass and trees are flattened.
The **cloud’s head passes** the **Northern Sea (北海)**,
**rain’s foot reaches** the **Southern Darkness (南冥)**.
The **Black Slayer** is the **Central Taboo (中禁)**,
**Tianpeng** establishes the **Divine Camp (御营)**.
The **Spirit Official** holds the **jade seal (玉印)**,
**Supreme Unity** presents the **golden essence (金精)**.
Seated on the **Quaking Steed**, astride the **Red Tiger (朱虎)**,
the **vanguard rides** the **Great Whale (大鲸)**.
**Lightning flames** fly with **fierce fire**,
**thunder drums** shake the **Celestial Court (天廷)**.
Commands are issued to the **Three Realms (三界)**,
punishments are carried out by the **Six Celestial Warriors (六丁)**.
The **White Sovereign** proclaims the **Great Release (豁落)**,
the **Spirit Child** advances with the **Brightening Incantation (开明)**.
The **Earth Net** encircles all,
the **Heavenly Snare** is woven as soldiers.
**Fiery outputs** rise with **red flames**,
**feathered banners** generate **emerald smoke**.
The **Heavenly Axis trembles** and the **Earthly Pivot moves**,
the **cosmos is shaken** in terror.
*Qi* devours the **exhausted sea**,
force topples the **leaning Tai Mountain (泰山)**.
The **Tiger responds** to **Geng-Xin (庚辛) White**,
the **Dragon follows** **Jia-Yi (甲乙) Green**.
Sever the **maddened and chaotic**,
dispel the **evil and venomous**.
Subdue the **lower ghosts** and the **maddened and rebellious**—
no need for laborious warfare.
All **demons** are today extinguished,
**ten thousand ghosts** flee in haste.
**Swiftly, swiftly**, as the **Jade Purity Sovereign’s (玉清上帝) sacred decree**,
there shall be no disobedience.
Recite the incantation **three times**,
gather the *qi* from the **east-northeast**,
and blow upon your left and right sides.
With the **left hand**, pinch the **Jade Seal of the Dao (玉诀)**,
strike teeth **thirty-six times** to circulate *qi*,
and inscribe this incantation.
Have someone bring it back,
together with **gold coins, clouds, and the Horse of the Gods (云马)**,
and burn it in the **central courtyard**—
this shall confirm the capture of **malevolent spirits and evil specters**.

**Taboo-Dispelling Talisman (解秽符):**
All **Daoist officials and Dharma Masters**,
when entering or exiting, or passing through places
such as **funeral homes, defiled sites, or rooms of childbirth**,
or encountering **hunting dogs, livestock, or any defilement**,
shall return to the **altarpiece** and purify it.
Use this talisman, burn it to ash,
mix with **pure water**, and take *qi* from the **east-southeast** in **three sips**.
Recite the **Jade Sovereign’s Incantation** **three times**,
pinching the **Jade Seal of the Jade Sovereign (玉帝诀)**,
and name it the **Three Realms Incantation (三境咒)**.

**Taboo-Dispelling and Body-Purifying Talisman (解秽净身符):**
Recite the **Pure Heaven and Earth Incantation (净天地咒)**,
gather the *qi* from the **east-northeast**,
and with the **incantation-brush**, write in **red ink**.
Burn the ash into the water and recite the incantation.
Gather *qi* once more and blow into the water.
**Daoist officials** and those of the **Three Jia (三甲)** or **outer ranks**,
use the method with **three sprays of water**.
Incantation:
*"Heaven and Earth move in cycles,
the essence of sun and moon.
Light pierces the **Four Seas**,
cutting off all **demonic spirits**.
Ghosts are suppressed and lie dormant,
the body radiates with **divine light**.
Once the **divine light** manifests,
all **defilements** are swept away.
Any who dare not submit,
shall be sent to the **Heavenly Executioner (天丁)**.
**Swiftly, swiftly**, as the **sacred decree**.
Establish the **altarpiece ritual (建坛式)**."」

---

**Ritual for Establishing the Altarpiece (建坛式)**

In all cases of establishing the altarpiece,
sit facing south with north at your back,
and arrange the **Three Teacher (三师)** positions.
In the center, place the **Uppermost True (上真)** position;
to the left, the **Divine General (神将)** position;
to the right, the **Dharma Master (法师)** position.
Additionally, set one **Celestial Master (天师)** position,
and place an ink seal box on either side.
Place a peach-branch altar before the table,
and set out a jar of water.
At the heart of the altarpiece,
secure the **mirror-sword (镜剑)**.

**Rite of Prohibition (禁式)**

For those who wish to perform this ritual,
upon entering the chamber,
first recite the **Purification of the Body Incantation (浄身咒)**,
then the **Purification of Heaven and Earth Incantation (浄天地咒)**.
When finished,
next recite the **Incantation for Entering the Gate (入户咒)**.
Visualize the **Functionary Officials’ Divine Soldiers (功曹神兵)** descending from the void to your left and right.
Pinch the second knuckle of your index and middle fingers,
and perform the **Yu Bu (禹步)** in the **Fighting Stance (斗)**.
Gaze toward the southeast and gather *qi*,
blowing it leftward and rightward.
Visualize yourself as the **True King (真王)**,
with the **Four Spirits (四灵)**—left as the **Sun Spirit (日)**, right as the **Moon Spirit (月)**—
the **Five Stars (五星)** above your head,
and the **Twenty-eight Constellations (二十八宿)** encircling you.
The **Divine Mist (神霄)** and **Divine Treasury (神府)** stand beside the Teacher,
like a dense fog.

Next, visualize the **True King (真王)**, **Qinghua (青华)**, and **Master Han (韩君)**—the **Three Teachers (三师)**—
within the **Five-Colored Auspicious Clouds (五色庆云)** in the southeast.
Having completed the **Three Celestial Steps (三台丁步)** before the incense altar,
press your hands to your heart,
and strike your teeth three times,
visualizing the *qi* of the **Nine-Colored Clouds (九色云炁)** rising from the incense,
piercing the **Nine Heavens (九天)**.

**Invocation:**

*"The sky is clear, the *qi* pure,
the Three Lights (三光) radiant and bright.
The Golden Chamber, the Jade Hall,
where Five Sacred Herbs (五芝) flourish with treasure.
The Black, Yellow, Purple, and White *qi* come to illumine my form.
The Jade Boys and Jade Girls (玉童玉女)
attend to my sacred rites.
The Nine *qi* ascend in harmony,
the Three Lights move as one.
The Purple Canopy (紫盖) rises,
and I ascend into the Imperial Court (帝庭).
Swiftly, swiftly, as the sacred decree."*

**Next, offer incense and present the petition:**

*"Your humble servant of the [designated rank],
with incense burning and precious sticks ablaze,
the ritual drawn from the Celestial Texts (天文).
From the Golden Furnace (金炉),
the auspicious *qi* condenses in the void.
Scattering the Jade Smoke (玉烟),
the auspicious clouds form a canopy.
In response to this reverence,
I must now invoke the mirror.

With sincere devotion, I pray to the **Numinous True Ones (灵真)**,
that they descend and echo my call.

Now I perform the ritual,
offering with reverence the **Dao Incense (道香)**,
the **Virtue Incense (德香)***,
the **Incense of Effortless Purity (无为清浄香)***,
the **Incense of Naturalness (自然香)***,
the **Incense of Marvelous Cavernous Truth (妙洞真香)***,
the **Incense of Numinous Treasure and Wisdom (灵宝慧香)***,
the **Incense Beyond the Three Realms (超三界香)***,
the **Incense of the Three Realms (三境真香)***,
and the **Incense of the Perfumed Jade Capital, Encompassing the Universal Dharma Realm (满琼楼玉京遍周天法界香)**,
to honor the **Three Pure Ones (三清上帝)**,
the **Ten Directions of Highest Truth (十极高真)**,
the **Ancestral Teacher, Most High Numinous Celestial Master, True King of Jade Purity, Eternal Life Preserver, Heavenly Sovereign of Command (祖师高上神霄玉清真王长生保命天尊)**,
the **Master Teacher, Most High Numinous Celestial King, Qinghua the Saviour of Suffering, Eternal Life Preserver, Heavenly Sovereign of Fixed Fate (宗师高上神霄玉清王青华救苦太一定福天尊)**,
the **True Teacher, Master Han of the Nine Heavens, Director of Beneficial Calculations, Keeper of Life, Saviour of Suffering, Heavenly Sovereign of Auspicious Fate (真师九天益算司命好生可韩君丈人保福天尊)**,
the **Eastern and Western Celestial Platforms’ Immortal Lords (东西华台仙卿)***,
the **Leftmost Numinous One (左玄真人)***,
the **Officer of the Demon-Driving Agency (驱邪院使)***,
the **Supervisor of Divine Symbols (神符总监)***,
the **Two Great Generals Commanding the Armies (统兵二大将军)***,
the **Generals of the Thunder Department (雷部诸大将军)***,
the **Divine Symbol Clerks and Soldiers (神符吏兵)***,
the **Functionary Officials’ Messengers (功曹使者)***,
and all **Rulers and Sovereigns (一切主宰)**.
May they descend their **True *Qi* (真炁)**,
enter my humble servant’s **penetrating script (笔法)**,
and inscribe the **divine symbols (符)** to subdue ghosts,
with great and numinous power.

Your servant, presumptuous and guilty of transgressing Heaven’s might,
deserves ten thousand deaths.
Your servant, in deepest dread and fear,
prostrates with head bowed and hands clasped,
twice kneels in solemn reverence,
and humbly speaks these words."*

When performing rituals before all **Rulers and Sovereigns (一切主宰)**, one should present the request as desired and they will grant it. After completing the invocation, recite the **Great Exorcism Chant (都咒)** once, gather **True *Qi* (真炁)**, and blow it onto the pen. Then, strike the pen three times firmly on the ground before writing. Do not speak with others, lest you risk wearying the **Divine (神)**.

Use only **yellow silk with vermilion script (黄素朱书)** for the **Great Exorcism Chant (都咒)**, placing it within the pen’s shaft. On every **third *Jiu* day (三九日)***, gather **True *Qi* (真炁)** three times and infuse it into the pen’s shaft. For ordinary writing purposes, this **ritual pen (法笔)** must not be used.

When entering a patient’s home for treatment, wear the **True Form Diagram (真形图)** and carry the **Step-Drum (步斗)** with care. Next, lay out the **Divine Domain Diagram (分域图)** on the ground, visualizing it as a **true golden jade gate (真金玉阙)**, with thirty doors—eastern, western, front, and back—each emitting golden radiance and jade light that envelops my body.

Then, with the left hand, pinch the **Hypothetical Celestial Stem (辰文)** and write the **Summoning Functionary Officials’ Symbol (召功曹符)** once, burning it on the **Perseus direction (巽)**. When the **Functionary Officials (功曹)** arrive, loudly proclaim:

*"To me, by fire! Quickly assemble all the **Divine Generals (灵官)** of this **Domain (府)**, the **Functionary Officials (功曹)**, **Generals (将军)**, **Junior Officers (童君)**, **Jade Juniors (玉童)**, **Jade Maidens (玉女)**, and **Clerks and Soldiers (吏兵)**! Now, array yourselves in solemn **威仪**, descend together in unison, and obey my command at this **Domain (府)**. Swiftly, as the **precepts decree! (如律令)**.*

*"All the **Supreme Commanders (主帅)** mentioned above shall be within the **Five-Colored Auspicious Clouds (五色庆云)**, clad in **Five-Colored Cloud Brocade (五色云锦)**, each wielding new **divine instruments (新器械)**. Now, burn the **left and right Supervisors’ Talismans (左右总监坛符)** and the **Generals’ Talismans (将军符)**.

*"To me, **Commanders of the Armies (统兵)**! Follow me to the home of **so-and-so (某人)**. Seize the **ghosts and gods (鬼神)**, interrogate the **possessing entity (附体)**, and reveal its name in clear speech. Swiftly! (疾疾)**.*

*"If further use is required, present the request as desired and employ them accordingly. Now, invoke the **Dispatched Chants (遣咒)**:

*'By the **Sovereign’s Mandate (皇天睿命)** and the **Jade Emperor’s Symbol (玉帝颁符)**, I am entrusted with this **Daoist office (法职)**, overseeing the **Jade Celestial Treasury (神霄玉府)**, granted the **Nine Sacrificial Offerings (九锡)**, the **Ten Auspicious Titles (十贾)**, the **Eight Thunders of Authority (八威之册)**, the **Lantern-Carriage of the Celestial (丹霄之舆)**, the **Dragon Script and Phoenix Seal (龙文凤玺)**, and the *Purple Silk Canon (紫素之书)*. I hereby announce to all **Ten Thousand Gods (万神)**, none dare obstruct me!*

*'The **Five Sacred Mountains (五岳)** and **Four Great Waters (四渎)**, respond to my command! By **imperial decree (敕)**, let **so-and-so God-General (某神将)** proceed to **so-and-so’s home (某家)** to fulfill **this matter (某事)**, moving with the urgency of wind and fire, not lingering in place!*

*'The **Thousand Demons and Ten Thousand Spirits (千妖万魅)** shall receive my command and be exterminated. The **Divine Retribution (明回报应)** will be clear, and the **reward of merit (功)** shall be inscribed in **Jade Emptiness (玉虚)**. Within the **Three Realms (三界)**, who dares oppose me? My **Divine Sword (神剑)** will slaughter, and my **Mighty Soldiers (威兵)** will charge swiftly! I stand before the **altarpiece (坛)**, sword in hand, awaiting them. Swiftly! (疾疾)**.*

*'Swiftly, by the **Highest Sovereign’s Precepts (高上神霄玉清真王天尊律令)**!*

### **Method of Exorcism for Possession (摄邪治祟附体法)**
When treating illness, upon entering a home, step with the **left foot (左脚)** upon the door. Visualize the **Jade City and Golden Gate (玉城金阙)**, then proceed with the **Step-Drum (藏身斗)**.

With the **right hand (右手)**, pinch the **Step-Drum Seal (斗印)**. As you step forward, recite the **names of the Yang Stars of the Big Dipper (阳斗名)**, and as you step backward, recite the **names of the Yin Stars of the Big Dipper (阴斗名)**. Envelop the body with the **Step-Drum’s protective energy (剔斗盖身)**, then swiftly recite the **Protective Body Chant (护身咒)**.

Only then shall you recite the **patient’s affliction (病人)**. Next, proceed in order with the **ritual (持)**.

### **Protective Body Chant (护身咒)**
*"The **Seven Sovereigns of the Big Dipper (北斗七王星)**, great and responsive, their **numinous power (灵)** felt! The **Three Celestial Platforms (三台)** aid me before and behind, shielding my form with their **auspicious protection (覆护)**. Swiftly, as the **Highest Sovereign’s Precepts (高上神霄玉清真王律令)** decree!"*

### **Fire Enclosure Talisman (火罩符)**
*"Flame’s numinous essence (炎灵), flame’s numinous essence! The **Fire Emperor’s essence (火帝之精)**!*

*'Fire spreads ten thousand *li*, vanquishing ghosts without trace (万里流火，鬼灭无形)! It clears the heavens and brings eternal peace to the earth (喷天豁清，噀地永宁)! It grants **longevity (长生)** to mortals and annihilates the **form of demons (鬼灭形)**!*

*'Temporarily departing the **Treasure Hall (宝殿)**, the **Fire Enclosure’s numinous power (火罩之灵)**! I summon the **Great Fire Wheel General of the Southern Realm (南方大火轮将)**, who shall **awaken the Three Mystic Fires (放三昧真火)** and enclose them for my protection. Swiftly! (疾疾)**.*

*'By this method, form the **Great Fire Seal (大火输印)** and pinch the **central text (中文)** with the middle finger. Visualize the **patient’s form (一人形)**, or the **General’s appearance (若将军状)**, riding upon the **True Fire (真火)** and leading **a hundred thousand Fire Soldiers (火兵十万人)**. Before and behind, they shall enclose and protect, and the **patient’s home (病人家)** shall all be within **smoke and flames (烟火中)**!"*

### **Entering the Home Method (入门法)**
*"Jade Celestial Treasury (神霄玉清), Ten Thousand Heavenly Soldiers (十万天丁)!"*

Seize the malevolent spirits swiftly and press them into **Yin City (酆城)**.
Pursue the wandering soul and capture the wandering spirit, delivering them to the afflicted person.
*"With **Gaja** and **Kai** (伽与栲), with capture and restraint (与捉与擒).*
Conform to the imperial decree, and declare their name upon attachment.
Swiftly! (疾疾).

**Method:**
Pinch the **Chenwen (辰文)** and gather the **Xun-qi (巽炁)**, visualizing the **Heavenly Soldiers’ mighty warriors (天丁力士)** driving away what would not come.
If they do not arrive, then employ the **Confusion of the Soul Spell (迷魂咒)**.

**Confusion of the Soul Method (迷魂法):**
Write a **Soul Official’s (灵官)** talisman of one’s life destiny in accordance with the method, and burn it beneath the afflicted person’s feet.
Visualize the Soul Official ascending in **Jiangxiao (绛霄)**, clad in the **Nine-Beam Crown (九梁冠)**, arriving above the patient’s head.
**Spell:**
*"By the decree of **Jade Celestial Treasury (神霄玉清)**, I urgently seize the living soul of [name] and place it under my guardianship, with no negligence allowed.*
Swiftly! (疾疾).

**Again, the spell:**
*"Heaven is darkened, earth is darkened, the Six Spirits are darkened—
the Soul Official, **Dai Zuo (戴佐)**, swiftly darken with me!"*

**Great Capture Method (大捉法):**
First, step into the **Lunar Lodge (斗)**, positioning the afflicted person within it.
On all sides, visualize the **Divine Officials (神吏)** encircling and securing them.
Burn two talismans—**Grand Marshal General (总监大将军)** and **Commanding Army General (统兵大将军)**—beneath the afflicted person’s feet.
**Spell:**
*"By the decree of **Jade Celestial Treasury King (神霄玉清王)**:
Summon the **Grand Marshal General** and **Commanding Army General** to swiftly arrive at the altar,
following the talisman to seize the malevolent spirits and urgently deliver them to the body,
declaring their true name.
Swiftly, as the **Highest Sovereign of Jade Celestial Treasury (高上神霄真王)** commands!"*

**Method:**
Pinch the **Chenwen (辰文)**, gather the **North Star qi (正北炁)**, and visualize its arrival.
Then gather the **Jade Celestial Treasury qi (神霄炁)** and blow it onto the head.
If attached, recite again.
If not yet attached, recite the spell to urge it forward.
*"By the decree of **Jade Celestial Treasury (神霄玉清)**:
I solemnly summon the **Certain General of Jade Celestial Treasury Palace (玉清神霄王府某将)**,
following the talisman’s decree, to urgently drive away the malevolent spirits and bind them to the body.
Swiftly! (疾疾)."*

**Method:**
Pinch the upper joint of the second finger, gather the **root qi (本炁)**, and visualize the two generals standing at either side.

**Binding with Shackles and Kai (缚枷栲):**
Write a **Black Talisman of Fate (历黑符)** in accordance with the method, gather the qi as prescribed, and invoke [specific matter].
Burn it beneath the afflicted person’s feet—this is most effective.

**According to the Method (照法):**
Command a young boy to stand at the teacher’s right, close his eyes, and use the **Monting of the Soul Spell (蒙魂咒):**
*"Flying soul, flying soul, urgently descend at the crown!
Living soul, living soul, urgently exit the crown!
Swiftly! (疾疾)."*

**Method:**
Recite the spell three times.
With the left hand, pinch **Hai to Mao (亥至卯)**, gather the **Jade Celestial Treasury qi (神霄炁)**, and blow it beneath the feet, burning a talisman of one’s life destiny.
Next, recite the **Opening of Light to Drive Ghosts (开光驱鬼)**.

**Spell:**
*"Jade Celestial Treasury Soldiers (神霄天丁), Soul Official Generals (灵官将军),
urgently drive away the resentful spirits—
if they manifest before the afflicted, bind them to the body.
Swiftly! (疾疾)."*

**Method:**
Recite the spell three times, pinch the **Chenwen (辰文)** with the left hand, gather the **Southeast qi (东南炁)**, and blow it three times, ordering the boy to exhale the qi and blow it.
Then, open his eyes.

*"Jade Celestial Treasury Soldiers (神霄天丁), Soul Official Generals (灵官将军),
urgently drive away the resentful spirits as though into water—
into water!
As though into fire—
into fire!
Manifest their form!"*

**Method of Transferring and Subduing [Evil Spirits]**
If a child cannot speak, command the wet nurse to act in their stead.
Have a close relative face the afflicted and exhale *qi* three times.
The master shall use the **Celestial Soldier Seal (天丁印)** with the right hand, pointing the middle finger at empty space, and traverse a **Black Talisman (黑符)** once.

Recite the following spell while holding the **Golden Spear Seal (金枪印)** with the left hand, pointing at the patient and loudly summoning:
*"Hail, Black General (号黑), Hail, Historic Black General (历黑)!*
*Swiftly obey my command and descend to transfer the affliction!*
*Clad in golden armor, with a face of crimson-purple hue,*
*Wielding an axe, riding upon black clouds.*
*Soon, black *qi* shall fill the space before you.*

**Spell:**
*"Celestial Primordial Treasure Scroll (天元宝箓),*
*Great Transformation of the Great Jia (太甲易形).*
*Hail, Black! Hail, Historic Black!*
*Swiftly follow my decree,*
*Transfer the malevolence and descend as spirit!*
*By the edict of the True King,*
*I command you to ascend and attach to the body—*
*No delay shall be permitted!*
*Swiftly! Hail, Black! Hail, Historic Black—*
*Two Great Generals!*
*Or dispatch the shrouding ghost-spirits!*
*Burn this talisman to ash and ingest it.*
*Also inscribe the summoning and dispatch—*
*Most wondrous!*
*Visualize the two generals before you,*
*Black clouds shrouding yourself or the ghost-spirits.*
*But think upon this often—*
*Most wondrous!*
*Inscribe the talisman and recite this spell.*

**Summoning Spell for Thunder-Clap Black General (召霹雳号黑大将军咒):**
*Pure Water True Essence, the Black Sovereign descends!*
*The Celestial Talisman, a keen blade,*
*Its might subdues all spirits.*
*Demons bow in submission,*
*All malevolence vanishes!*
*Swiftly, as the Highest Celestial Jade Purity True King’s decree!*
*Talisman Form:*
*By this method, gather Southeast *qi* and visualize*
*The Black General, Money the Flying Hero (钱雄飞),*
*Short-faced, crimson-purple, with a great mouth,*
*Brandishing a sword-whip,*
*And exhale it.*
*When the afflicted sees this,*
*The sky darkens, the earth dims—*
*No longer distinguishing man from ghost, day from night!*
*Recite the decree-spell:*
*Within the Celestial Court of the Jade Purity,*
*Inner and outer prisons, dragon circles,*
*Devouring poison, beheading malevolent ghosts,*
*Wailing in dispersion—*
*Black Historic clouds traverse the netherworlds.*
*The Black General’s envoy,*
*Swiftly descending, darkening heaven and earth,*
*Sealing the ground in blackness.*
*The monstrous dragon loses its luster,*
*The demonic loses sight.*
*Upon arrival at my altar,*
*The fire-bell tolls urgently!*
*Swiftly, as the Highest Celestial Jade Purity True King’s decree for salvation!*
*Thunder-Fire Historic Black General Talisman (雷火历黑大将军符):*
*By edict, summon Hail Black, Historic Black,*
*With thunderous might!*
*By the Han Official’s decree,*
*Descend swiftly, descend urgently,*
*Hasten to the Ninth Heaven!*
*Yang crystallizes, yin congeals,*
*The heavens and earth grow dark and murky.*
*First shroud brings spirit-fog,*
*Second shroud brings ghostly confusion!*
*Swiftly, as the Highest Celestial Jade Purity True King’s decree!*
*By this method, inscribe the Thunder-Fire Historic Black Talisman*
*Using bound yang peachwood,*
*Two *cun* long, two *cun* and six *fen* wide.*
*Assume the Spirit-Step *Gang* formation,*
*Gather Thunder-Fire *qi*,*
*And exhale while inscribing.*
*When finished, decree it with the spell*
*And place it in the central courtyard.*
*Ghosts, seeing the thunder-fire and claps,*
*Shall flee a thousand *li*,*
*Never to return with ill intent!*
*Another talisman,*
*Black ink on blue paper,*
*Worn as an amulet.*
*Burn it when needed—*
*Then the black *qi* shall vanish!*
*Ingest it to resolve vomiting,*
*To treat witchcraft,*
*And expel a dead fetus.*
*Its spirit:*
*Face crimson-purple, grotesque,*
*Wielding a great axe,*
*Riding a black *lei* [dark vehicle].*

**End of the Third Volume of the Purple-Written Great Law of the Highest Celestial Jade Purity True King**
**Fourth Volume of the Purple-Written Great Law of the Highest Celestial Jade Purity True King**

**Chapter on Thunder Scriptures – Self-Employed Rituals**
*Summoning the Twenty-One Generals’ Spell*

To the **Divine Thunder Hall of the Celestial Jade Purity True King**,
The **Supreme Sovereign of Thunder and Lightning**—

Form the **transformative *qi* of the Nine Suns** into script.
Above, command the **Thunder Generals**;
Below, subdue the **officers and soldiers**.

No hidden realm shall resist,
No spirit dare disobey.
Drive forth thunder, chase lightning—
Command all spirits in unison.

Riding a **ten-thousand-vehicle chariot**,
Following the **Celestial Officer Ding**.
The **Thunder Commander of Jade Purity**,
With **left and right generals** in attendance.

The **Fire Boar and Black Hound**—
Four **Sacred Envoys**—
Track dragons, seize demons,
Descend upon summons.

I, by decree of the **Highest Celestial Jade Purity True King**,
Summon **General [Name]**.
*Swiftly, as the Law commands!*

---
**Right Ritual:**
Left hand traces the **Chen Formation**, drawing **Xun *qi***, facing the **Xun direction** to summon.

Pursue and capture **General Yan Qing of the Eight Directions**, with **one hundred twenty officers** bearing swords.
**Teng Qi**, the **Ghost-Driving General of the Southern Ridge of Taiwei in the Nine Heavens**, obeys.

---

Trace the **Zi Formation**, face **Xun**, draw *qi*, inscribe the talisman.
Burn it before the afflicted or within the **Law Hall**.

Alternatively, invoke the **Spirit-General**—
**Crimson robe, wide golden armor, Celestial Officer’s cap**,
Riding **five-colored clouds** to descend.

**Invocation:**
*"By decree of the Jade Purity True King,*
*I summon **General Yan Qing of the Eight Directions**,
To swiftly seize and bind the malevolent ghost,*
*Transfer it to the afflicted body,*
*Reveal its true name.*
*Swiftly!"*

**The Twenty-One Thunder Scriptures of the East**

These are the alternate names of the **Twenty-One Qi Lords of the Eastern Long-Life, Great Vitality Sovereign**. If one suffers from prolonged illness and unrest, burn incense, recite the spell, and inscribe it. The *qi* and the **decision** are both of the **Xun** orientation.

**Spell:**
*"Eastern Thunder Spirit, swift in motion,*
Cast fire, strike the drum—enter my talisman.
Save and protect all living beings,
Swiftly, swiftly—no delay permitted.
Swiftly, as decreed by the Highest **God of Celestial Purity, True King** of **Divine Highness**.*

**Summoning the Nine-Heaven Thunder Scripture General:**
*'Divine General of **Spiritual Highness**, spirit of the abyss,
**Southern Dipper Fire Official**, **Northern Pole General**,
**Nine-Heaven Powerful Warrior**, heed my summons.
Take your true form—seize and behead malevolent spirits.
Swiftly descend, execute the ghosts.
Search and capture malevolent spirits, sever the path of death.
Swiftly summon, swiftly seize—malevolent ghosts submit.
**Conduct investigation, examine, restrain, and apprehend.**
Bind with ropes and chains, act as I command.
If not obeyed at once, the guilt lies with you.
Swiftly, as decreed by the Highest **God of Celestial Purity, True King** of **Divine Highness**."*

**Method:**
With the left hand, pinch the **Great God’s Decision** at the base of the middle finger’s nail.
With the right hand, pinch the **Commander’s Decision**.
Then dispatch it.

**Instruction:**
This is the **Nine-Heaven Thunder Scripture**, which rescues the living and guides the dead, each with its own proclamation. For all matters, verify accordingly.

If a child suffers from **convulsions**, write in cinnabar on yellow paper, form into a pill, and swallow it.
For **parasitic infestations and venomous harm**, decoct **ghost plant** in water and swallow it.
Submit a **petition to the Underworld authorities**, burn it for dissolution, and immediately dispel misfortune. Decree:
*"Inscribe the talisman and deliver it to the local **City and Earth Deities**—this too can refine and elevate one to transcendence. Those burdened by worldly sins and calamities, wearing it, shall all be freed."*

**Urgent as the Highest God of Celestial Purity’s decree.**

「Third, **Ding Wenyi**. Fourth, **Ding Wenkuang**.
Assist me in seizing ghosts and binding spirits—go swiftly, do not slack in your duty.
**Hurry!**
Commanded to perform as prescribed.

The ritual procedure states: Whenever this method is enacted, declare and petition the **Celestial Pivot of the Northern Pole, Northern Dipper Heavenly Axis Office** (北极北斗天枢院), requesting the aforementioned **Four Marshal Envoys**. Follow the ritual to worship the **Sun**, using **Regap Day** (庚申), **Jiazi Day** (甲子), **Northern Dipper Descent Day** (北斗下降日), **Triple-Seven Day** (三七日), and **Triple-Element Day** (三元日). Take the **Gang Qi** (罡炁), and blow it over the patient’s head.

For the secondary ritual, always use **Chen Day** (辰日). Employ four divided **gold coins** (金钱) and **tea-leaves** (荼) in four cups. During the ritual, recite the names of the **Four Divine Generals** (前四神将) once.

Then recite the **incantation**:
*"O Sun of the Midday, your power is steadfast—uphold the **Dharma** with rectitude.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the **Celestial Mandate** decrees."*
Recite this **incantation** seven times, then wait a moment, burn the coins, and pour the tea-leaves. Again, silently recite the **incantation**:
*"Heavenly Yang is verdant, Earth’s response is numinous.
**Four Marshal Envoys**, seize ghosts and gods.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the **Celestial Mandate** decrees."*
With your left hand, hold the *Dough Decision* (卯文) and the *Fighting Mouth Talisman* (斗诀), and blow the **Qi** into the altar.

The **Incantation for Seizing Ghosts with Dates** (咒枣捉鬼法):
*"O **Divine Spirit of Heaven’s Hue** (天色神), swiftly seize the wronged spirits.
O **Divine Spirit of Earth’s Hue** (地色神), swiftly seize those clinging to the patient’s illness."*
First, recite the **incantation** and blow it upon the dates, commanding the patient to eat them, while saying aloud: *"Seize below!"* (捉下).
Then inquire in sequence the names of the spirits.
Another method...」

**"The Mighty Marshal Tian Ding’s Directing Method"**

*"Great Power Marshal Tian Ding, ruling the sun’s circle.
Great Power Marshal Tian Ding, ruling the moon’s square.
Descend to the lower realm, swiftly, swiftly.
Drive away malevolent sickness, swiftly make it vanish.
Concentrate the **Gang-qi** and the **Talisman**—
**Twelve Marshal Envoys’ Distant Seizing Method**—

Swiftly summon the **Six Ding Gods**, the **Six Jia** most spiritually attuned.
I, bearing the **Northern Emperor’s Mandate**, command you to swiftly pursue the soul.
Seize and bind the malevolent ghosts; when they enter the body, reveal their names.
First, question the one who lodged the complaint—no need for personal attendance.
Merely visualize the patient, then declare their dwelling place.
Recite the method and draw in the **qi**, then blow it upon the complainant.
After swallowing, use your left hand for the **Tian Ding Talisman**, your right for the **Sword Talisman**.
Draw in the directional **qi** again and blow it onto the paper.
Ask: *Is the paper heavy?*
If heavy, the malevolent spirit has attached itself.
Next, the **Dharma Master** shall use the **Gaiters of Constraint** and the **Root Talisman**—no leniency allowed.
After questioning the crime, deliver the guilty to their proper authority.

**Another Method:**
Reverently summon the **Gang Gods**, swiftly descending their true spirits.
Distant seizing of wronged souls and ghosts—when they attach, reveal their names.
Swiftly.
I bear the **Supreme Lord’s Edict**, commanding the **Jiao Que Marshal**, the **Gang Marshal**—permission granted.
The **Eight Directions’ Malevolent Marshals** stand ready.
The **Great Power Marshal Tian Ding** beheads the Ghost Marshal—**Zhang Da**.
The **Great Power Marshal Tian Ding** shackles the Ghost Marshal—**Lian Chongdao**.
The **Great Power Marshal Tian Ding** binds the Ghost Marshal—**Guo Shun**.
**Nine-Heaven Cloud Path Pursuit and Seizing Method**—

I call upon the **Nine-Heaven Cloud Path Pursuit Marshals**: **An Shouxin**, **Li Pingquan**, **Xing Zhongli**, **Guo Zisheng**.
I bear the **Northern Emperor’s Edict**, convening the household gods to pursue the malevolent ghosts.
You must go swiftly and return swiftly.
Swiftly.
Pinch the **Great Killing Talisman** and recite the incantation, drawing **qi** from the north, visualizing the four marshals driving them in.

**Again**, I call upon the **Nine-Heaven Cloud Path Supreme Lord’s Pure and One Functionary**: **Zhai Shining**, **Jiang Juyuan**, **Zhao Ziyu**.
According to the **Upper Clarity’s Edict of Descent**, search and seize the malevolent spirits, directing them to the patient’s body.
Swiftly.
The **Qi Talisman** follows as before."*

**The Four Cardinal Directions Seizing Method of Heaven’s Bolt and Earth’s Axis**

Binding and seizing malevolent ghosts with shackles and fetters.

**The Supreme Eight Poisons Killing Ghosts Red-Staff Pill**

For **ghost arrows**, use:
**Feathers, stone, *gǔpú*, and *zhúchú* (washing with **soapberry**),
**Inverted *húliú* (ghost urtica), *yùmǎo* (Chinese cantharides), and *zhēngshí* (realgar)**—
Each **one liang**,
**Cinnabar and female sulfur**—each **one fen**.

Grind into fine powder, mix with **alcohol paste**, and form into pills the size of **willow seeds**.
Recite the incantation: *"*...*"*

**Supreme Eight Poisons Killing Ghosts Red-Staff Pill (Continued)**

Recite:
*"Engrave upon the Ming River Marshal, transmit through the Marshal.
Little Ji Victory First, Supreme Heavenly Gang.
Supreme Charged Functionary, Great Auspicious Spirit Sovereign.
Recite this incantation three times, then invoke Tianpeng’s Glare seven times, blowing into the medicine with sincere devotion and careful preparation.
Next, summon the Twelve Monthly Generals, pinch the Great Killing Sigil, and blow upon the elixir.
When fully formed, place in a purified chamber.
If someone requests the elixir, inquire about their ailment.
If malevolent spirits haunt the dwelling, manifesting shadows, or if foul, noxious *qi* assails the person, or if epidemic pestilential *qi* lingers within—burn one pill in the censer.
To dispel malevolent poisons and disperse illness, proceed as follows:

For **heart ailments**, take one pill, chew finely, and swallow with ginseng decoction.
**Heart Incantation (Wuwen):**
*"Yuewen Fire Star Lord, I command you to restore the heart and return the *qi*!
Swiftly, as the law decrees!"*

For **liver ailments**, take one pill, chew finely, and swallow with ginseng decoction.
**Liver Incantation (Maowen):**
*"Sui Virtue Wood Star Lord, I command you to restore the liver and return the *qi*!
Swiftly, as the law decrees!"*

For **spleen ailments**, take one pill, chew finely, and swallow with ginseng decoction.
**Spleen Incantation (Dashawen):**
*"Earth Virtue Zhen Star Lord, I command you to restore the spleen and return the *qi*!
Swiftly, as the law decrees!"*

For **lung ailments**, take one pill, chew finely, and swallow with ginseng decoction.
**Lung Incantation (Youwen):**
*"Tai Bai Jin Host Lord, I command you to restore the lungs and return the *qi*!
Swiftly, as the law decrees!"*

For **kidney ailments**, take one pill, chew finely, and swallow with ginseng decoction.
**Kidney Incantation (Ziwen):**
*"Water Virtue Chen Star Lord, I command you to restore the kidneys and return the *qi*!
Swiftly, as the law decrees!"*

Use these divine incantations according to the affected organ.
If inverted malevolent ghosts persist, employ the following incantation:
*"The Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper, the Monthly Generals descend.
The Twenty-Eight Constellations, seize and bind by name.
Swiftly, as the law decrees!"*

Recite this once, form the **Fighter’s Seal** with the left hand, face north to gather *qi*, and blow upon the elixir.
Then, invoke the **Child-Midday Dipper**, sending it into the medicine—use as before.*

**Supreme Numinous Treasure True Person’s Method for Fumigating Malevolence and Healing Illness**

**Ingredients:**
Ghost arrows, *gǔpú* (knotty vine), earth dragon, *fúshen* (aconite root), white *fúlíng* (poria), *rúxiāng* (frankincense), *zhōnghuáng* (realgar)—each **half a liang**.
Mugwort—**three liang**.

The above are the **major ingredients** (each half a liang).
The **minor ingredients**—each...

**Supreme Numinous Treasure True Person’s Method for Fumigating Malevolence and Healing Illness (continued)**

One *qián* [⅛ *liang*]. Pound and sift into a fine powder, then mix with mugwort. When using, burn some sacred mugwort in an incense burner to produce smoke—direct it toward the affected **acupuncture point**, and the pain will naturally subside. For wheezing, coughing, or asthma, inhale the smoke three or four times, and recovery will be immediate. For deafness, fumigate the ears with the smoke, and the condition will be cured. Each application requires a small dose; holding the smoke in the mouth ensures all ailments are soothed.

**End of Volume Four of the *Highest God of Celestial Serenity’s Purple Scripture Great Law***

**Volume Five: Refining the True and Verifying the Immortal**

**Lord Khan, the Paternal Uncle, instructs those aspiring to Daoist cultivation:**

The **True King**, commissioned by Heaven, governs the central realm.
The **Jade Emperor** descends his spirit, harmonizing the flourishing of Dao.
He opens the **seven-stage secret talismans**, arranging the **three-grade forbidden scriptures**.
His might governs the ten thousand heavens; his merit surpasses all ranks.

The transmitted Law has its own cultivation—its functions are not easily exhausted.

The **Highest Celestial Serenity Secret Talismans** are indeed the **Mystic Essence of the Primordial Origin**, the ultimate aspiration of all saints.
In the **Kaihuang era**, they were bestowed from the **Eastern Reserve Palace**.
Established across countless kalpas, they were never transmitted to lowly disciples.
Sealed with **purple jade**, hidden in the **uppermost green pavilion**.
Greatly preserving the order of Heaven and Earth, subtly summoning the spirits—
All true officials follow this wondrous model.

Now, as Heaven’s auspicious age dawns and the age of High Perfection arrives,
Pitying the common folk lost in heterodox practices,
The **Highest Celestial Serenity** reveals its celestial secrets,
To restore the vast source of the Great Teaching.
For every thought of compassion, countless beings are liberated.
Having received this precious instruction,
One must strive to emulate pure cultivation.

Ascend the **Celestial Serenity Unity Stage**,
Transcend the **Green Silk Great Thousand-Worlds**.
Pursue your lofty resolve—do not slacken your initial resolve.
Believe, receive, and practice—thus attaining divine response.

Moreover, the **Three Officials** hold the pen in judgment,
The **Five Sovereigns** wield the talismans—
Recording virtue and vice without error,
Chronicling deeds and misdeeds without omission.
Whoever dares transgress shall face no pardon from the Great Law.
This proclamation extends infinitely—all must strive with diligence.

**The Seven-Stage Rectification of Offices and Ranks for the Celestial Serenity Preservation-of-Immortal Secret Talismans** is now conferred.

Those who have **not yet received the *Nine-Grade Scripture-Talismans of the Most High*** are called **White Tablet disciples**, and should be addressed as **Celestial Serenity Initial True Disciples**.

Those who have **received the *Seven Elements Eternal Youth Talismans of the Most High*** are called **Celestial Serenity Peace-Assisting Transformation Disciples**.

Those who have received the **Northern Emperor’s Subduing-Demons Abyssal Ascension Talismans** are called **Highest Celestial Serenity Peace-Assisting Transformation Disciples**.

Those who have received the **One-Alliance, Three-Five, Nine-Districts Functional Talismans** are called **Highest Celestial Serenity Peace-Assisting Transformation Law-Talisman Bearers**.

Those who have received the **Purple Void Yang Light Talismans** and the **Celestial Serenity Lower-Grade Scripture-Talismans** shall be addressed as **Highest Celestial Serenity Primordial Transformation Masters of Mysterious and Wondrous Origin**. If incomplete, they may be called simply the **Ten-Character Title-Bearers** of the preceding rank.

Those who have received the **Soul Treasures Central Alliance Law-Talismans** shall be addressed as **Highest Celestial Serenity Cavernous Transformation Masters of Preservation and Salvation, Illuminated and Harmonious Purple Light Lords**. The **Sixteen-Character Title** marks the second stage; if incomplete, they may be called **Masters of Mysterious and Wondrous Origin**.

Those who have received the **Upper Clarity Great Cavern Talismans** shall be addressed as **Highest Celestial Serenity Jade Heaven Cavernous Landscape Masters of Void Primordial Unification**. As the first stage, if incomplete, they may be called **Celestial Serenity Cavernous Landscape Masters of Void Primordial Truth**.

For the **Highest Celestial Serenity Great Dao**, one must have received the Great Cavern Talismans and shall be addressed as **Master [Surname] of [Mountain Name], [Qi]-True Person**.

The ranks and titles for the **Celestial Serenity Three Caverns and Four Auxiliaries** are fully recorded hereafter.

All initial-stage disciples and those who have received the Talismans must **devote their hearts to cultivation**, avoiding reckless transgression of ranks, lest **True Qi be disordered** and **spiritual clarity obscured**. The **Three Officials** will then **seize their fate**, and the **Nine Ancestors** will **suffer retribution**. Be cautious, and **eternally preserve the Dao-True**.

- **Pale Yellow Daoist Robe**, **azure-green three-hued cloud-patterned** silk.
- **Pale Yellow Inner Garment**, **azure-green three-hued cloud-patterned** silk.
- **Pale Yellow Skirt** of five panels and four flaps, **three-hued cloud-patterned**.
- **Sandalwood Tablet**, **white jade pendant**, **crimson footwear**.

**Fifth Stage Robes:**
- **Seven Stars Harmonious Crown**, **ivory hairpin**.
- **Pale Yellow Outer Garment** of twelve panels, **black-green three-hued cloud-patterned** silk.

**Sixth Stage Robes:**
- **Pale Yellow Daoist Robe**, **black-green two-hued cloud-patterned** silk.
- **Pale Yellow Inner Garment**, **black-green two-hued cloud-patterned** silk.

- **Pale Yellow Daoist Robe**, **Pale Yellow Inner Garment**, **Pale Yellow Skirt**.

**Regarding the Supreme First Stage Robes:**
Those who receive transmission from the Celestial Mastery and are ordained on the altar to uphold the sacred registers—alongside the secret scriptures of the Celestial Mastery—wear the **emerald crown, crimson robe, red footwear, and sandalwood tablet**. This is the sacred learning of the **Jade Purity Palace of the Celestial Mastery**, where celestial kindred attain virtue and ascend to the Dao.

Those who receive the affairs of the **Jade Purity** are granted the robes and crowns.

The **Three Caverns and Four Auxiliaries** preserved in the Celestial Mastery’s inner treasury include anciently transmitted texts, some of which are widely seen in the world. There are also **one thousand two hundred volumes of forbidden, secret scriptures** that have never been transmitted across kalpas, divided into **six grades and twelve categories**, arranged into **upper, middle, and lower stages**, stored in the **Eastern and Western Flowery Platforms**. Since the era of **Great Peace and Auspicious Beginnings**—from the years **Renchen and Gengzi** onward—they shall gradually be revealed.

Those who master **one complete upper scripture** shall be called **Celestial Mastery Jade-Heaven Cavern-Scene Master, the True Person of Universal Transformation**. Upon attaining the Dao, they shall hold the rank of **Supreme Chancellor and True Marshal of the Jade Palace**.

Those who master **one complete middle scripture** shall be called **Celestial Mastery Cavern-Transformation Master, the True Person of Preservation and Illumination**. Upon attaining the Dao, they shall hold the ranks of **Celestial Officials and Marshals of the Eastern and Western Platforms**.

Those who master **one complete lower scripture** shall be called **Celestial Mastery Primordial-Transformation Master, the True Person of Spiritual Mystery and Original Unity**. Upon attaining the Dao, they shall hold the ranks of **Celestial Officials and True Governors of the Eastern and Western Platforms**.

Their ritual robes are:
- **Cloud-Patterned Jade Crown of the Jade Purity**.
- **Purple Spirit and Emerald Jade Hairpin**.
- **Thirty-six-panel Robe of Flying Clouds and Verdant Luminosity**.
- **Crimson-Brown Outer Garment with Yellow Skirt of Flying Azure**.
- **Jade-Sun Footwear**.
- **Spiritual Cavern Emerald Jade Tablet**.
- **Triple-Qi Radiant Jade Pendant**.
- **Sword of Resplendent Robe and Magic-Dispelling Brilliance**, three *chi* six *cun* long.
- **Platform of the Nine Qi**.

If, among the three stages, one attains **upper, middle, or lower scriptures** but lacks the complete volumes, or if they possess **one or two scriptures of the Three Caverns in the mortal world**, they shall be called **Celestial Mastery Great Peace Auxiliary-Transformation Disciples**. Upon attaining the Dao, they shall hold the rank of **Celestial True Persons**, or serve as **Celestial Officials under the Celestial Mastery’s dispersed ranks**. Yet they cannot ascend to the noble station of the **High Celestial Jade Palace**, nor wield authority over the **Supreme Celestial Bureau**.

Their ritual robes are:
- **Pure Jade Three-Flowered Crown** (emerald or triple-pure).
- **Purple Essence and Water Jade Hairpin**.
- **Thirty-six-panel Robe of Pure Purple**.
- **Emerald-Brown Outer Garment with Yellow Skirt**.
- **Azure-Trimmed Skirt**.
- **Yellow Flower Jade Tablet**.
- **Red Footwear and Jade Pendant**.
- **Sword of Five-Eight Elixir Precision**, three *chi* two *cun* long.
- **Platform of the Three Lights and Eight Measures**.

If one receives the scriptures and completes all three stages, attaining the Dao, they shall ascend to the rank of **High Sovereign Daoist Lord of the Three Heavens**, equal to the saints.

Unless they present petitions and registers to the **True Ones**, conducting rituals in accordance with the sacred scriptures, they may not arbitrarily don these ritual robes. Inspecting officials shall verify their attainment.

**Celestial Mastery Supplementary Official Ranks:**

Those who receive the Celestial Mastery’s teachings begin as **Highest Celestial Mastery Great Peace Auxiliary-Transformation Officials**, charged with implementing the Celestial Mastery’s great law and assisting in the **Scripture Bureau’s rightful affairs**.

If, within one year, they accumulate **140 merits of conduct, virtue, and righteousness**, they may petition the **Celestial Mastery’s Heavenly Bureau** for promotion to **Celestial Official ranks**.

Those who govern the **Eight Offices** shall not exceed the **Celestial Mastery’s ranks**, nor surpass the **Celestial Realm**. They may attain **Celestial Official ranks**, governing mortal affairs as if ruling the world from heaven. Below, they correspond to **Functionary Officials**; above, they align with **Heaven’s Will**. This is the **Celestial Rank**, entering the **Daoist Lineage**, transcending mortality to become saints.

To govern the **Heavenly Bureau** is not to be exceeded—offenses are grave.

Those who receive the **Three Caverns’ scriptures and registers**, ascending to the rank of **Celestial Mastery True Officials**, follow the same regulations as **Official Disciples**, managing **clerical duties** rather than **celestial appointments**.

Those who have received the **Orthodox One’s registers** and hold **nine ranks of Celestial Officials**—as **Officials, Disciples, or True Officials**—enter the **nine grades of initial rank**.

For those above the **Four Auxiliaries**, **360 merits** are required. Each act of saving a person, delivering a person, or performing a great **virtue/power** deed for a living being counts as merit.

When advancing an official grade, one must submit a petition to the **Supreme Sovereign** without omission. If there is a fault, one must immediately confess and offset the merit against the fault.

**The Daoist Officials** must each day burn the **Talisman of Official Rank** to advance one grade. During their term of duty, they command **ten million spirit-soldiers and officials**. If they do not burn the talisman, the spirits will consume it themselves, but they will still have Daoist Officials to assist them.

**Invocation of the Daoist Officials’ Department Talisman:**
*"High in the heavens, the Jade Pure Palace reigns supreme.
The Celestial Treasure of the Three **Qi** governs the Three **Provincial Ministries** of the **Pivot**.
Before the **Supreme Sovereign**, the Heavenly Tribunal and Palace of **Life Decrees** presides.
Each has its appointed duty, aiding the **Jade Laws** below.
Ranked by grade and stationed in their places, the Daoist Officials reside.
At the call, they descend in obedience; at the **Heavenly Seal**, they align.
The lofty decree of the **Heavenly Highness** is revered—
I humbly petition the **Certain Official**,
to act in accordance with the **Laws** and fulfill their command."*

**Invocation of the Daoist Officials’ General Talisman:**
*"The **Right Mysterious Golden Gate Talisman**—
The **Mystic Pass** of the **Supreme Sovereign**,
The **Supreme Decree** to the **Heavenly Demon**,
The **Supreme Decree** to the **Earthly Demon**,
The **Supreme Decree** to the **Ghostly Demon**,

The **Supreme Decree** to the **Beastly Demon** of the **Red Sky Demon King**,
The **Supreme Decree** to the **Mountain-Reversing Demon** of the **White Sky Demon King**,
The **Supreme Decree** to the **Homeless Demon** of the **Black Sky Demon King**,
The **Supreme Decree** to the **Force-Bearing Demon** of the **Yellow Sky Demon King**,
The **Supreme Decree** to the **Great Demon Lord of the Six Abysses of the **Pangdu** Region**,
The **Supreme Decree** to the **Ten Million Demons** to obey and act.
The **Heavenly Officials** lead the way and sever the **Ghostly Traces**.
The **Thirty-Six Heavenly Gods’ Talisman**—
With **flying spears and drifting halberds**, they strike down offenders.
The **Great Abyssal Ghost-Demons** dare not charge forward.
By **wind, thunder, and fire**, they shatter the ghosts.
At the command, they lead the way—when the talisman arrives, they act.
*Swiftly, as the **Highest Heavenly Sovereign** commands.*
This talisman is inscribed with the **hourly stem and branch**, using the **perverse **Qi****, written in **cinnabar** on **yellow paper**.
It is drawn with a **barrier-child** to command the **Ghostly Demon** to lead the way and suppress the ghosts.
Within the talisman are the **spirit-officials, merit-recorders, and talisman-bearers**,
who petition the **Suffering Spirits** to submit their words.
The **Heavenly Tribunal’s Spirit-Generals** will then act in their stead.
Before the **spirit-official’s** arrival, the **spirit-talisman-bearers** will first reach the afflicted’s home,
and without waiting for the master, they will bind the ghosts below.
The master arrives, and the bonds are severed and the ghosts dispatched.

Another method: burn the talisman and blow its ashes away—
the ghosts will be seized immediately.
For distant cases, inscribe the **hourly stem and branch**,
blow the talisman’s ashes, and point with a sword—
the malevolence will depart ten thousand *li* away.

For **mountain goblins, Five Paths spirits, and malevolent ghosts** that cannot be treated,
or when one is in a **mad, frenzied state**,
use **vinegar and charcoal** to burn the talisman and fumigate them.
The talisman must be inscribed with the **Five Emperors’ Great Demon King Spell**,
and the **Demon-Subduing Mystic Pass Spell** must be recited in secret.

The **Twelve Jade Boys** of **five-colored embroidered robes**—
