**The Jade Boys’ Method for Commanding and Employing Ten Thousand Spirits:**
The **Twelve Jade Boys** above, according to the **Laws**, are visualized in their **five-colored embroidered robes**.
In spring, the **three months**, one boy governs the **Five Lords** for each month.
In summer, autumn, and winter, the **three months** each, one boy governs the **Five Lords** for each month.
During this month, the talisman is inscribed and burned to summon them.
The **Jade Boys** attend, guard, command, and present themselves before the **True One**.

When summoning them, one must also **visualize the General Spell**, the **perverse **Qi****, and inscribe it in **cinnabar**.
For all who wish to employ them, on each **three-nines day** (i.e., 27th day of each lunar month),
prepare **five bowls** of **date wine, glutinous rice milk, and honeyed rice gruel**,
along with **fragrant flowers**.
After calling the **Jade Boy**, one may employ them.

**The Jade Boy’s Method for Seizing Ghosts:**
The **Jade Boy** (not a female spirit) closes their eyes,
absorbs the **ghostly **Qi****,
and blows out a breath.
In darkness, they call the names of the **Three Souls**,
and within, they point to the **Superintendent Spell** and tightly **visualize it**.
They blow out a **black breath**.
They **visualize the Jade Pure Palace Spell** and recite the spell three times.
The **Jade Boy** will then appear,
and one may petition the **Jade Boys** of the **direct day** to come,
using them as one pleases.

**The Jade Boy’s Method for Invoking the Nine Souls of the Jade Maiden:**

The **Jade Boy** recites the spell aloud,
invoking **Yingsu True Lord** (to compel spirits to manifest in form).
Again, he **visualizes the spell in his heart**,
summoning the **Green Boy** to obey his command,
and descend with **imperial edicts** to his servant.
Swiftly, he aids his servant in divining humans and objects,
and in **communing with spirits** to receive their responses.

**The Ritual for the Jade Maiden:**
On **Jiazi** or **Gengshen nights** (i.e., nights of the 1st Heavenly Stem or 7th Earthly Branch),
recite the **Law Spell** over water and drink it.
To invoke the **Jade Maiden’s Division**, he earnestly requests the **gentle and yielding Qi**,
the **Nine Souls of the Jade Maiden**, whose name is **Jade Maiden**.
She wears **phoenix-patterned robes and light embroidered skirts**,
by the **True King’s command**, summoned to the **Spirit Court**.
Swiftly, as the **Jade Pure Edict** commands.
**Hypograph the spell** with **perverse Qi**,
and write it down.

The **Jade Maiden’s Five Viscounts** hold:
- **A banner** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A scepter** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **An axe** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A noose** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A spear** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A fan** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A mirror** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **Incense** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **Medicine** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A torch** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A bottle** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A sword** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A seal** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A talisman** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A register** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A ritual diagram** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A ribbon** with five-colored embroidered robes,
- **A jade tablet** with five-colored embroidered robes.

**The Invocation:**
The **Jade Maiden’s Five Viscounts** are called forward,
and the **Jade Maiden’s Five Viscounts** are blown upon.
The **Jade Maiden’s Five Viscounts** of **Jiazi**, **Jiaxi**, **Jia申**, **Jiawu**, **Jiachén**, **Jayin**,
**Dingmào**, **Dingsì**, **Dingwèi**, **Dingyǒu**, **Dinghài**, and **Dingchǒu** are summoned.

**The Jade Maiden’s Retention:**
According to the Law, retain her.
On **Jiazi** or **Gengshen nights**, recite the **Law Spell** over water and ingest it.
Each has their own duties—
for **offering incense**, **presenting petitions**, **submitting memorials**, or **conducting rites**,
summon them as needed, and they will naturally attend.
After seven days of **fasting and abstinence** (斋戒),
they will appear at once.
Do not gaze upon the **Jade Maiden** for too long.
In a year, there are **six Yang**, **six Yin**, **six Jia**, and **six Ding** (天干).
Each month is divided into **three decans** (旬),
allocating **six Jia** and **six Ding**.
Each decan has one person,
with **five hundred men** serving as the decan’s attendants and guards,
alongside the **Jade Boy**, coming to assist.

She may also be employed to **seize spirits and pursue souls**,
and to **foresee future auspiciousness or calamity**.
Summon her by name and employ her at will—
she will respond without fail.

**The Sixth Scroll of the Highest Dao/Way of the Jade Pure True King’s Purple Text**

**The Division of the Great General**

**The Supreme Invocation Spell:**

*"I obey the True King’s edicts,
the Jade Emperor’s golden talisman,
and establish this altar to inform the Heavens.
I model the Earth and mirror the Heavens,
and compel spirits to dispatch ghosts.
On my left, I bind the **Dragon Scripture’s** (龙文) power,
and on my right, I wear the **Jade Pure Celestial Edict’s** (玉律) authority.
With my mouth, I recite the **Jade Pure Feathered Edict** (玉清羽章),
and pay homage to the **Great Emperor** (大帝).

Below, I command the spirits of **mountains, rivers, lands, and seas**,
and above, I list the **True King’s** ministers and viscounts.
I chant the **Great Mysterious Dao/Way’s** (大洞玄机) essence—
once invoked, the **Nine Celestial Life Officials** (九天司命) respond,
twice invoked, the **Nine Celestial True Immortals** (九天真仙) appear.

I am the **Immortal Sovereign** (仙主),
the **Supreme Venerable Master** (太上丈人),
and the **Five-Peak Mountain King’s** (五岳王主) overseer.
My duty is received in my heart.
I can **call the winds and absorb the rains**,
and **drive the thunder to fury**.

The **Thunder Division** advances before me,
its might shaking the **peals of thunder** (霹雳),
and causing **mountains and peaks to collapse**.
The **Primordial Heaven’s Emperor** commands the **Four Cardinal Directions’** winds and fire,
and all **ten thousand spirits** under Heaven.
He also orders the **golden-armored officers** within the **registers**,
the **thunderous and fierce Heavenly Ding** (天丁),
to appear before the altar at once—
none may dare to defy his command.

Swiftly, as the **Highest Dao/Way of the Jade Pure True King’s Edict** decrees.

The **True King** says:
*"The **Spirit Treasury’s** Jade Scriptures,
the **Jade Palace’s** Sacred Texts,
each have their own duties and cases to oversee.
Every division has a master of **thirty thousand men**,
and each sends one down to descend.
**One hundred and twenty officials** descend to attend.
If there are matters to be addressed,
summon and question them—
one must first purify the body and mind.
If one reveals the **Heaven’s secrets** (天机),
he will die and fall into **Tangdu Hell** (酆都),
and be pardoned in **ten thousand kalpas** (万劫) not."*

---

The **Temporal Edict** (辰文) is **perverse qi** (巽炁).
The **General of Qi** (主炁大将军), the **Heavenly Spirit Official** (天神灵官) overseeing the **Spirit Treasury’s Qi Registry** (神府炁候案主者), commands all **four seasons and the twenty-four qi** (四时二十四炁) in their **proper and inverted order** (逆顺之祥).

The **Edict of the Wood** (卯文), **the Rectified East Qi** (正东炁).
The **General of Rain** (主雨大将军), the **Heavenly Spirit Official** (天神灵官) overseeing the **Spirit Treasury’s Rain Registry** (神府行雨案主者), commands all **sacred assemblies of rain** (一切行雨圣众), and **relieves great droughts** (救大早泌).

From **Child to Ox** (子至丑), **the West-North Qi** (西北炁).
The **General of Slaying** (主杀大将军), the **Heavenly Spirit Official** (天神灵官) overseeing the **Spirit Treasury’s Punishment of Evil Registry** (神府伐恶案主者), commands all **ungrateful and rebellious acts of treachery** (不孝逆奸), **slaying evil and beheading malevolence** (杀邪斩凶). **Midday points to the upper text**, **drawing forth the lower nodes**, **the Temporal Qi** (辰炁).

The **General of Life** (主生大将军), the **Heavenly Spirit Official** (天神灵官) overseeing the **Spirit Treasury’s Life Registry** (神府掌生案主者), commands all **births and children** (一切生产小儿), **and predetermines the prosperity of descendants** (前定子孙昌运).

The **Edict of the Wood** (卯文), **the Perverse Qi** (巽炁).
The **General of Disease** (主病大将军), the **Heavenly Spirit Official** (天神灵官) overseeing the **Spirit Treasury’s Disease Registry** (神府灾病主者), governs all **spread of sickness and calamity** (一切疾病淹延患难).

The **General of Inspecting Evil** (检恶大将军), the **Heavenly Spirit Official** (天神灵官) **holding the ledger**, governs **all malevolent deeds**, **examining the records of accumulated sins** (检人所积恶罪之籍), **and must not recklessly employ them**.

The **General of Transformation** (变化大将军) and the **General of Release** (发放大将军) **specialize in dispatching the Spirit Treasury’s texts**.

The **General of Retribution** (对定大将军) **commands the rectification of sins and blessings**.

The **General of Severing Sickness** (断疰大将军) and the **General of Collecting Toxins** (收毒大将军) **attend to sores, toxins, itching, and pain**.

The **General of Severing Pestilence** (斩温大将军), the **General of Fire Bells** (火铃大将军), the **General of Returning Names** (回名大将军), the **General of Swiftness** (急速大将军), and the **General of Reversing Movement** (返行大将军) **all employ the Temporal Edict** (并掐辰文), **the Perverse Qi** (巽炁).

The **Generals above** (已上所主大将军), **each according to their intent**, inscribe **talismans** (符), **register the causes of afflictions** (下注事因), **recite the assembled divine incantations** (念集神咒), **and observe their appointed domains** (看所主).
When performing these rites, **do not let others know the slightest deviation**—once the **talismans are dispatched**, **divine efficacy will manifest**, and **none will fail to respond**.

The **Supreme Edict of the Highest Dao/Way of the Jade Pure True King** (高上左玄真卿曰) commands:
*"The **Soul-Catching Spirit Official Generals** (捉魂灵官将军), **up to the Barrier-Riding Generals** (至堠骑将军), **each has their appointed Heavenly Generals** (前有神将).
If **one invokes them to grant life** (注生), **extinguish fire** (救火), **sever epidemics** (断瘟), **behead malevolence** (斩邪), **punish evil** (伐恶), **demolish temples** (破庙), **interrogate and bind malevolent spirits** (考缚凶邪), **return names and register merits** (回名注功), **or transmit and recite swift commands** (传念急达)—
**all will respond without fail**.

To **collect wandering vital essence** (收精疰), **resolve misfortune** (解厄对), **rectify and dispatch** (定遣发), **ward off false transformations** (辟非变化), **restrain imprisoned spirits and demons** (禁囚鬼怪), **collect toxins and sever sickness** (收毒斩疰)—
**whatever is invoked will surely arrive**.

**One must first purify the heart and observe strict abstinence** (兆须浄心斋戒), **and before the altar, assemble the divine and summon** (临坛集神呼召), **only then will they respond**.

**Together they recite the incantation, invoke the talismans, and again recite the incantation to burn the talismans**—
**each general is summoned one by one**, and **they appear instantly**.

If **one seizes, binds, or interrogates**, **they will enter the mind and serve as commanded** (入意从役之), **each with their own domain**.

**Inscribe in red, affix in yellow**, and **burn over the afflicted person’s head**—
**while reciting the Supreme Incantation**, **blow the qi forth**.
If **one performs the method of driving and seizing**, **then take the North Qi** (便取北炁), **and blow it forth**.
The **method of driving and seizing** (驱捉法) **is to drive away malevolence**, **forcing it to dwell in the North**.

**Summon the Supreme Overseer and Commanding Generals with the incantation of the Jade Pure Heavenly Dao/Way’s Edict** (召总监统兵将咒 神霄玉清王劫):
*"Conjure the **Supreme Overseer General** (总监大将军) and the **Commanding General** (统兵大将军), swiftly arriving at **my altar** (一吾坛), **instantly appearing as the talismans decree** (随符立至).*
**Swiftly, as the Supreme Edict of the Highest Dao/Way of the Jade Pure True King** (急急如高上神霄玉清真王律令).

**Conjure the Supreme Overseer with the incantation of the Jade Pure Heavenly Dao/Way’s Edict** (召都正咒 神霄玉清劫令):
*"Reverently conjure a certain general of the **Jade Pure Spirit Treasury** (神霄玉府), swiftly arriving at **my altar** (吾坛), **following the talisman’s command** (随符所勑), **to treat this matter for me** (为吾治某事).*
**Swiftly, as the Supreme Edict of the Highest Dao/Way of the Jade Pure True King** (急急如高上神霄玉清真王律令).

**Again**, **invoking the Jade Pure Heavenly Ding General** (玉清天丁神将) and **Master Han** (韩君丈人), **the True Vital Essence descends and manifests**.

**The Heavenly Generals ascend**, **swiftly rushing to the altar** (急赴坛所), **with urgency and haste** (火急速行).
**Swift!** (疾).

**Assembling the Divine Incantation**:
*"I, by the **Heavenly Dao/Way’s Edict** (神霄劫命), **and the Highest Spirit Scripture** (高上灵文), **command the Heavenly Spirits and Earthly Deities** (统领天神地祇), **to search and seize malevolent vital essences**, **sever sickness**, **remove evil, treachery, and oppression** (除凶、奸害、强梁), **and rectify the times in accordance with virtue and vice** (随时正定善恶孝逆).
**Seeing me**, **they must divide and return names** (分回名), **register virtue** (注善), **transmit commands** (传令), **rush to assist** (奔倾), **sever epidemics** (斩瘟), **collect toxins** (收毒), **ward falsehood** (辟非), **and grant life** (注生).*
**The Heavenly Treasury’s duties and responsibilities** (天府天职) **are held firmly in hand**. **One call summons a thousand miles** (一召千里), **the divine army descends**.
**Following the talisman’s command** (承符所勑), **do not question my ability or victory**.
**They arrive swiftly**, **and must not delay**.

The Heavenly Spirit Officials, the myriad Heavenly Soldiers, the Golden-Armored Envoys, and the Commanding Generals—
**Receive my spoken command and carry it out below.**

First, inscribe the matter at hand upon the talisman, recite the spell, blow upon the talisman, and burn it.
**Fix your gaze**—**the true form shall manifest.**

Then declare:
*"With utmost reverence, I summon so-and-so Generals to the Sacred Altar.
Swiftly, as the Highest Celestial Sovereign of the Divine Tao commands."*

Take the **qi** and blow the ashes toward the sick or the place of concern, and with sword-pointing, shout: *"Disease, be gone!"*
**As you will it.**

True talisman presented to the **Mysterious Spirit Celestial Venerable**,

Fire decrees to sweep away inauspiciousness,
Crush demonic hosts,
The Heavenly Prison to seize demons—
Swiftly descend, True Spirit!

**Divine Regulations of the Celestial Treasury (Shén Fǔ Tiáo Yí):**
To receive the **supreme Daoist seals of the Celestial Treasury (Gāo Shàng Shén Fǔ fǎ luó fú yìn)**, fulfill one’s **celestial office (xiān zhí)**, and enter the **Grand Daoist Cadre (Dà Dòng xiān pǐn)**, one must first proclaim one’s **official rank (guān pǐn)**, then ascend in rank to attain the **Daoist official grades (xiān guān pǐn)**. This is not a mundane affair; it is known as **hidden leadership (àn lǐng)**. After daily practice, if the **divine qi (shén líng)** manifests anomalies, one may then enter the **first grade**. Gradually ascending in rank, one reaches the **ninth grade of the Daoist Cadre (jiǔ pǐn jiào zhí)**. According to the law: *"This is to enter the Celestial Treasury at night to adjudicate official matters, then ascend to the solar office by day."* Now, however, since mortal bodies are impure and cannot fully attain the **wondrous Dao (miào Dào)**, one must first **refine the body and atone for sins (liàn shēn xiè guò)**, **adjust the spirit and gather the qi (tiáo shén jí qì)**, to achieve even slight purity, thus allowing one to practice the Dao. If even slightly impure, one may not practice it. When future achievements are accomplished, one must **present a memorial to the Celestial Treasury (jù zòu shén fǔ)**, **face the Holy Sovereign (duì shèng gěi kuàng)**, and receive the **Daoist official seals (xiān guān luó)**. Wearing the **solar office seals (yáng zhí)** above and the **lunar office seals (yīn zhí)** below, one commands the **divine soldiers and generals (bīng jiàng)**, and none shall refuse. Thus, one attains the **perfect composition of the Daoist scriptures (měi zhuàn chéng zhāng)**.

The original **Daoist edicts (yuán kuàng)** once feared the leakage of **heavenly secrets (tiān jī)**, but the **Verdant Emperor of Azure Splendor (Qīng Huá Dà Dì)** declared: *"For all who wish to act, they must first **recollect and visualize the True Sovereign (Zhēn Wáng)** before the **auspicious sign (Zhào)**. They must also **daily draw the qi of the Celestial Treasury from the southeast (shén xiāo qì)**, which is **green in hue (qīng sè)**. When responding to seals, use **yellow silk paper inscribed with cinnabar (huáng sù dān shū)**, drawing the southeast qi and reciting the **Celestial Treasury incantation (shén xiāo jiè)**. The **middle finger bears the script (zhōng zhǐ shàng wén)**. Hold up the hands, extending the **second, fourth, and fifth fingers (èr sì wǔ zhǐ)**, to command the **divine officers and soldiers (shù yòng zhū jiàng děng)**, as needed in thought and deed. When **applying seals to summon deities (shī fú zhào shén)**, **direct the intent while writing (shì yì xià bǐ)**, and **close the qi at will (rén yì yú fú xià bǐ qì)** beneath the seal, **cultivating the left and right eyes seven times (yíng zuǒ yòu mù qī cì)**. The deity shall descend, and one shall naturally know it. **Official seals must be stamped with incantations (guān biǎo yòng yìn)**, requiring **secret mantras (mì zhòu)**, to await **divine response (gǎn yìng)**.

This method is not restricted to **Daoists or laypersons (dào sú)**, nor to **men or women (nán nǚ)**; all who have sincerity may practice it. To summon the **divine officers (zhū shén)**, one must first **invoke the Golden Boy functionaries (Yù Tóng Gōng Cáo)** to request them.

When applying seals and **visualizing the qi (cún xiàn)**, use the **inkstone as a Dragon Circle (yàn wéi Lóng Quān)**, the **ink as Red Jade (mò wéi Chì Yù)**, the **brush as Yellow Dragon (bǐ wéi Huáng Lóng)**, and the **paper as Golden Tablet (zhǐ wéi Jīn Bǎn)**. As one writes, **close the qi (bǐ qì)** and **focus the intent (zhù xiǎng)**, forming the **Golden Seal (jīn zhuàn)**. **Visualize the Five Stars of the Celestial Treasury (Shén Xiāo Jù Wǔ Xīng)** descending as **threads of light (sī máng)** into the seals. With water, **send them forth (shuǐ sòng zhī)**, and the **Five Stars shall stand in attendance (wǔ chén shì lì)**.

**Subduing Demons and Dispelling Ghosts (Fú Mó Xiāo Guǐ):**
The **Verdant Emperor of Azure Splendor (Qīng Huá Dà Dì)** said: *"I see demons and ghosts intermingling, now not subjugated by the **Forest of the Dao (Lín Zhì Dòng)**, causing harm to mortals and bringing calamity and illness."* By fortune, the **True Sovereign (Zhēn Wáng)** has appeared; I pray for **Your compassionate mercy (yán bèi cuí mǐn)**.

The **Verdant Emperor** further declared: *"The human heart governs all transformations (wàn huà). If one **harbors the divine spirit (cún qì shén)**, the spirit abides within the heart, governed by all transformations. If one **knows the divine spirit (rú zhī qì shén)**, the spirit guards the person. If one **does not know the divine spirit (zǐ bù zhī qì shén)**, the spirit departs from the person. If one **does not harbor the divine spirit (zǐ bù cún qì shén)**, the spirit returns to the person—this is the spirit’s nature."* The **Three Officials (Sān Guān)** lament, and the **Five Deities (Wǔ Shén)** depart the body. This is when **demons arise from within (mó cóng nèi qǐ)** and **ghosts come from without (guǐ cóng wài lái)**. When demons and ghosts rejoice, the **divine qi becomes a thief (shén biàn wéi zéi)**. **Life and death are inscribed in the left and right seals (zuò shēng míng yú zuǒ qiè, zhù sǐ luó yú yòu gōng)**. **Illness and injury invade the body (jí bìng lái shāng)**, how much more so to **prolong one’s distant lifespan (yǐ yán xiá shòu)**? I now beseech Your mercy and **explain the supreme Daoist method of Subduing Demons and Dispelling Ghosts (Wú Jí Jìn Mó Xiāo Guǐ zhī Dào)**. You must **listen attentively and receive it with reverence (mì tīng jìng xìn shòu zhī)**, not revealing it to the unworthy.

With this method, **all demons shall be banished (pì chú wàn mó)**, and the **three calamities (sān zāi)** shall not afflict you. The **nine adversities (jiǔ héng)** shall not invade, and **ten thousand ghosts and myriad fiends (wàn guǐ qiān yāo)** shall forever dare not approach.

**The Five-Star Demon-Subduing Method (Fú Mó Wǔ Xīng Fǎ):**
**Visualize the Golden Star (Jīn Xīng)** at the **head (tóu)**.
**Visualize the Wood Star (Mù Xīng)** at the **left ear (zuǒ ěr)**.
**Visualize the Water Star (Shuǐ Xīng)** at the **right ear (yòu ěr)**.
**Visualize the Fire Star (Huǒ Xīng)** at the **left shoulder (zuǒ jiān)**.
**Visualize the Earth Star (Tǔ Xīng)** at the **right shoulder (yòu jiān)**.

Invoke the **Five Stars with the Mantra of the Heavenly Stem and Earthly Branches (Hé Lì Shén Xiāo)**:

Add the **Five Measures (Wǔ Dǒu)** to complete the incantation: *"..."*

The **Four Spirits counteracting**, the **Five Measures** come to aid.
A thousand calamities scatter and vanish, ten thousand misfortunes are self-removed.
Now I act, turning my back on **solitude and emptiness**.
What petty ghost dares approach my dwelling?
**Heavenly Laborers and Mighty Warriors**—when moved, they exterminate all.

This method, **subduing the heavens above and the earth below**, vanquishes all powerful ghosts—this is the most essential and wondrous Dao-gate.

**The Supreme Dao of the Celestial Palace’s Jade Purity True King’s Purple Script Great Dao Volume Eight.**

**Great Protective Body Method for Subduing Ghosts and Pacifying Demons**
The Master says: On the first day of the first month or before, stand in a secluded chamber, facing north, and pay four obeisances to the **Elemental Sovereign** [元君].
The **Elemental Sovereign** is the primordial lord who opened the heavens, also called the **Dao Ancestor Holy Mother** [道祖圣母].
If one does not pay homage to the Holy Mother, the practice of the Dao will never be efficacious.

Compose and recite a **Confession of Sins** [忏罪文].
After recitation, strike the teeth three times [叩齿三通], and in secret visualize the **Five Stars** [五星]:
- The **Solar Year Star** [岁星] in the left hand, its hue like jade.
- The **Great White Star** [太白] in the right hand, its hue like white jade.
- The **Mars Star** [荧惑] upon the crown, its hue like a fire pearl.
- The **Lunar Star** [镇星] within the heart, its hue like yellow gold.
- The **Wood Star** [辰星] beneath the feet, its hue like black gemstone.

All radiate divine light, illuminating the entire body.

Recite the incantation in secret:
*"Five Stars arrayed in splendor,
Their light piercing the dark abyss.
Ten thousand gods and saints,
Guard my true spirit.
Titanic heavens and fierce beasts,
Subdued by the Five Weapons.
Five Heavenly demons,
Perish in body and form.
Wherever I stand,
All gods pay homage.
Swiftly, as the Law commands."*

Again, visualize the Five Stars guarding you, their transformations boundless:
- The **Wood Star** transforms into a **Wind Wheel**.
- The **Fire Star** becomes a great flame, encircling the body.
- The **Metal Star** in the right hand becomes a **Diamond God-Sword**, its radiance piercing the heavens, emitting scorching fire.
- The **Wood Star** beneath the feet transforms into a river, swiftly becoming a sea, from which five dragons surge forth.

Recite the incantation:
*"Five Stars anchor my form,
Their light illuminating the fiery essence.
Preserve my five limbs,
Subdue my ten thousand spirits.
Six Heavenly demons,
Cut down upon movement.
Swiftly, as the Law commands."*

Next, visualize the **Heavenly Coalescent Killing Qi** [天罡大煞炁] descending from the **Heavenly Coalescent** [天罡].
Its qi is **yellow within, black without**, reaching before you—inhale it twelve times through the nose.

Recite the incantation:
*"Great Killing True Qi,
Yin within, Yang without.
Preserve my life-force,
Drive away evil, avert calamity.
Mountain goblins and wights,
Land spirits and [殃歹十羊].
Red-mouthed, white-tongued,
Serpents, beasts, wolves.
Those who harm me die,
Those who plot against me perish.
Those who love me prosper,
Those who serve me flourish.
Ten thousand gods crushed,
Cowering beneath the Heavenly Coalescent.
Swiftly, as the Law commands."*

Place the left hand over the heart, the right hand on the crown, and in secret visualize:
- [□ Star] in the right hand,
- [□ Star] in the left hand,
- [□ Star] before the chest.

Recite the incantation:
*"[□ Star] Great Killing,
Anchor my heart’s origin.
Ward off the Five Weapons without,
Eliminate the Five Plagues within.
Those who oppose me falter,
Those who plot against me die.
Malevolent ghosts and fiendish gods—
What power do they hold against me?
Swiftly, as the Law commands."*

Place the left hand over the heart, the right hand pointing to heaven, and visualize:
- [□ Star] in the right hand,
- [□ Star] in the left hand,
- [□ Star] upon the head.

Recite the incantation:
*"Bright Yang True Qi,
Crown me with crimson radiance.
Ward off ten thousand calamities,
And all inverted misfortunes.
Thieves, malevolent men,
Serpents, beasts, wolves.
Those who plot against me die,
Those who harm me perish.
Red-mouthed, white-tongued,
Cowering beneath the Heavenly Coalescent.
Swiftly, as the Law commands."*

Point the right hand backward toward the heart, the left hand toward the heart, and visualize:
- [□ Star] in the left hand,
- [□ Star] upon the head,
- [□ Star] in the right hand.

Recite the incantation:
*"Luminous True Qi,
Residing in the Heavenly Coalescent.
Anchored in the Vermilion Palace,
Warding off all unnatural disasters.
What god dares remain,
What ghost dares approach?
Ten thousand gods and ghosts,
Subdued by my Heavenly Coalescent.
Swiftly, as the Law commands."*

With both hands, support the **Three Palace Stars** [三台星] as a **Flowery Canopy** [华盖].
Store the **Upper Palace Star Official** [上台星官] in the left middle finger,
the **Middle Palace Star Official** [中台星官] in the right hand,
the **Lower Palace Star Official** [下台星官] beneath both knees.

Recite the incantation:
*"My head wears the Flowery Canopy,
My feet tread the [□ Coalescent].
The Earth Net spans the Eight Extremes,
The Heavenly Net stretches in four directions.
The Northern Dipper falls in death,
Yin evils perish in calamity.
The Southern Dipper ascends in life,
Longevity extended.
Prayers fulfilled as desired,
Wherever I stand, auspicious fortune.
Internal and external calamities,
Perish upon movement.
Swiftly, as the Law commands."*

**Form the Seal and Gesture** [造印式].

「The **Dharma** speaks: *"For all who form the Seal, let it be done on the days of **Jiazi** [甲子] or **Gengshen** [庚申], facing southeast, during the **Chen** [辰] and **Si** [巳] hours. In a **pure and secret chamber** [浄密室], first burn incense and silently pray to the **Celestial Sovereign** [神霄真炁] to blow into the wood.

Then, command the artisan to carve it within one hour, ensuring no breaks or interruptions in the strokes. Use **clear jade stone** [清玉石] or the **heartwood of the jujube tree** [赤枣心], and follow the **Dharma** to consecrate it. The **Dharma for consecrating the Seal** speaks:

*"For all who consecrate the Seal, let it be done on the **three nines day** [三九日] or **Jiazi** [甲子], at the time when humans are in **meditative stillness** [人定]. Set up a single table in the secret chamber, spreading **silk cloth** [缯帛] upon it. Offer **steamed cakes** [蒸饼] three pieces, **soup** [汤] three bowls, and **incense** [香] one burner. Also arrange **thirty-six candles** [三十六分列] on both sides as incense and lamps. Light the incense three times, and pour wine upon the table.

Stand in the northwest, facing south, and bow twice, stating: 'A humble servant, [臣某], who delights in longevity and cultivates the **Dao/Way** [大道] for great blessings, now solemnly offers this prayer. On this auspicious night, I devoutly prepare incense, lamps, and offerings to seek **spiritual grace** [灵贶].'

I, [臣某], humbly petition the **Great Emperor of Longevity** [长生大帝君], the **Emperor of Azure Clarity** [青华大帝君], the **Revered Master of Good Life** [好生韩君丈人], the **True Sovereign of the Radiant Treasure Heaven** [曜华玉宝天真皇人], the **Upper True Sovereign of the Celestial Sovereign Jade Gate** [神霄玉阙上真元君], the **True Consorts** [左右真妃], the **Celestial Minister** [上相仙伯], the **True Officials of Left Clarity and Right Extremity** [左华右极真宰仙圣], the **Celestial and Spirit Officials** [仙官灵官], the **Saintly Assembly of the Seal of Universal Chapter** [通章印中圣众], the **Jade Text and Precious Seal** [玉文琼玺], and the **Swiftly Commanded General of Thunder-Fire to Sever Evil and Pursue Plague** [急催追捉斩邪断瘟电火大将军], as well as the **Saintly Assembly of Seal-Bearers** [掌印捧印擎印圣众], the **Local Deities of the Direct Altar** [直坛土地], and all **true spirits** [一切真灵].

I, [臣某], am pure in body and mind, bearing this **precious Seal** [宝印]. May I be free from internal illness and external malevolence, aiding **Heaven** in its transformations and assisting the **state** in saving its people, severing all evil and banishing malevolent spirits. Yesterday, on the [某] year, [某] month, [某] day, at [某] hour, I went to [某处] and, following the **scriptures** [箓], received the transmission of the **Celestial Sovereign Jade Text Seal** [神霄玉文琼玺], the **Universal Chapter Precious Talisman** [通章宝符], and the **Thunder-Fire Seals for Swiftly Severing Evil** [雷火斩邪急捉等印]. Now, on this auspicious day, I solemnly consecrate and offer them in the **pure chamber** [浄室] of [某处].

The Seals I have received were, on the [年月日], presented to the **Three Teachers** [三师帝君] in a **flying petition** [飞奏]. I humbly beg for their **command** [勑命] to be issued and bestowed upon my subordinates and all those involved, so that when they encounter my movement, they may verify, recognize, and execute them accordingly.

Furthermore, I beg for the **bestowal of Heavenly Saints to guard the Seal** [天仙圣众护印], and for the **Spirit Kings of Thunderous Might and Divine Envoys** [神王雷霆猛吏、直符使者] to protect the **Jade Text Universal Chapter Talisman** [玉文通章符印].

May the **Dao/Way’s myriad layers of virtue/power** [道炁] flow into my Seals, enabling me to summon **spirit generals** [神将], rally **divine soldiers** [吏兵], capture **evil essences** [邪精], and slay **spirit demons** [神鬼], thereby rescuing the people and achieving swift efficacy.

Next, I wish to petition **Heaven** naturally, aligning with longevity, ascending to the **Jade Palace** [玉府], and paying homage to the **Supreme Deity** [上帝], merging with the **Dao/Way’s true essence** [道合同].

I, [臣某], am overwhelmed by reverence and awe, bowing repeatedly. I light incense, pour wine, scatter flowers, and bow again. The **Celestial Sovereign Jade Text Seal** [神霄玉文宝印] is hidden in the **Nine Heavens and Eighty Thousand Eons** [九霄八万余劫].

This command aligns with the **virtuous and auspicious** [契贤昌运], as desired by **immortals and spirits** [仙民]. Before using it, one must first consecrate it to gain its efficacy. Spread the **Elemental Heaven’s Blockhouse** [元天坎户] upon my head and the **Square Earth’s Separate Palace** [方成离宫] beneath my feet.

With **five divine swords** [神剑] and **five precious mirrors** [宝镜], five **silk banners** [缯旛], five **soup bowls** [栢汤], five **offerings of seasonal fruits** [时果], and one **cauldron of jujube honey and incense soup** [木蜜陵香汤], along with **pure water and strong tea** [浄水清酽], arrange incense and flowers below the altar, in two middle layers, and one upper layer. Place the five Seals below the **Nine Heavens Lamp** [九霄灯], following the **Great Microconstellation’s Aegis** [太微罡].

I humbly report: *"A minor servant of the Celestial Sovereign, [臣某], now reverently petitions the **Three Teachers** [三师帝君], the **True Sovereign of Heaven** [天真皇人], the **Master of the Han Department** [韩司丈人], the **Heavenly Worthy of the Jade Palace** [玉府天尊], the **Thunder-Fire General** [雷火大将军], the **Universal Chapter Envoys** [通章使者], the **Heavenly Seal-Bearers** [掌印天丁], the **Wind Lord and Rain Teacher** [风伯雨师], and the **Saintly Assembly of the Thunder Department** [雷部圣众].

I have been graced by the **Great Transformation** [大化], receiving the **unique blessings** [殊恩] of the **Dao/Way**. I now bear the **scriptures of the Dao/Way** [法箓], ascending to the **immortal stages** [仙阶]. Today, I walk the **Heavenly Round** [建天圆], standing at the **Earthly Blockhouse** [地户]. With utmost sincerity, I convey my devotion to the **Celestial Sovereign** [神霄].

I possess the **immortal precious Seal** [仙宝玉印], and according to the **science** [科], I now consecrate and bow. I humbly pray that the **true saints and immortals** [真仙众圣] take pity on my sincerity and bestow **immortal virtue/power** [仙真道炁], infusing it into the **precious Seal** [宝印]. May all **talismans and scriptures** [飞符走箓] be granted to execute this command.

Those who defy the **Dao/Way** [不顺道者], upon seeing the Seal, shall turn to dust.

Next, I hope that after my consecration, all my sins may be absolved, and I may be granted **original pardon** [原赦], achieving **serenity of body and mind** [身心泰定], **harmony within my spiritual realm** [神宇和平], and **prosperity in all endeavors** [所向利亨].

I earnestly pray for **spiritual response** [灵应], as if my petitions were granted. I am deeply indebted to the **Dao/Way’s boundless grace** [罔极之恩].

I now solemnly present my **verbal pledge** [口章] and bow to the **Jade Palace** [玉府]. I, [臣某], am sincerely fearful and trembling, bowing repeatedly in reverence and awe.

I now humbly conclude. Next, light incense with a **red Seal** [朱印], imprinting it seven times and swallowing it. According to the **Dharma**, perform three consecrations to purify **impure, unclean, and turbid places** [忌秽浊处], and the Seal shall fly and move on its own.

On the day the **merit is fulfilled** [功满], wear the Seal and ride the **Phoenix Chariot** [凤车], ascending to the **Celestial Sovereign’s court** [神霄上朝].

It is most auspicious to keep this **Seal secret** [大宜秘之].

This Seal, made of **gold** [金], governs the **divine spirits of the Nine Heavens and Nine Earths** [九天九地神祇], the **Jade Palace** [玉府], and the **dragons of the Four Seas and Three Rivers** [四海三江水曹龙神]. Using this Seal to command, none shall escape its influence.

It cures **all ten thousand diseases** [万病]. Swallowing it shall bring immediate recovery.

This Seal, made of **jujube wood** [枣木] or **gold** [金], with **cinnabar** [丹砂] applied to the imprint. When used in **Heavenly affairs** [天上], it aligns with the **true essence** [真契], able to reach the **Ninth Heaven** [玉九], and not fall back down.

All **divine spirits** [万神] can be summoned through this Seal, using **cinnabar** [丹砂] to empower it.

This Seal, made of **gold and jade** [金玉], or carved from **jujube wood** [枣木] and imprinted with **cinnabar** [丹砂], is the **inscription of the Eightfold Awe** [八威毒蛇之篆], governing the **Thunder Spirits of the Jade Palace** [玉府雷神] and petitioning the **Two Marshes** [两泽].

Burning or incinerating it shall subdue **evil spirits** [邪鬼], and striking it shall slay **water demons** [水怪]. Cast the Seal in **yellow silk** [黄纱] into the water to destroy **monstrous beings** [怪], banish **plagues** [瘟疫], and subdue **demonic spawn** [鬼胎].

Use the Seal to **strike and summon the Wind and Heavenly Spirits** [惊风天吊], and imprinting it shall cure **all ten thousand diseases** [万病即瘥].」

「The ailments of **wandering tigers** [走虎], upon striking with this Seal, shall vanish instantly.

Once the **Thunder Department Seal** [雷部符] is applied, its efficacy is beyond measure.

This Seal, carved from **jujube wood struck by thunder** [雷震枣木], and imprinted with **cinnabar** [丹砂], commands **eight million divine soldiers** [神兵八百万], who follow the Seal to drive away plagues and slay evil spirits.

During great epidemics, deploy the **Sorting Gate Seal** [排门印] to prevent the plague from entering homes. Those who swallow the Seal shall sweat and be spared from infecting others.

When **malevolent spirits** [邪怪] torment people and defy the **Dao** [法], arrange the Seal on all four sides of the altar, facing its own direction, and set it ablaze. The spirit shall then perish in form.

Change the Seal as needed when performing rituals.

This Seal, carved from **jujube wood struck by thunder** [雷震枣木], shall be used according to the situation.

For all urgent matters, imprint with the Seal—its designated **spirit** [所司] shall act swiftly without delay. To seize spirits and pursue demons, the Seal shall arrive instantly.

When wielding the Seal, **all divine spirits** [万神] shall guard in attendance, never daring to leave the altar.

**Offering the Seal and drawing upon the Dao/Way’s qi** [取炁咒], **imprinting the hour** [掐辰], and **inscribing longevity at the Southern Pole** [南极长生] shall dissolve calamities and bring life.

When the **Three Officials** [三台] have been subdued, **all virtues/powers** [万善] shall be attained.

For urgent matters, as the **Highest Sovereign of the Celestial Palace** [高上神霄玉清真王] decrees: **Swiftly, like the lofty Celestial Palace!**

**Unsealing and invoking the Seal’s power**:
O **Highest Sovereign of the Celestial Palace** [神霄上帝], grant this Seal its **spiritual efficacy** [通灵].
May **Lord Han** [韩君] descend with blessings—no wish shall remain unfulfilled.
Let **malevolent spirits** [邪妖] return to **orthodoxy** [皈正], and the **Dao’s qi** [道炁] shall secretly cultivate.

Swiftly, like the **Highest Sovereign of the Celestial Palace** [高上神霄玉清真王] decrees!

**Invoking the Seal’s power**:
O **Celestial Palace’s Sacred Seal** [神霄宝印], command the **hundred spirits** [百灵] to obey.
By **imperial decree** [勑令], those who receive the command shall be **Heavenly Laborers** [天丁].
With one strike of the **Divine Seal** [神印], life shall be endless.
All **demons** [万魔] shall bow in submission, and **thousandfold evils** [千邪] shall perish in form.

Swiftly, like the **Highest Sovereign of the Celestial Palace** [高上神霄玉清真王] decrees!

**Seal’s Efficacy Invocation**:
The **Highest Sovereign of the Celestial Palace** [高上神霄] has secretly bestowed this upon the heavens, and messengers have proclaimed it.
The **cloud inscriptions** [云篆] radiate with brilliance, profound and yet more profound.
Sealed in secret, the auspicious smoke ascends.
No delay shall occur—it shall swiftly reach the **Jade Throne** [玉几].
By **imperial decree** [勑命], the **Heavenly Edicts of the Celestial Palace** [神霄仙旨] are proclaimed.

Swiftly, like the decree!

**Sealing Invocation**:
Heavenly Laborers receive the command, mighty warriors bear the talisman.
**Demonic spirits** [妖精] shall be beheaded and slain, **evil demons** [邪魔] shall be executed.
Within the **Three Realms** [三界], they shall obey my orders.

Swiftly, like the **Highest Sovereign of the Celestial Palace** [高上神霄玉清真王] decrees!

Swiftly, like the decree!

**True Talismans of the Thirty-Six Heavenly Prisons of the Celestial Highness**
**The Celestial Highness True King declares:**
Behind my palace lies the **Yùlíng Void Realm**,
Where the **Thirty-Six Heavenly Prisons** are arrayed.
I command the **Central Yellow Emperor** to govern all prisons,
Thus bringing them under heavenly jurisdiction.
These **True Talismans of the Heavenly Prisons** are formed from the **six yang qi of the Ninefold Highness—pure, refined, and luminous**,
Naturally coalescing into authentic talismans.
Mere mortals, shaped by the womb and born of filth,
Their impure qi not yet dispelled,
Their bodies not yet perfected in truth,
Cannot summon the heavenly qi.
But if one practices the **Dao of Highest Clarity**,
Then the **three realms’** evil demons and rebellious spirits shall assail the true gods,
Disturbing the heart,
Stirring up chaotic thoughts,
And summoning ten thousand evils to harass.
Thus, beyond the **Six Heavens**,
When the **auspicious cycle converges**,
The **Dao transformation shall be enacted**,
And the **True Talismans** shall gradually reveal themselves.
Those who receive them
Shall be able to subdue evil demons,
Sever evil desires,
And ensure the **Three Palaces** remain tranquil,
With the **Ninefold Qi** guarding the form.
If one violates these precepts,
The guilt shall not be absolved.
**As the Highest Clarity True King of the Celestial Highness decrees.**

**Method:**
Each prison has one **Supervising Official of the Prison**,
And within the prison, **one hundred and twenty spirits, true officers, and attendants**.
The **Heavenly Prison Officials, soldiers, and scribes**
Shall hold these talismans,
Drive and bind evil spirits,
And with solemn hearts and fasting,
Inscribe the **True Talismans** in cinnabar seals,
Using them at will to summon and compel.
For all talisman-holding,
Only one **Heavenly Prison Talisman** is required;
It is not necessary to use all of them.

**Method:**
For stubborn and malevolent spirits that refuse to be pacified,
Establish the **Thirty-Six Heavenly Prisons**,
And transform your body into that of the **True King**.
Pinch the **Shēn** finger,
Visualize the vastness of the Heavenly Prisons,
The Heavenly Soldiers on either side,
The thunderous formations encircling,
And the **True King** standing with sword in hand.
The **Supervising Officials, true scribes, and attendants** shall be stern and resolute.
The **Divine Edict** must be strictly observed,
And the malevolent shall be captured and revealed.
The **True King’s** command shall be fulfilled,
And the evil traces shall be clearly manifested within the prison.

**Investigation and Examination:**
For those who practice the **Dao**,
When entering or exiting a household,
If malevolent spirits or evil entities harass the practitioner,
First cleanse the resting place,
Making it pure and spotless.
Then, erect a **monochrome prison formation**,
And upon it, offer the **Generals, scribes, and soldiers**.
Raise a **black banner** at the center of the formation.
Summon the generals to capture the evil spirits,
Who shall then reveal their true forms here.

**True Talismans of the Heavenly Prisons of the Highest Sovereign**
**True Talismans of the Flying Divine, Flowing Light, and Supreme Vermilion**
This talisman shall summon the **Heavenly Prison Masters of the Ninefold Highness**.
**The Celestial Highness True King declares:**
All who practice the **Dao of the Celestial Highness**
Shall, above, capture Heavenly Miasms,

With none left untreated.
Or, within any region or corner,
Mountains, rivers, lakes, or seas,
If **earthly or wooden spirit evils**,
Or **five-phase imbalanced deities**,
Act in deviance,
Stirring up miasms and calamities,
Harming living beings,
Or endangering the people,
And all other methods fail,
Then summon the **Heavenly Prison Just Gods**,
The **Void-Heaven Officials of Auspicious Terrains**,
And the **Spiritual Soldiers and Cavalry of the Five Peaks, Four Marshes, Rivers, Lakes, Mountains, and City Deities**,
To search and capture them for annihilation,
At will summoning and binding.
Or, if within the **Ninefold Abyss**,
The **Ninefold Shoulder, Northern Darkness, and the Black Capital of the Yang**,
Evil spirits, malevolent deities, and vengeful ghosts
Entangle and harass living beings,
Extending upwards and downwards,
And no method can resolve them,
Then summon the **Ninefold Ranks, Heavy Darkness, and the Black Officials of the Northern Capital**,
And the **Spiritual Soldiers and Cavalry of the Nine Regions**,
To drive and dispatch them at will,
And thus accumulate merit for the world.
**Do not harbor thoughts of greed for wealth,**
Or covetousness in your heart.
If one uses the **Dao** to seize what is not wealth,
Then the guilt shall extend to the **Nine Ancestors**—
How can one not be warned?

On each occasion of talisman-holding and advancement,

And presenting petitions at will.

To arrest the evil spirits—
And their retribution shall be immediate.

*Tiāngāng* (天罡): A term from Daoist cosmology, often referring to a celestial force or a type of punishment. In this context, it likely signifies an irresistible or severe decree.

**Right: The Thirty-Six Heavenly Prisons**—
These are the **Yin-Prison and Yang-Prison**,
Established according to the cardinal directions.

**At the Prison, use a single tablet to honor the Prison Officials:**
For **Yin**, employ fine sand;
For **Yang**, use fire ash.
Write the talisman upon it,
Then cover the **Grand Heavenly Prison** with the ash and sand.
**Stars** are drawn with the **Taunting Trigram** method—
Shining like a mirror’s reflection, leaving no trace.

With the **Daoist Decree** and **Magical Script** inscribed, forming **emptiness** into **Vajra** (梵), letting **true *qi*** (真炁) arise naturally.

Healing diseases and beheading demons (斩邪), all beings live in peace.

**The Three Talismans of the Three Palaces:**
**First Talisman** – The **First Upper Palace** (上丹明堂), the **White Emperor** (白帝) banishes malevolence.
The **Six Palaces** (六宫) are illuminated and pure, the **Daoist transformation** (道化) brings eternal life.
All diseases depart swiftly, granting you eternal life.
**Second Talisman** – The **Middle Palace** (中丹赤子), the **Yellow Emperor** (黄帝) as **Primordial Sage** (元仙).
He foreknows fortune and misfortune, purifying and calming the **heart and essence** (心元).
The **crimson elixir** (丹晶一液) preserves life and extends years.
**Third Talisman** – The **Lower Palace** (下府神君), the **Red Emperor** (赤帝) and **Black King** (黑王).
The **Six Palaces** (六府) flow with **liquid essence** (流液), no disease can harm.
The **golden elixir** (金液) safeguards life, the talisman brings eternal auspiciousness.

**Talismans of the Three Elements:**
**Upper Element Talisman** – The **Upper Element Child** (上元赤子), guarding in the **Yellow Chamber** (黄房).
He **captures spirits** (摄神) and **restores life** (皈命), safeguarding the child’s eternal prosperity.
**Middle Element Talisman** – The **Middle Element** (中元太乙), seated in the **Jade Hall** (玉堂).
He **summons souls** (招魂) and **protects the body** (卫身), allowing you to behold the True King.
**Lower Element Talisman** – The **Lower Element Sovereign** (下元元主), arrayed in the **Divine Court** (神庭).
He **controls the soul** (制魂) and **creates vitality** (成阳), ascending to the **Jade Hall**.
The method states: These **three talismans** govern the **ascension and descent of the Three Palaces** (三宫升降), all diseases vanish, **true *qi*** (真炁) endures forever.
With **finger-tracing script** (掐辰文), drawing **perverse *qi*** (巽炁), inscribed in **cinnabar** (朱), burned to ash, and mixed with **frankincense broth** (乳香汤).
For children, wear it on the chest.
Facing **east-southeast** (东南), recite the **Jade Purity Decree** (玉清诀) after swallowing, invoking the **Supreme Sage of the Great Compassion** (太乙救苦天尊) three hundred times.

**Daoist Decree Talisman:**
The **Eastern March Sovereign** (东华元君), the **Lord of the Han** (韩君) descends.
The **Jade Registry** (玉府) holds **true destiny** (真命), safeguarding **living beings** (生灵) with vitality.

**Method for Cursing Water to Heal Diseases:**
For those who request **Daoist talisman water** (符水), state the reason clearly.
After invoking the **spirits** (祝神), settle the water.
With the right hand, draw **southeast *qi*** (东南炁) as per the method, using the **Decree of Ding and Jia** (丁甲诀).
Left hand’s thumb presses the middle finger, tracing the **Zi character** (子文), then reversing, pressing the four fingers onto the thumb; the remaining **two and five fingers** (二五指) stand straight.

**Decree:**
*"The **Supreme Virtue** (乾元) of **Heaven** (亨利), **Sincerity** (贞) – the **Six Jia** (六甲) align with me.
The **spiritual spring** (灵泉) enters the **Five Zang** (五脏), the **Six Fu** (六腑) remain undisturbed and secure.
*As fast as the high celestial decree of the True King of Jade Purity in the Divine Tao.*

After completing the decree, **dip the talisman into the water** (挑诀入水), then trace the **Jade Purity Decree** (玉清诀) again.
Next, recite the **decree**:
*"The **Seven Stars** (七政) and **Eight Spirits** (八灵), the sun and moon born together.
Rooted in **Dao** (道德) and **De** (德), I hold the **true name** (真名).
The **North Star** (北方辰星) is my **true form** (真形).
I can **purge all impurities** (荡万秽), I can **nourish all truths** (润万真).
I can **endure in unity** (终守一), preserving life for all.
All **hundred demons** (百邪) are purged, the **Five Zang** (五脏) are secure.
**Ren-Gui-Ren-Gui** (壬癸壬癸), entrusted to **Heavenly Ding** (天丁).
*As fast as the high celestial decree of the True King of Jade Purity in the Divine Tao.*

Then **draw the Big Dipper** (子午斗).
Dip into the water and recite:
*"Glowing and resplendent** (荧荧煌煌), the **Seven Stars** (七星) gaze upward.
Born as the **Big Dipper** (北斗), they are the **Heavenly Ganges** (天罡).
**Supreme Virtue** (乾元) and **Sincerity** (亨利贞) – all radiance belongs to the **Imperial Realm** (帝乡).
*As fast as the high celestial decree of the True King of Jade Purity in the Divine Tao.*

**Talisman Decree for Dispatch:**
The **celestial thunder** (天雷) is hidden, the **Dragon and Tiger** (龙虎) merge.
The sun, moon, stars, and **Big Dipper** (斗) shine clearly.
On such-and-such a day, the **Functionary** (功曹) carries the talisman forth.
To **banish disease and subdue evil** (去病伐恶), delay not, come swiftly.
The **manifest retribution** (报应) is clear – do not harm your own body.
Swiftly now.
After completing the decree, **store the talisman** (存将) and let it follow the talisman’s command.

language shall not form chapters.

you shall be consigned to the **Kui-Gang** (魁罡).
**急急如高上神霄玉清真王律令。**

This method: **pinched with the hour’s mark**, drawing **xun-qi** (巽氣),
written in cinnabar on yellow paper.

If a person is struck by a flying corpse,
unconscious and unresponsive,
or if one hunts in the southern marshes and is plagued,
swallow it with peach-branch decoction—
immediate relief shall follow.
Further, with one *dou* of the decoction,
sprinkle it—most efficacious.

**Exorcising Monsters Talisman**
Incantation says:
**Jade Purity Celestial Sovereign**, slaying the Celestial Essence.
**Upper Purity Earthly Sovereign**, slaying the Earthly Demon.
**Supreme Purity Human Sovereign**, warding off inauspiciousness.
To the **Seventh Generation of You-Jiao** (酉角), consign to the **Heavenly Officials**.
The **Primordial Sovereign** prostrates—
the **Ghost Emperor** diminishes in form.
Ten thousand monsters, a hundred thousand demons—
none may linger.

**急急如神霄玉清灭魔王律令。**

This method: **pinched with the hour’s mark**, drawing **xun-qi**.
For all who:
- Lure chickens and dogs,
- Knock at doors and ransack homes,
- Cause financial loss and depletion,
- Or make livestock eat one another—
all manner of monstrous disturbances.

In the courtyard, bury square tiles in the eight directions—
the calamity and monsters shall then depart.

**Verdant Emperor**, resplendent and transformative,
cross-cutting calamity, driving away the raging winds.
**急急如高上神霄玉清真王律令。**

capable of severing human grudges,
capable of cutting through human enmity.

speak my name.
**Azure Dragon Meng-Zhang**, drink your own blood.
**White Tiger Marshal**, bite your throat.
**Red-Fanged Great Knife**, grind your tongue—
heaven and man alike.
Today, I denounce you—
your deceitful body is seized.

**急急如高上神霄消魔王律令。**

This method: **pinched with the hour’s mark**, drawing **xun-qi**,
written on **paulownia wood** at the **Spring Equinox or Double Fifth**,
nailed into the doorframe of the hall.
If cursed by slanderous speech,
write in cinnabar on yellow paper,
swallow and wear,
reciting the **Sage’s Holy Name of the Exalted One Who Dissolves Calamity and Resolves Misfortune** three hundred times.

**Talisman to Manifest the Form of the Ghost**
**Primordial Sovereign of the Dao**
**Exalted Lord of the Highest Dao**
**Exalted Lord of the Supreme Dao**
Binding the southwest, north, and all directions above and below,
suspended in radiant illumination—
**Above, harmonizing qi as Heaven;**
**Below, harmonizing turbid qi as Earth.**
**The Supreme Departed Sovereign** pursues and seizes ghostly souls,
**Day and Moon** communicate with spirits—
all ghosts and gods revealed.
**Laying the Golden Bridge,**
**Conducting the Ghostly Souls,**
**Heavenly Emperor commanding Heavenly Gods—**
all demons and malevolent spirits manifest.

all malevolent essences become transparent.

**Human executioner of ghosts.**
**Heavenly Gang of the Supreme One—**

following **Kui-He**, ascending **Ming-Shen**—
**Great Auspiciousness of the Grand Functionary, Tai-Ke.**

**Invoking the Thunder God’s Method**
**Method:** When invoking the Thunder God, first purify impurities, sincerely declare:
*"I, [name], of [rank and surname], through countless lifetimes’ fortune, have encountered the Great Dao and met with teachers. By grace, I have received the Great Law. For all who have taken refuge, dare I forget to inform? Now, for [specific matter], I respectfully summon [specific deity]. According to the *Highest Celestial Supreme Ultimate Hidden Scriptures*, I bear this petition and supplication, humbly beseeching the numinous deity to descend upon this altar, displaying divine might."*

Incantation:
*"Heaven, Earth, Sun, Moon, and Stars,
Winds, Clouds, Thunder, Lightning, and Gods—
I, by the decree of the Nine-Heaven Holy Immortal Supervisor,
urgently summon the Five Thunder Generals to swiftly descend."*

*Swiftly, as the Upper Clarity’s decree.*

**Right Ritual:** Recite the Five Thunder Secret, face the Heavenly Gate, strike teeth seven times, and chant seven times. Focus the spirit’s return, and let incense smoke signal completion.
Then, pray for [specific matter]’s conclusion, sending off the day.
Having respectfully declared, the petition’s covenant is complete.
The mortal world’s dusty realm cannot retain celestial steeds.
Return to the divine treasury, bestowing grace upon [name].
For future petitions, proceed as before.

---
**Celestial Constellation Jade Purity Five Thunder Secret Method**
When people suffer harm from malevolent ghosts, spirits, or demons, and cannot drive them away, the method requires sincere devotion, fasting, bathing, and wearing ritual robes within the ritual precinct. Offer incense and declare to the Three Pure Ones, the Supreme Thunder Sovereign.

Then, establish the altar to sacrifice to the Thunder God, and devoutly pray. Step through the *Dou* formation, pinch the Five Thunder seals, close the eyes, and visualize the Four Peach Dragon Kings’ troops emerging with the Thunder God. Spit water and recite the secret, shouting angrily: *"Thunder God, swiftly go and exterminate!"*
Imagine the deity departing ten thousand *li* away. In a moment, the wind will return—this is the return.
That night, offer sacrifices to thank them.

**Thunderfire Marshal, Liu Zhong.**
Left-hand *Qianwen* seal, step facing north, visualize the received Thunder *qi*, take one breath, and store it in the *Dantian*. Take another breath, blow the secret upward, and strike teeth nine times.
Again, take one breath of Thunder *qi*, imagining the abdominal thunder roar.
North Black *qi*—blow toward the afflicted.

**Earth-Thunderfire Marshal, Li Yongzhi.**
Left-hand *Maowen* seal, step facing east, visualize the received Thunder *qi*, take one breath, and store it in the *Dantian*. Take another breath, blow the secret upward, and strike teeth nine times.
Again, take one breath of Thunder *qi*, imagining the abdominal thunder roar.
East Green *qi*—blow toward the afflicted.

**Water-Thunderfire Marshal, Song Shouning.**

**Thunderfire Marshal, Zhou Wenqing.**
Left-hand *Chouwen* seal, step facing south, visualize the received Thunder *qi*, take one breath, and store it in the *Dantian*. Take another breath, blow the secret upward, and strike teeth nine times.
Again, take one breath of Thunder *qi*, imagining the thunder sound rising, the face flushed and warm, the mouth as if fire emerges—blow toward the afflicted.

**Thunderfire Marshal, Zhu Yong’an.**
Left-hand *DaShaWen* seal, step facing north, visualize the received Thunder *qi*, take one breath, and store it in the *Dantian*. Take another breath, blow the secret upward, and strike teeth nine times.
Again, take one breath of Thunder *qi*, circulate the *qi*, and evoke the abdominal thunder roar—blow upon the afflicted.

**Summoning Wind Ritual**
Heavenly *Ding* follows my footsteps, the wind’s traces.
Swiftly march and aid my troops,
Bending the demon’s ferocity.
As the law commands, so it is done.
**Right Ritual:** Two hands form the *Yiwen* seal, recite twelve times—mighty wind arrives immediately.

**Gathering Wind Ritual**
Heaven One, Great One—below fills the Mysterious One.
Vast winds gather, the numinous *Gang* spirits assemble.
Follow the sound and breathe in—no pause, no delay.
As the law commands, so it is done.
**Right Ritual:** Two hands form the *TianWai* seal, shout: **"Swiftly cease!"** The wind subsides.

**Summoning Clouds Ritual**
*Qi* of mountains and rivers, the essence of a hundred peaks.
Condensed as a *Huagai*, poured forth as clouds.
Drive the cloud messengers, bind the *qi* as Spirit Lords.
By command, swiftly summoned—no hesitation, no delay.
As the law commands, so it is done.
**Right Ritual:** Two hands form the *Ziwen* seal, recite twenty times—*qi* clouds come in response.

**Gathering Clouds Ritual**
Named peaks and the Five Sacred Mountains, the *Huagai*’s *qi*.
Bound as clouds, dispersed as *qi*.
Retreat back to valleys, return to sacred realms.
When I call, hasten, hasten.
As the Highest Law of the *ShenXiao*玉清真王 commands, so it is done.
**Right Ritual:** Form the *BenShi* seal with both hands, shout: **"Swiftly disperse!"** The clouds scatter immediately.

**Gathering Thunder Ritual**
The Master’s transmitted Way, obeying the decree of the Great Mysterious.
Having issued the command, drive away the source of evil.
Return to their original positions—do not dare delay.
If summoned again, respond with order.
As the *XuanDu* decree commands, so it is done.

**Seal of the Thunderfire Marshal**
**Right:** This seal is recited with the preceding ritual. Two hands form the *QiLe* seal, recite one hundred times, absorb the Thunder *qi*, and store it in the **Pure Bottle**. Seal the bottle’s mouth with the talisman.
For treating illness or subduing demons, a resonant reply will come immediately.
**End of the Tenth Scroll of the Supreme Daoist Canon of the Highest Heavenly *ShenXiao*玉清真王.**
**Beginning of the Eleventh Scroll of the Supreme Daoist Canon of the Highest Heavenly *ShenXiao*玉清真王.**

**Secret Method for Invoking Rain at the Divine Storehouse**

For invoking rain, when erecting the altar, one must not allow monks, nuns, women, filial sons, impure persons, or those involved in slaughter to wander about. The laborers who build the altar should ideally be fed plain vegetarian meals.

If one desires a swift and resonant response, the local magistrate must be instructed to prohibit the tolling of bells, beating of drums, or playing of cymbals within the city walls.

After three days, the rain will descend immediately.

Additionally, when issuing the talisman at midnight, one must offer money, horses, wine, and fruit to appease the Thunder **Deity** and express the intent of the invocation.

**Opening the Celestial Gate**

When performing this ritual, the Daoist master must wear black garments, let his hair hang loose, carry a black banner on his shoulder, and hold a mouthful of pure water. Facing northeast, he spits once and shouts aloud, reciting the *Opening the Celestial Gate* incantation:

*"Ten thousand deities aid the clouds,
Heavenly officials lend their power.
Ghosts traverse rivers and lakes—
Guard the sun for my sake.
Three Marshals exchange their stations,
All deities rush forth in haste.
Heaven and Earth tremble,
Sun and Moon falter and decline.
Meteors drive back the throng,
Demons reveal their true forms.
My words pierce the day,
Swiftly done as the **Supreme Sovereign’s** decree."*

**Right:** Using the left hand to form the *Hai* seal, recite seven times. Then shake and sway the black banner toward the Celestial Gate. Stand with sword’s tip drawn to the ground, and spray the area seven times with wine.

Next, form the *Sealing the Celestial Gate* mudra, and blow upward toward the Celestial Gate with a single breath. Afterward, recite the *Opening the Celestial Gate* incantation.

For summoning wind and rain, each may be invoked seven times.

**Examples of Responsive Rainfall**

Spring thunder arises in the **Leopard’s Court** (寅) and **Tiger’s Court** (卯) of the Central Palace.
Summer thunder strikes in the **Shocking Court** (震) and **Windward Court** (巽) between the **Snake’s Court** (巳) and **Horse’s Court** (午).

In autumn, thunder returns to the **Elemental Court** (申) and **Rooster’s Court** (酉) of its original station.
In winter, it ascends from the **Dog’s Court** (亥) to the **Rat’s Court** (子) at the cycle’s end.

In all four seasons, clouds gather and rain falls—
At **Dragon’s Court** (辰), **Dog’s Court** (戌), **Ox’s Court** (丑), and **Sheep’s Court** (未), the **Heavenly Barrier** opens.

This is the incantation, also used to dispatch the luminaries of the dawn.

**Talisman for Overturning the Sea**

*Right talisman*: Forge with **raw iron** (生铁), shaping a board **19 inches long** (一尺九寸), **3.3 inches thick** (厚三寸三分), and **7 inches wide** (阔七寸).
Within the **two talismans**, inscribe in **sequential vermilion script** (次朱书) one layer, or write on both sides, and cast it into the **river source where dragons dwell** (河源有龙所在). If no dragon abides there, first draw a dragon and submerge it in water. After some time, cast the talisman.
Following the **ritual steps of the Hexagram’s Array** (步罡行持), shortly thereafter, **heavy rain will descend instantly** (大雨立至).

**Dispatching Talisman Incantation:**
Six Ding, Six Jia,
Five Thunder Marshals and Officers (五雷将吏).
Wind Lord and Rain Master (风伯雨师),
Thunder Commanderies’ Sacred Assembly (雷部圣众).
Long overdue rains and blessings (久愆雨泽),
I pray for Your grace and salvation (愿赐救护).
When the **Heavenly Talisman arrives** (天符一到),
All will be universally rescued from drought (普济焦枯).
Swiftly, as the **Heavenly Sovereign’s Commandments** (上帝律令).

*Right*: Pinch the **Five Thunder Talisman** (掐五雷诀), recite it **forty-nine times** (诵四十九遍), cast its talisman, and **rain will descend instantly** (使雨立至).

**Nine Dragon Talisman**

*Ritual Method:*
If drought persists, at a **flowing water source or dragon pool** (流水龙潭处),
Hold the **Chenwen Talisman** (辰文) in your left hand,
Grasp a pen in your right hand,
Conceive of your **original teacher** (本师) before you,
And your **ancestral teacher** (祖师) behind you.
With the pen in the water, inscribe the **Nine Dragon Talisman** (九龙符) once,
Using the following incantation to write it.

*Incantation:*
Eastern Dragon Lord (东方龙君),
Southern Dragon Lord (南方龙君),
Western Dragon Lord (西方龙君),
Northern Dragon Lord (北方龙君),
I bear the **Heavenly Sovereign’s Command** (奉上帝勑命),
Assisting **Heaven in its transformations** (佐天行化),
Rescuing and guiding all living beings (救度群生).
Now I come to **this place** (某处),
Where the **High Star clashes with Metal and Gold Fire** (亢星金火相克).
I now inscribe the **seal talisman and scripture** (篆符箓),
Summoning and binding the **cloud dragons** (摄召云龙),
Swiftly unleashing their **mighty powers** (速逞威灵).
Let the rains soak the earth,
Instantly revive the **sprouting crops and rice** (立苏苗稻).
Let the **ears of grain form and mature** (吐穗结实),
And safeguard the **foundations of prosperity** (保崴元亨).
Swiftly, as the **Heavenly Sovereign’s Commandments** (上帝律令).

*Right*: Pinch the **Chenwen Talisman** (掐辰文),
Recite the incantation **forty-nine times** (诵呎四十九遍),
Inscribe the talisman **three times** (书符三次),
And **response will be immediate** (立应).

*Incantation:*
Dark Heaven resounds (玄天荡荡),
Dark Origin clears the mist (玄元雾清).
Pure and wondrous **movement** (妙运),
Stabilizing and pacifying the **years and seasons** (安镇年龄).
Original Beginning opens the **True Dao** (元始开真),
The **Rectified Way flows bright** (正道流明).
Nurturing Heaven commands Earth (营天勑地),
Ten Heavens tremble in awe (十天骇惊).
Divine efficacy summons (神功摄召),
Ten thousand demons bound in form (万魔束形).
Encompassing the **Four Symbols** (周盖四象),
Wind and Fire dare not halt (风火敢停).
Shaking the **Six Heavens** (威震六天),
Wild **Dao** (ways) will not arise (野道不生).
Dark Talisman’s Command arrives (玄符勑到),
Subduing fierce warriors (役使刚兵).

Gold flows, lightning strikes (流金激电),
Wind and Fire are crushed (风火摧明).
Swiftly, as the **Commandments** (律令).

**Twenty-Four Command Talisman Incantation:**

The **Twenty-Four Divine Ones**, each wielding their might (二十四神各有威力).
Where **Qi** gathers, malevolent spirits are oppressed (炁所示郁峨鬼),
The **Three Ganges** subdue and seal the **Nine Minutiae** (三罡所摄镇九微).
Spirit-born **Qi** pursues water, opening its own mechanism (灵生逐水自开机),

Through kalpas ever preserved, ever remembered (历劫常存常追思).
Swiftly, as the **Commandments** (急急如律令).

**Deploying the Twenty-Four Command Talisman:**
The **Mysterious Reflection radiates** (玄映流耀),
The **Five Directions’ Divine Lords** (五方神公) are summoned.
To **crush the mountains** (策山之摧),
To **drain the waters** (策水之竭).

To **annihilate the demons** (策妖妖亡).
The **Four Cardinal Directions and Ten Directions** (四维十方),
All spirits safeguarded (万灵保当).
After donning the talisman,
One may traverse the **Ten Constant Realms** (任遍十常).
Form and spirit steadfastly guarded,
Unharmed through ten kalpas (万劫无伤).
Swiftly, as the **Commandments** (急急如律令).

**Talisman Invocation to Drive the Ding-Jia:**
By **Heavenly Sovereign’s Decree** (上帝有命),

On **Yang Days**, use to drive the **Six Jia** (右法，阳日，驱六甲用).
On **Yang-Fighting Days**, use to drive the **Six Ding** (阳斗阴日，驱六丁用).
On **Yin-Fighting Days**, perform the **Yú Steps** (阴斗，禹步为之).

*"Incantation:"* (次收 咒曰：)

**Yang-Fighting Steps & Yin-Fighting Steps Talisman:**
*"Incantation for Yang-Fighting and Yin-Fighting"* (阳斗步斗咒):
White and black, **mixed chaos** (混沌) douses my form,
The **Yú Steps** (禹步) urge me toward **Bright Clarity** (登阳明).
**Heaven revolves, Earth turns** (天回地转), stepping the **Seven Stars** (步七星),

Every **demon** (一切邪魔) vanishes in form.

I attain **longevity**, ascending to **Upper Clarity** (朝上清).
Swiftly, as the **Heavenly Sovereign’s Commandments** (急急如上帝律令勑).

**Yin-Fighting Method:**
On **Yin-Fighting Days** (阴斗), **right** (右),
Take the **Lunar Loom’s qi** (取罡炁),
On **Yang Days** (阳日), use the **left-hand Master’s Seal** (左手本师诀),
Emerging from **Yang** into **Yin-Fighting** (自阳出阴斗).
On **Yin Days** (阴日), face from **Yin-Fighting** toward **Yang-Fighting** (自阴斗向阳斗).

**Ritual for Sacrificing to the Thunder:**
For all **Thunder sacrifices** (祭雷),
Within the **twelve months of a year** (十二月内),
Must select the **Six Bing Days** (六丙日), the **Thunder Assembly’s Days** (雷会之日).
Three days prior, **fast and purify** (斋戒),
**Strictly cleanse** (严洁),
Wear **new and pure garments** (着新浄衣),
Enter the **altar’s sacred precinct** (入靖),
Burn **incense** (焚香) and **proclaim** (启告) to the **ancestral Master** (祖师),
**Report to the Celestial Court** (奏申天省),
Prepare **documents** (备牒) for the **Thunder Department’s officials** (雷部官众),
**Local City Deities** (本属城隍),
**Community Marshals** (社令),
**Altar’s Sacred Land Deities** (坛靖土地),
All **verify and respond** (咸析证应).
Next, **proclaim and request** (伸启请) the **Supreme Sacred Master** (上圣师真),
**Thunderous Marshals and Attendants** (雷霆将吏),
**Thunder Master, the Radiant Old One** (雷师皓翁),
**Thunder Lord** (雷公),
**Lightning Mother** (电母),
**Wind Lord** (风伯),
**Rain Master Deities** (雨师神君),
**Sudden Fire Great Immortal** (欻火大仙),
**Black Teeth’s Fierce Attendants** (苍牙猛吏),
**Thunder Marshal Heavenly Deities** (雷令天神),
**Thunderous Mighty Deities** (震威大神),
**Thunder Chariot and Thunder Fire Deities** (雷车雷火神君),
**Thunder Department’s Judges** (雷部判官),
**Thunder Light Messengers** (雷光使者),
**Torch-Bearing Child Attendants** (执幢童子),
**Direct Seal, Purple Light Child Attendants** (直印紫光童子),
**Five Cardinal Five Thunder Deities and Soldiers** (五方五雷神兵),
**Divine Generals of the Five Directions** (当司神将),
**Five Thunder Messengers** (五雷使者),
**Six Jia Generals** (六甲将军),
**Six Ding Talisman Messengers** (六丁符使),
**Dragon King’s Followers** (龙王部众),
**River and Stream Messengers** (江河使者),
**Thunder Deities that Move Wind, Spread Rain, Emit Mist, and Stir Clouds** (行风布雨吐雾兴云雷神),
**City Deities** (城隍),
**Community Marshals** (社令),
**Direct Day’s Functionary Attendants** (直日功曹),
**Direct Altar’s Sacred Land Deities** (直坛土地),
And all other **deities** (等神),
**Universally grant descent and presence** (普赐降临).
At the same time, **offer sacrifices** (同时祭献),
Arrange and **present offerings** (罗列供物).
Three **libations of wine** (三奠酒),
**Prayer and declaration of intent** (梼祝白意).
**Humbly beseech** (伏乞) the descent of **divine manifestation** (降灵),
**Protect and assist** (护助行持) my **ritual observance** (行持).
For the **nation** (国) and **people** (民),
**Petition for rain and clear skies** (祈祷雨旸).
**Grant me divine response** (愿赐感应),
**Greatly manifest the Mysterious Wind** (丕阐玄风).
After the **sacrifice concludes** (祭毕),
**Transform money** (化钱).
For all **Thunder sacrifices** (祭雷神),
**Must be performed with sincere resolve** (切须志诚).
**Thereafter**, all **petitions and supplications** (祈祷),
**Shall be answered without fail** (无不感应也).

**Five Thunder Seals:**
**Heavenly Thunder Seal** (天雷诀):
Both hands pinch **Yin** (寅),
All five fingers **conceal within the palm** (五指俱藏於甲).
**Divine Thunder Seal** (神雷诀):
Second and third fingers **bowed like a bow** (弓),
**Great finger pinches Ding** (大指掐定子),
Fourth and fifth fingers **press down the Great finger** (压定大指).
**Celestial Dipper Thunder Seal** (斗雷诀):
The **Great Celestial Dipper Seal** (大斗诀) is this.
**Dragon Thunder Seal** (龙雷诀):
Second, third, and fourth fingers **bowed like a bow** (弓),
**Great finger also bowed** (弓),
Pinch **Ding at Hai** (掐定亥),
Fifth finger **pinches the Great finger** (掐定大指),
**Conceal within the palm** (藏甲).
**Water Thunder Seal** (水雷诀):
Second finger **bowed like a bow** (弓),
**Great finger pinches Chou** (掐丑),
Third, fourth, and fifth fingers **press down the Great finger** (押定大指).
**Demon Thunder Seal** (妖雷诀):
Second, third, and fourth fingers **bowed like a bow** (弓),
**Great finger pinches Ding** (掐定),
**No palm concealment** (并不见甲),
This is called the **Community Marshal’s Thunder** (社令雷也).

**Grand Ritual for Summoning the Celestial Thunder:**
*"Ritual Law"* (法曰):
Before the **summoning** (摄召),
**First sacrifice nine days prior** (先於九日前祭之),
Use **Three-Lichen and Ginseng Decoction** (参苓汤),
**Clear wine** (清酒),
**Pure fruits** (浄果),
**Wax tea** (腊茶).
Burn many **talismans of the original form** (多烧本形符),
**Pray at the incense burner** (祝於几日),
Summoning rituals are **declared** (摄召事云).
Burn **paper money, horses, and other offerings** (烧钱马等),
On the **summoning day** (於摄召日).
First, at a **pure ground** (浄地),
**Establish the meal for summoning spirits** (立摄灵之膳),
Use a **green banner** (青旛) of **one standard** (一首),
**Nine zhang long** (长九尺),
**Nine cun wide** (阔九寸).
**Set the summoning complete** (安摄召毕),
Together with **paper talismans**, burn them.
**Total Summoning Functionary Attendants Incantation** (总召功曹咒).

**Celestial Thunder: Ritual Law of the Celestial Dawn (神霄) Summoning**

*"Finger Pressures"* (指押):
Press firmly on the **Great Finger** (大指).
**Celestial Thunder Incantation** (妖雷诀):
Bend the **Second, Third, and Fourth Fingers** (二、三、四指) into a bow,
Press firmly on the **Great Finger** (大指掐定),
So that no knuckle is visible—
This is called the **Village Marshal’s Thunder** (社令雷).

**Great Ritual of the Celestial Dawn (神霄玉清王) Summoning**

*"Ritual Law"* (法曰):
Before the **summoning** (摄召),
**First sacrifice nine days prior** (先於九日前祭之),
Use **Three-Lichen and Ginseng Decoction** (参苓汤),
**Clear wine** (清酒),
**Pure fruits** (浄果),
**Wax tea** (腊茶).
Burn many **talismans of the original form** (本形符),
**Pray at the incense burner** (祝於几日),
Summoning rituals are **declared** (摄召事云).
Burn **paper money, horses, and other offerings** (钱马等),
On the **summoning day** (於摄召日).
First, at a **pure ground** (浄地),
**Establish the meal for summoning spirits** (立摄灵之膳),
Use a **green banner** (青旛) of **one standard** (一首),
**Nine zhang long** (长九尺),
**Nine cun wide** (阔九寸).
**Set the summoning complete** (安摄召毕),
Together with **paper talismans**, burn them.

**Total Summoning Functionary Attendants Incantation** (总召功曹咒):
*"O, Celestial Dawn Jade-Purity King* (神霄玉清王),
Today by **decree** (勑下),
Descend from the **Ninth Heaven** (九霄).
**Command the spirits, summon the spirits** (命神召神),
**Oversee the Functionary Attendants** (摄掌功曹).
**Jade Scripts spread the proclamation** (玉文敷告),
In accordance with the **Heavenly Precepts** (应天条).
I practice the **True Talismans** (真箓),
**Pursue my Three-Lichen and Ginseng Decoction** (逐我参调).
Swiftly, as the **Highest Celestial Dawn True King’s Commandments** (高上神霄玉清真王律令),
I earnestly request the **Celestial Dawn Certain Dao Functionary Attendants** (神霄某道功曹主者),
Swiftly attend at the **altar** (赴坛所).
**Right Ritual**: Press the **fingers and script** (掐辰文),
First visualize the **True Form** (想真形),
Write the **talisman and burn the ashes** (书符烧灰).
**Recite the incantation**, gather the **perverse qi** (巽炁),
Blow upon the **sick person** (吹病人),
**Enter the realm and report** (入境自报).
**Swallow it for a hundred days** (吞之百日),
Its effect shall be **as resonant as a reply** (其应如响).

**Summoning Talisman of the Heavenly Dao Functionary Attendants** (召天道功曹符):
**Heavenly Dao Functionary Attendants** (天道功曹), **Light-Bearer** (将光辅), **One Hundred and Twenty** (百二十人).

*"Incantation"* (咒曰):
**By decree of the Ninth Heaven** (九天之勑),
O **Great Dao Ancestral Lord** (大道祖君).
**Creating forms within the Radiant Realm** (造象昊境),
**Thirty-Two Pure Ones** (三十二清).
**Following the Commandments by Law** (奉命随法),
**Enter the Supreme Mystic Dao** (入上玄真).

**Right Ritual**: Within the **incense burner** (香炉内),
Burn the **summoning prayer** (烧召祝之).
Use a **dispatch talisman** (牒差功曹),
Request the **Heavenly Dao Command** (请命天道),
**Merge and descend the True Spirits** (合降真灵),
**Dispatch with the intent of the ritual hall** (牒书斋意).
Again, use **one talisman** (符一道),
Burn it together.

This **Functionary Attendant** (功曹),
Knows the **secrets of the Heavenly Palace and Purple Treasury** (天宫紫府秘禁),
**Eclipses of the Sun and Moon** (日月交蚀),
**Stars filling and emptying their orbits** (星辰盈阙),
**Auspicious winds and rains** (风雨吉祥),
**Oversees the Dao Repository and Heavenly Dao disasters** (掌管神府天道灾变).
If one wishes to **inquire and summon** (问召摄),
All shall be known.

**Summoning Talisman of the Earthly Dao Functionary Attendants** (召地道功曹符):
**Earthly Dao Functionary Attendants** (地道功曹), **Liu Kang** (刘罡), **One Hundred and Twenty** (百二十人).

*"Incantation"* (咒曰):
**Penetrating the Mystic Dao’s Essence** (洞玄品品),
**Layer upon layer, transforming into forms** (垒垒化形).
**Five Yangs respond thoroughly** (五阳彻应),
**Ten Extremes of the Profound Darkness** (十极幽冥).

**Dispatch with the intent of the ritual hall** (牒书斋意).
Again, use **one talisman** (符一道),
Burn it together.

This **Functionary Attendant** (功曹),
Oversees the **Nine Layers of Water and Earth** (九垒水土),
**Grains and crops** (禾苗),

All shall be known.

**Total Summoning Functionary Attendants Incantation** (总召功曹咒):
*"Mystic Dao Jade Scripts"* (玄曹玉文),
**Establish the Functionary Attendants** (立功之官).
**Oversee the Jade Purity Dao** (主治玉清),
**Report to the Three Heavens** (奏报三天).

**Decree from the Supreme Dao:**

*"The Celestial Sovereign commands—
Swiftly descend the divine light!
With solemn reverence, I summon the **Functionary Attendant** of [specific rank], to act in accordance with the law."*

**Urgent Ritual Procedure:**
Pinch the **hourly talisman script** (掐辰文), gather the **perverse qi** (巽炁), and invoke them.

**Beheading-Evil Functionaries** (斩邪功曹) – one hundred twenty.
**Pursuit Functionaries** (追捉功曹) – one hundred twenty.
**Binding-Delivery Functionaries** (缚送功曹) – one hundred twenty.
**Name-Fixing Functionaries** (定名功曹) – one hundred twenty.
**Joyous Jade-Calendar Functionaries** (喜玉历功曹) – one hundred twenty.

All Functionaries wear **hooded robes**, **crimson garments with wide sleeves**, and **black-and-green sashes**.
Write the talisman and summon them.

Each day, they stand duty at the altar, leading **soldiers and cavalry** (勾兵马从), each with their assigned roles.
Whether submitting petitions to inspect the **celestial registers** (勘会仙籍),
pursuing malevolent spirits (追捉邪祟),
or treating and beheading evil—
all may be employed by them.

**Functionary Summons Formula (引式):**
*"Highest Dao: Celestial Constellation Jade-Purity True King’s Palace, Subordinate Office:*
This office now, for the matter of **[specific purpose]**, summons **one hundred twenty Disease-Treating Functionaries** (治病功曹) to urgently proceed to **[location]**, to heal **[patient’s] affliction within [timeframe]. How shall they act?**

With solemn decree to the **Disease-Treating Functionaries**:
We invoke the **Nine-Heaven Exalted Physician Officials** (九天扁鹊官吏), the **Heavenly Doctors and Divine Immortals** (天医神仙).
The **Pharmaceutical Attendant Youth** (尚药童子), **Divine-Responsive Preserver of Mysteries** (神应保玄).
**Dan-herbs cure disease**, **jade essence prolongs life**.
A hundred ailments vanish swiftly, ten thousand maladies find no foothold.
**Transmit the debt of the dead**, subdue the malevolent corpse—
**rebellious forces perish swiftly**, the afflicted restored to peace.
**Celestial Constellation’s decree**—all meridians healed.
*Urgent, as the law commands.*

**Year of the Celestial Stem** [太岁], **Month**, **Day**, **Hour**,
By decree of the Celestial Constellation, dispatched.
**Rank:** [具位], **Name:** [姓某], **Seal.**

**Soul-Pursuit, Spirit-Summoning, Ghost-Subduing Talisman (追魂摄魄降灵符):**
**Incantation:**
*"Nine times nine—perfected numbers,
Cosmic transformation before Heaven.
The Five Phases revolve—all life sustained.
The Great Dao nourishes—all things complete.
*Urgent, as the Highest Celestial Constellation Jade-Purity True King’s law commands.*"

**Ritual:**
Write this talisman on the **summoning banner**.
Use a **white banner**, three *chi* three *cun* in length,
with the **deceased’s name** inscribed on one side.
Next, the **priestess of souls** (魂婶) holds the incense burner,
burning the **Return-Soul, Subdue-Spirit, Descend-Ghost Talisman** (返魂摄魄降灵符).
As the banner grows heavy, when reaching the **deceased’s resting place**,
the spirit shall **manifest in form**.

**Urgent Manifestation Incantation (催现咒):**
*"Pursue the soul, subdue the spirit—
Swiftly descend, O spirit-bearer!
The **Northern Dipper’s canopy** opens,
**Playful Tortoise** guards the gate.
**Vermilion Bird** stands watch,
**Azure Dragon** transforms.
**White Tiger** bears witness—
all spirits secure.
When the **sacred instrument arrives**,
**manifest before our eyes!**
*Urgent, as the Highest Celestial Constellation Jade-Purity True King’s law commands.*"

**Ritual:**
Pinch the **hourly talisman script**, gather the **perverse qi**, and blow the brush.
If the spirit has not yet manifested,
recite this incantation to **urge its appearance**—
**it shall immediately take form**.

universally extract the suffering souls.
