---
**Dissolving the Form (散形):**
*"Primordial Command, Universal Vital Qi—
Proclaim to the Three Realms, all crossing thresholds, celestial hosts:
**Wind and Marsh, Hollow and Void—ten thousand qi, all immortalized!**
**Primordial Cavern, Jade-Calendar**—
**dead souls receive rebirth**.
**Nine Abysses, spectral purity**—
**severed from earthly roots**.
**Rebirth at the appointed hour**—
**ascend to transcendence**.
**Three Officials, Nine Registries**—
**reduce malevolent karmic roots**.
**Drawn from the earthly gate**—
**nine ancestors ascend to immortality.**"

**Gathering the Form (聚形):**
*"By the Jade-Purity Decree—
universally extract the suffering souls.
When **celestial light shines once**,
guilt and karma melt like ice.
Urgent, as the Highest Celestial Constellation Jade-Purity True King’s decree."*

**Again, the Talisman Decree Spell:**
*"Suffering souls, so many in sorrow—
pain demands divine contemplation.
O Celestial Lord of Jade-Purity,
your **true-gold talisman** shines resplendent.
**Crash open the abyssal gates**—
release you from your spectral prison.
**Drawn forth and liberated**—
from depths to heights, reborn.
**By Heaven’s honed blade**, refined—
ascend to the **Dan Court** of transformation.
Urgent, as the Highest Celestial Constellation Jade-Purity True King and Heavenly Sovereign’s decree."*

**Celestial Constellation Talisman to Shatter the Underworld (神霄破地狱符勑笔咒):**
*"Jade-Purity Heavenly Sovereign,
proclaims to the Jade-Purity below.
By **Primordial Decree**—
**urgent compliance is commanded.**
To the **Nine Abysses and Dark Realms**,
to **Yin and Du’s great gods**,
to **sacred peaks for judgment**,
to the **Watery Courts of Law**—
all ten directions submit,
all forms obey.
**Guilty departed souls**—
by Heaven’s will, you are pardoned.
Urgent, as the Highest Celestial Constellation Jade-Purity True King and Heavenly Sovereign’s decree."*

**Method:**
*"This ritual—pinch the hour-mark, take **black qi**, blow upon the brush, and inscribe.
**Dissolving the Form (散形):**
At the **Nine Abysses’ cold night**, no longer sinking—
in the **spectral chasms’ depths**, swiftly behold the radiance.
**Shattering the Nine Fortresses**, how dare they not follow?
Obeying the Emperor’s iron decree—
**wind and thunder disperse**, the **fire-physician’s pool** transforms.
**Chill darkness yields to warmth**, all-pervasive grace—
**fire-chariots’ flames extinguish**, the **cauldron’s boiling ceases**.
**Copper Pillars collapse**, slaughter halts.
By **Primordial Decree**, the talisman arrives—
**souls depart from Yin and Tai**, **spirits escape the iron enclosure**.
Guilty or innocent—**urgent pardon**, no defiance.
The **Three Realms’ sentinels**, ten thousand gods, respectfully comply.
**Exhortation Talisman (劝符呎):**
Jade-Purity Celestial—
**pierce the spectral shoulders**.
**Bitter cold springs**, **deep abysses overflow**.
O **Yin and Du’s god-kings**—
by talisman’s summons, all halt.
**Jailers and officers**—
proclaim Heaven’s sacred will.
By **True Scripture’s Dao-transformation**—
**shatter the earthly barriers**.
**Sacred Light proclaims**—
**wandering spirits shift form**.
**Sacred Light shines once**—
**Celestial Constellation seizes the soul**.
Beneath Heaven’s radiance—
**universally liberate the lost spirits**.
By **Jade-Purity’s sovereign decree**—
**crush what dares not yield**.
**Gate-opening Generals**, by **Imperial Command**—
**reveal forms swiftly**, ten thousand ghosts manifest.
**Northern Emperor’s True Light**—
**pierces the spectral darkness**.
**O lost souls, lost souls**—
all attain illumination.
By **Jade-Purity’s decree**—
command the **Three Officials**.
**Nine Departments, Four Bureaus**,
**Five Peaks, Nine Abysses**,
**Six Caverns, Ten Palaces**,
**Abyssal and Curved Courts**—
O **Yin and Du’s rulers**,
follow this decree today.
**Universally release the departed**—
**free from the Underworld’s grasp**.
Urgent, as the law commands."*

**Combined Decree of the Two Talismans:**
*"By **Celestial Constellation’s Decree**—
command the **Nine Abysses**.
All **heavenly officers**—
by talisman’s arrival, act.
**All guilty souls**—
pardoned, ascend to Heaven.
Urgent, as the Highest Celestial Constellation Jade-Purity True King and Heavenly Sovereign’s decree."*

**Method:**
*"Before invoking these two talismans,
first kneel before the **Three Treasures**, petitioning.
After proclaiming the decree,
**seal the Celestial Constellation’s earthly registrar**,
carrying them forth—
or to the **Five Sacred Peaks**, **Yin and Du’s Northern Bureau**, **Abyssal and Watery Gates**—
broadly proclaim.
To reclaim the departed,
this is the talismans’ power."*

**Jade-Purity’s Three Heavenly Lords’ Supreme True Talisman (玉清三天君上元玉简真符):**
*"Three **qi** surge as smoke—
**clear qi** spreads in four directions.
A hundred million ancestors’ suffering souls,
their **bitter chasms** now extinguished—
by **Taiyin’s recorded day**, refined and liberated,
**ascend to immortality**.
Guilt and virtue, prohibitions, fate—
all receive **universal liberation**.
**Departed souls regain life**—
hearing Heaven’s proclamation.
**Decree Spell:**
O **Great One of Taiyi**,
**gather the True Qi**.
**Taiyi preserves life**,
**stabilizes the spirit**, secures birth.
For me, **draw Jade-Purity’s Qi above**,
**spread the Purple Gate’s court below**.
**Jade Scripture ascends**, **mud-ball radiance brightens**.
**Seven Ancestors rejoice together**—
all ascend to **Upper Purity**.
Only wish—**enter the formless**.
**Simplified Talisman:**
Three Heaven’s **white tablets**,
Jade-Purity’s **jade talisman**."*

**Proclamation to the Highest Heaven, Left and Right Wardens, Registrars, and Sovereign Gods of the Celestial Prisons:**

*"I hereby proclaim and liberate [Name], extinguishing great offenses and sealing perverse origins.
May form and spirit ascend and transcend—
paying homage at the Celestial Sovereign’s gate.
Wisdom and fortune spontaneously arise,
serving the Dragon-Chariot in boundless ease.
Free from constraint, the True Dao endures forever.
As decreed by this proclamation,
transmitted by wind and fire messengers.
In the year of the Great Year, month, day,
this tablet was inscribed at the Daoist hall at an auspicious hour.
This tablet, crafted from *xiang* wood,
seven inches long, four inches wide, three *fen* thick,
was used to elevate ancient emperors and empresses.
For liberating departed souls, separate proclamation texts are provided."*

**Nine-Heaven Inner-Sound Treasure Edict**
**Mid-Autumn Golden Script Seal**
**Imperial Decree Spell:**

*"O Sovereign of the Imperial Court, Encountering the True Qi of the Daoist Sage!
The Sovereign’s degree-symbol registers,
rectifying the black to summon ten thousand spirits.
Above, I summon the True Qi of Jade-Purity,
filling and spreading between the two brows.
From the Primordial Void, the Imperial Form emerges,
three pure essences forming my transcendence.
Feasting on the gale, ascending on the flying canopy,
directly rising to the Highest Pavilion.

**Ritual of Refining and Liberating the Soul**

**Fire-Refinement Method:**
Use eighteen *zhuózi* tablets, arranged in a single row.
On each tablet, place a censer with blazing fire and burning incense.
Refine from the crown to the vital-symbol—eighteen stages.
Recite the *Yùqīng* incantation, chanting the appropriate spell for each stage, burning it in the censer’s flames.

**Water-Refinement Method:**
Use a pool of water, nine inches or nine feet in dimension—always a multiple of nine. Constructed of metal, stone, wood, or brick.
Pour nine measures of water, placing censers at each corner with blazing fire and incense, shrouding the pool in mist.
The ritual master intones the invocation, casting the *liánshēnfú* (body-refinement talisman) into the water, commanding the officiant to perceive the soul of the deceased.
If unseen, repeat with the *cuī* (urgent) incantation.
If the soul does not manifest human form—or appears as a beast—return to fire-refinement.
If human form is achieved, proceed with the ritual rites, crossing the Daoist bridge to the Birth-Heaven platform.
Adapt as needed.

**Divine Highest’s Scripture on Preserving the Transcendent and Dispelling Demons to Protect the Orthodox Rites**

**The Divine King Speaks:**
Worthy scholars in the world must believe in the Dao, revere the Heavenly Will, and harmonize with the spirits.
Devote to loyalty and filial piety, commit no evil, and cultivate the great root of virtue.
All actions should aid in liberating all beings.
Without relying on precepts and vows, how can one uphold the path?

In ancient times, the Ancestor of Yang, the Great Red High Wall of the *Tai Ji*, the Purple Clarity Palace’s True Primordial Divine Treasure of Great Compassion, transmitted to me the supreme Dao and instructed those who seek transcendence.
The Dao’s foundation is gradual; precepts come first.
Precious standards and refined laws—secret scriptures of the Purple Palace—list the Seven Grades of Precepts and classify the Nine Levels of Scripture.
Thus, the *Yun* seals and double *Luo* talismans, the jade seals and flower-bound registers,
The wise platform and jade gate—nine tiers of celestial realms—illuminate all hidden things, liberating all without exception.

Precepts begin at the initial stage, restraining desires and suppressing transgressions, gradually ascending to sainthood.
Now, those who earnestly study must follow the law’s procedures, facing the sacred presence.
As those entrusted with the Dao’s duties, first proclaim the Nine Precepts of the Nine Constellations and Nine Celestial Exaltations to clarify the merit of the ritual.
All officials must sincerely repent and listen attentively.

**The Wisdom Praise:**

1. **The Divine Highest of the Nine Constellations, Eternal Heavenly Long-Life, and Supreme Virtue** proclaims the **Precept Against Demons**.
   Reflect on the Mysterious Sovereign’s wondrous Dao, giving birth to the Two Principles.
   The Three Constellations’ primordial function creates all things.
   Divine spirits and transcendent sages assist in generation.
   Do not be deceived by the silence of barbarians or the emptiness of the void.
   Do not arrogantly exalt yourself, lest you fall into demonic realms.
   Those who uphold this precept attain the fruit of flying ascent.

2. **The Dao-Master of the Dan Constellation, the Peaceful and Transformative Sovereign** proclaims the **Precept Against Evil**.
   Reflect on emperors and kings receiving talismans to govern the people.
   The Dao transforms the ten directions, and benevolence nurtures the four seas.
   Do not trust in deceit or harbor malicious intent.
   Do not indulge in licentiousness or deceit, lest you fall into evil destinies.
   Those who uphold this precept attain the fruit of wealth and nobility.

3. **The Elemental True Treasure of the Qing Constellation, the Good-Generating Sovereign** proclaims the **Precept of Nurturing Nature**.
   Reflect on the toil and nurturing love of parents.
   Always cherish filial piety and modesty, obeying with reverence.
   Do not rebel, lest you fall into hell.
   Those who uphold this precept attain the fruit of longevity.

4. **The Cloud-Opening Dao-Transmitting Sovereign of the Bi Constellation, the All-Generating Sovereign** proclaims the **Precept of Cultivating the Body**.
   Reflect that Heaven generates all things, nourishing all beings.
   Borrowed temporarily, do not be stingy.
   Always distribute wealth to aid the poor.
   If greedy and covetous, you will sink into ruin.
   Those who uphold this precept attain the fruit of abundance.

5. **The Crystal-Shining,威德耀晶天尊 of the Yu Constellation** proclaims the **Precept of Upright Mind**.
   Reflect that all beings share the primordial black essence.
   Through karma and conditions, they manifest diverse forms.
   Do not indulge in desires for tastes, nor commit harm.
   Nor rely on arrogance to oppress the lowly.
   Harbor no malicious intent, lest you be bound in cyclic suffering.
   Those who uphold this precept attain the fruit of wisdom.

6. **The Flowing Light, Pure Radiance Sovereign of the Tai Constellation** proclaims the **Precept of Calm Reflection**.
   Reflect that chasing honor and luxury harms life and nature.
   Lust and depravity corrupt the vital essence and disrupt authenticity.
   Worldly laws cannot tolerate this, and retribution is severe.
   Fleeting illusions offer no escape—eternally without release.
   Obsessive thoughts ensnare; one falls into torment.
   Those who uphold this precept attain the fruit of purity.

7. **The Universal Aid Sovereign of the Lang Constellation, the Flying Green Primordial Key** proclaims the **Precept of Caution**.
   Reflect that all beings strive with wisdom.
   Do not assume ignorance justifies hatred or jealousy.

---

8. **The Double Splendor Sovereign of the Purple Constellation** proclaims the **Precept of Guarding and Protecting**.
   Reflect that the **Thunderous Deity** guards and protects with awe-inspiring radiance.
   If entering a **Treasure Mountain**, one must concentrate the mind and remain unmoved.
   Do not assume that those of different **Dao/Way** are unworthy of association or shared dwelling.
   Interfering with **evil paths** leads to **slackening and retreat**.
   Those who uphold this precept attain the fruit of **steadfastness**.

9. **The Most Wondrous Void Sovereign of the Central Constellation** proclaims the **Precept of Benefiting Others**.
   Reflect that within the **dusty world**, all beings—**sentient life**—receive retribution according to their deeds, enduring manifold **sufferings**.
   Thus, one must arouse the **Great Compassion and Mercy**, employing **skillful means** to rescue and liberate them.
   Even for minor kindnesses, one must accumulate them diligently, avoiding **procrastination** or **indulgence in neglect**.
   Those who uphold this precept attain the fruit of **fulfilling the True Primordial Essence**.

The **True King** declares:
From the **Nine Precepts of the Great Primordial** above, if one can **begin and end** by upholding them, **never slackening** throughout life, **internalizing** the suppression of **demons and bewitchments**, and **externalizing** the gathering of **True Spirits**, while **observing strict fasts** and **purifying thoughts**, advancing in **superior Dao/Way**, then all **wicked and violent** forces shall be unable to approach.
One may **command the Six Ding** to **ward off** and **banish** all evils.
When the **merit is complete** and the **fruit is fulfilled**, one shall **ascend to immortality in broad daylight**.

How can one not uphold these precepts? How can one not strive?

**Daoists** observing **fasts** and **ritual conduct** must **report to the Sacred Pass** and **White Court**.
The **Superintendent of Rituals** and **Ceremonial Masters** shall **bow three times** before exiting, and do likewise upon returning.
Those who violate this shall be **reprimanded by the Master** and **punished without reprieve**.

**Procedures of the Jade Bureau**:
When commoners submit petitions to **exorcise maddening and malevolent spirits**, one must **investigate thoroughly**, ensuring the presence of **ghosts or bandits**.
After judging the petition, **offer incense** and **recite aloud** to the **Ancestral Master, Sect Master, and True Master**, requesting them to **announce to the Divine Bureau Officials and Soldiers**, awaiting their deployment.

Upon completion, **write a decree** and dispatch **the Left and Right Grand Generals and their troops of ten thousand** to the afflicted household first. They shall **encircle the dwelling** and send **two divine talismans**.
The **Generals** shall command the **Gods of Destiny** to **urgently seize the malevolent ghosts and bandits** within the petitioner’s body, **forbidding them to flee**, and await further orders.

If the malevolent person is outside, **immediately convene the local community** and **urgently press them into the household**.
The **Exorcist** shall summon the **Divine Generals and troops** to return the petitioner home, preparing **incense and offerings**.
Upon arriving at the afflicted household, the **Exorcist** shall **recite the Six Ding Talisman**—the **Master’s Talisman**—and **assign the petitioner as the Chief General of the Current Bureau** to capture the malevolent spirits.
Then, **burn one talisman**, leading the **Divine Soldiers and Officials** in a **ten-thousand-strong army**, with **drums and gongs** resounding, **encircling the afflicted** from all four directions, **binding above and below** the malevolent ghosts.
With **步禹步 (Bu Yu Bu)**, proceed to the afflicted’s residence, **directly to the Heavenly Gate**.
Recite the **Heavenly Ding Talisman**; the **petitioner** shall be a **Heavenly Ding Warrior**.
Upon sighting the malevolent person, **recite the Combat Talisman**, the **Thunderfire Talisman**, and **burn the Lightning Talisman** to **seize malevolent spirits**, directing the flames to the doorstep.
Again with **步禹步 (Bu Yu Bu)**, enter with the **left hand reciting the Talismans of the Tiger, Rabbit, and Horse Hours**, and the **right hand reciting the Combat Talisman**.
Assign the **two Combat Talismans** to the head, with the **□罡星 (Gang Star)** pointing forward.
At the hall, the **Exorcist** stands **back to the □ (Gui), facing the Gang Star**, **offers incense**, and commands the **Divine Generals and Soldiers** to **urgently seize and bind the malevolent spirits**, awaiting their response.
Then, **order them to be carried out** and apply the **Heavenly Ding Talisman** to **bind the malevolent spirits**, along with the **Divine Warriors and Talismans** previously summoned.
At first sight of the afflicted, the **left hand recites the Heavenly Ding Binding Talisman**, and the **right hand recites the Combat Talisman**, using the **left hand’s Talisman to strike the lower ribs**.
The **left fist** becomes the **Gang Star**, the **right elbow** the **□ (Gui) Star**, the **left shoulder** the **□ (Gui)**, the **heart** the **□ (Gui)**, the **right shoulder** the **□ (Gui)**, the **right elbow** the **□ (Gui)**, and the **right fist** the **□ (Gui) Star**.
When the **stars’ radiance** fills the chest, the **left hand recites the Chenwen Talisman**, and the **Exorcist** shouts:
*"You are what malevolent spirit that harms the King’s subjects?*
*I am commissioned by the **Supreme Emperor**, here to **investigate you**—speak truly, or I shall **proceed with interrogation**!"*

After issuing commands, **quickly bind** the **right fist and left elbow** with the **Heavenly Ding Talisman** for **urgent interrogation**.
If they still do not confess, **bind them with the Heavenly Ding Seal** and **pierce their mouth** with the **Golden Staff**.
If they still refuse, **shackle them** and **recite the Thunderfire Lightning Talisman**—they shall **speak immediately**.
After **three thorough interrogations**, if the truth is confirmed, **order the Divine Generals to seize the ghosts and bandits**, and **immediately grant relief** to the afflicted, giving them the **talisman to swallow**.
**Offer incense daily**, and the **Divine Generals** shall **quickly deliver the malevolent spirits** for **final disposition** and **return them to their proper domain**.

**Seizing Wicked and Malevolent Ghosts**:
If there are **wicked and malevolent ghosts**, with petitions submitted and **repeated exorcisms failing**, record the **circumstances** in the petition and **dispatch to the Supreme Emperor, the Three Masters, and the Five Peaks**, notifying the **City Deities** or visiting **nearby sacred shrines**. On a **fixed day**, convene and proceed to the afflicted household, **seizing and executing the ghosts and bandits**, establishing an **instant tribunal** for judgment and dispatch.

On the appointed day, at dawn, summon the **Eight-Directional Pursuit Generals**—**Yang Shun** as the **Vanguard General**—and **issue the talisman** to **cross the dry and wet** and **fly to Heaven** to request troops.
Then, **one by one**, dispatch the **Divine Generals and Officials** of the **Current Bureau**, following the same method as before.
Upon entering, the **left hand recites the Talisman of Malevolent Spirits**, and the **right hand recites the Combat Talisman**, binding the malevolent spirits as previously described.
With **步地纪斗 (Bu Di Ji Dou)**, proceed directly to the hall, **back to Gui, facing Gang**, and **shout** to summon the **Divine Soldiers and Officials** of the **Current Bureau**, **urgently leading troops** to **supervise and bind** the afflicted household, the **Five Paths of Earth**, and related deities.
All shall be **seized and delivered immediately** to the **tribunal** for judgment.
The **Current Bureau** establishes the tribunal, **interrogates and commands** as decided, **reciting the two Talismans**, **grasping the malevolent Seal**, and **reciting the Yin Combat Talisman**.

The officers and soldiers stand arrayed to the left and right.

Seize the malevolent spirits and hold them fast—like a calamity, they shall make no sound or movement.
Once captured, immediately apply the **shackling cangue Seal** upon them, then burn the **Responsive Cangue Ghost-Soldier Talisman**. Next, pinch the **Ziwei Seal**, arrange the **Hexagram of Heaven (乾)** and deploy the **Combat Array**. Shout aloud while reciting the **Ziwei Incantation to the Heavenly and Earthly Spirits**, commanding them to be bound.
If they remain unsubdued, then summon the **Golden Blade Spirit Official** to subdue them, grasp the **Heavenly Ding Seal**, and recite the **Heavenly Ding Incantation**, invoking the **Ten Directions’ Heavenly Ding Warriors** to bind them in the air.
If no form or shadow appears, swallow the **Healing Talisman**, then press the **Subduing Evil Talisman** upon them—this is infallible.

**Demolishing the Malevolent Shrine**
When a petitioner reports that an unauthorized shrine or a haunted grove, tree, or spirit frequently disturbs the land, bewitching women, invading fields and homes, and falsely demanding sacrifices, the case must be meticulously documented and submitted for judgment. Request that the **Current Bureau’s soldiers**, the **Ten Directions’ Heavenly Ding Warriors**, and the relevant **Sacrificial Deities** assemble to suppress the disturbance.

On the appointed morning, inscribe the **Subduing Evil Talisman** on four wooden plaques, each seven *cun* long and three *cun* wide. After offering incense, arrange the **Hexagram of Heaven (乾)** and deploy the **Combat Array**, then fly as a spirit to petition above for the cause of the calamity. Next, step through the **Earth-Memory Array** and dispatch the **commander** with attendants bearing the talismans to enter the shrine directly.

Recite the **Personal Destiny Incantation**—*Chen*—and summon the **Spirit Officials**, arraying them to the left. With the right hand, grasp the **Northern Emperor Seal-Incantation**, invoking the **Three Teachers** and the **Great Emperor of the Northern Pole**, leading the soldiers, **Heavenly Ding Warriors**, the **Six Jia and Six Ding**, and the **Crushing Demon Thunder Division** to follow in the clouds behind you.

Recite the incantation, then grasp the **Ziwei Seal**, mentally invoking the **Great Emperor of the Northern Pole**, the **Three Enclosures**, and the **Northern Dipper’s Natural Covering Head**. Again, deploy the **Flying Combat Array**, invoking the **Seven Stars in Crossed Array** to envelop the shrine’s form.

Proceed to the shrine’s entrance, fly through the **Heavenly Gang**, step through the **Earth-Memory Array**, and command the **Supervising Officials** to shout each name in turn. The aforementioned soldiers and generals must urgently seize them all under your command.

Burn the **Commanding Demon-Scout Ghost Talisman**, declaring: *"These are demonic bandits—command them seized!"* Deploy the **Thunderfire Talisman**, burning it thoroughly. The **Teacher** invokes lightning—**crackling thunder shakes the earth**, flames fill the sky, and the officials raise their voices in triumph as they seize them.

Next, nail the **Iron Talisman** into the four cardinal directions of the shrine’s grounds, reciting the **Heavenly Gate and Earthly Axis Incantation**, invoking the **Four Directions’ successive movements**—thus, the demons have no place to enter. Reward the officials and soldiers—this method is supremely effective.
Do not use it habitually.

---

**Method for Invoking Rain in the Height of Summer**

A private chamber must be prepared, swept clean and made pure. Twelve measures of wine, one rooster, and offerings to the **Suppressing Demon** division’s middle-ranking generals are required.

With sword in hand, face the **Xun** direction. Draw a three-tiered altar, upon which are placed wine cups, incense lamps, and tea and fruit. In ritual formation, step toward the **Xun** door and assume the guise of a **Divine General**, sword pointing to the **Xun** direction, and loudly declare:

*"By the command of the Supreme Emperor, I urgently suppress the **Demon Division**. I call each name in turn and summon the **Five Directions’ Barbarian Thunder** messengers. On this month’s certain day, they must swiftly assist me in searching through streams and abyssal pools. Surely there are **Dragon Gods** present—hurry to [specific location], and save all the people from scorching drought!"*

*"Now, in accordance with the law, I have prepared blood wine and **zào money** to reward the **Thunder Division**. On the appointed day and hour, you must govern the great rain—do not defy my command!"*

When the incantation is finished, pour out the wine, and with the sword’s blade pierce the rooster, mixing its blood into the wine until it is evenly blended. The **Thunder Division** generals of the Five Directions will then appear before the altar to receive the sacrifice.

After the ritual is complete, dig a pit facing the **Xun** direction within the chamber, and bury the **zào money** and rooster’s blood wine. Place the sword upright upon it, then exit the chamber. As prescribed, prepare the **Rain-Invoking Talisman** and have someone cast it into the location where the **Dragon Gods** dwell.

When the time arrives, great thunder and rain will descend, relieving the drought. Then, give thanks to Heaven’s grace.

**Praying for Clear Weather**

In general, the **Flying Xun** incantation can subdue **Sky Gods**, while the **Treading Ji** incantation can subdue **Earthly Deities**. To govern the **Three Realms’** ghosts and gods, one must not neglect the **Flying Xun** and **Treading Ji** methods—how else could one achieve great deeds and manifest **virtue/power**, if these were mere empty exertions of effort?

For calming **void-dwelling malevolent ghosts** or **frenzied winds and torrential rains**, and for traversing perilous seas or mountains in times of danger, these methods suffice.

If the **Subduing Frenzied Evil** method is employed, the left and right hands must be reversed and the steps retraced.

Next, use the **Flying Xun** and **Treading Ji** incantations. With the right hand, point to the direction of the calamity, and the ghosts and gods will collapse, the clouds and rains will disperse, all **demons and malevolent forces** will be annihilated, and **prolonged rains** will not harm crops or people.

If a violent wind snaps trees, the ritual master must transform into a **Divine General** in **auspicious attire**, arrange the items in reverse order, and then recite the **Flying Xun** and **Treading Ji** incantations three times. With the right hand, point to the clouds and loudly declare:

*"By the command of the Supreme Emperor, I order the violent winds and torrential rains to cease immediately! You **Dragon Gods** who command the clouds, swiftly obey the imperial decree and disperse the clouds, halting the rain!"*

The winds and rains will then stop. If they do not, repeat the method, using the **Binding Dragon Spirit Official** to subdue them—this is supremely effective.

Next, petition the **Supreme Emperor’s Three Teachers**, and inform the **Dragon God Master of Rain** to swiftly forbid the rain. Set the **Altar of Transmission and Oath** in proper order:

*"This humble servant of [specific village], holding the office of [specific position], surnamed [surname], aged [number], born in the year [year]. I am under the jurisdiction of the **Big Dipper’s** [specific star] Lord. Deeply moved by the insignificant merits of this humble one, I reverently admire the **Dao/Way’s** transformations. With sincere devotion, I humbly present this pledge of sincerity, proffering it to the door of [surname] Lord. I seek to beg for the transmission of the **Highest Celestial’s** **Divine Constellation’s** **Long-Life**, **Protect-Life**, **Guardian of Immortality’s** secret method—one **school’s** talismans, diagrams, seals, and incantations. I vow to assist Heaven in its transformations, aid the state in saving its people, preserve my life and cultivate **authentic virtue**, and cut off evil to return to the right path."*

*"After receiving this method, it shall forever be a treasure of my body. I dare not disobey the Teacher’s words or recklessly transmit this to others, nor leak the sacred texts. Should I violate this even once, I shall willingly offer my body to the **Three Officials**, be tried by the **Wind Blade**, and bring misfortune upon the **Mysterious Ancestors**. I will not be pardoned in ten thousand kalpas, nor dare I blame the **Dao/Way** or accuse the Teacher."*

*"I have solemnly presented this petition, awaiting the Teacher’s compassionate grace to grant me the opportunity to prostrate and plead. I humbly await the Teacher’s command."*

*"This humble servant, [surname], now holding the office of [specific position], has submitted the above petition in accordance with the ritual. Since it has been seen and the oath is most earnest, I dare not refuse. I humbly present this petition, offering it to the **Supreme Emperor’s** **Highest Celestial’s** **Jade Purity True King of Divine Constellation’s** **Great Emperor of Long-Life** before the altar. I await the grace to issue a decree, informing the **True Officials of the Purple Bureau** to verify the above and transmit the method to the disciple. Should I or the disciple have any offenses, grant or withhold transmission as appropriate. I pray for the Emperor’s benevolent decree to be revealed to me in dreams or waking, so that I may rely upon it to perform the transmission."*

*"I am sincerely fearful and trembling, bowing my head and kneeling. I have solemnly presented this petition, awaiting the imperial decree."*

「The **Grand Marshal of the Year** (太歲), in the month and day of his position, humbly submits this memorial (具位臣姓某狀奏).

The newly appointed **transmission site** (授法址) is hereby called by imperial decree (勑) to the **Three Celestial Purities’** **Heavenly Gate** (三天門下). According to the petition of **Official Certain** (某官某人), I respectfully recommend **Person Certain** (某人), whose innate nature is pure and unadulterated, and whose resolve is steadfast and true. He reverently upholds the **Highest Celestial** (高真), and constantly takes refuge in the **Great Dao** (大道). He possesses a sincere heart for benefiting the nation and saving the people, and wishes to transmit the **Supreme Emperor’s** **Jade Purity True King of Divine Constellation’s** **Highest Celestial’s** **Preserved Immortal Secret Dao** (保仙秘法), safeguarding life and protecting the body, aiding the Celestial in its transformations, exterminating malevolent spirits (邪祟), and bringing relief to the people. I was born in the year of **Jia (甲) and Xian (建)**, and my fate is governed by the **Certain Star Lord of the Northern Dipper** (北斗某星君), awaiting his manifest response.

The **Recommending Master** (保舉師) submits this memorial: **Official Certain** (臣姓某).
The **Supervising Master** (監度師) submits this memorial: **Official Certain** (臣姓某).
The **Transmitting Master** (度師) submits this memorial: **Official Certain** (臣姓某).

The **Supreme Celestial Dao** (神霄大法) is the refuge of all ten thousand Dao paths (萬道同皈). How much easier is its practice than the difficulty of cultivating sincerity in one’s heart! It is fitting to appoint **Person Certain** as a **Celestial Purity’s Peace-Aiding Transformation Disciple** (太平辅化弟子), to practice the **Supreme Celestial Dao**, and to conduct the affairs of the **Right Hall Military Assembly and Scriptural Repository** (右殿軍同會書府事), following the prescribed procedures and reporting accordingly.

This decree (右牒) is issued by the **Three Pure Ones’ Jade Emperor** (奉三清玉帝), and the **Transmitting Master** (度師) submits this memorial: **Official Certain** (臣姓某).

**True Master:** **Lord Han of the Nine Heavens’ Beneficial Calculations and Life-Saving** (九天益算司命好生韓君丈人真君).
**Lineage Master:** **Lord of the Azure Flower Great Dao** (青華大帝君).
**Ancestral Master:** **Lord of the Long-Life Great Dao** (長生大帝君).

**Precepts and Rituals** (戒牒式):
To **Person Certain**, the Disciple (牒弟子某人):

According to the petition of **Disciple Certain** (弟子某), whose hunger and thirst for the Dao are evident, and whose resolve is firm as metal and stone, he seeks to inherit the **orthodox transmission** (正法) and requests instruction in the **secret teachings** (秘訓). This earnest devotion is commendable and worthy of praise. After first reporting to the **Imperial Court** (帝阙) and then submitting to the **True Officials** (真司), in accordance with the **mysterious principles** (玄科), he receives the **transmitted essence** (奧旨) with the oversight of all the Celestial Deities (諸天監度), the verification of all the Saints (眾聖证明), the support of the **Divine Generals** (神將贊扶), and the protection of the **Celestial Bureaucracy** (吏兵翊衛). Thus, he is qualified to fulfill his duties and attain the **rank of immortality** (仙階). He may now kneel and receive his official title in accordance with the **certificate of appointment** (簡券).

All the **precept texts** (戒文) should be reverently accepted and upheld. They are listed as follows:

First, the **Three Compliance Precepts** (三遵戒):
1. Do not betray or defy Heaven and Earth (不得負違天地).
2. Do not rebel against or disrespect one’s parents, teachers, and friends (不得悖逆父母師友).
3. Do not disobey the teachings and commands of the Master (不得違師所行教令).

Next, the **Five Precepts of Conduct** (五戒行):
1. Abstain from lust and greed (戒非色非財).
2. Refrain from killing and causing harm (戒殺物傷情).
3. Avoid strange desires, jealousy, and deceit (戒怪貪嫉拓).
4. Do not seek favor through crooked or insidious means (戒請曲邪佞).
5. Maintain equanimity and avoid erratic moods (戒喜怒變常).

Next, the **Seven Rectitudes** (七正直):
1. Let **orthodox faith** (正信) be the foundation of goodness (以正信為善根).
2. Let **orthodox sincerity** (正真) and mindfulness be the means to align with the Celestial Will (以正真留意，上應天心).
3. Let **loyalty** (忠) benefit the nation and **filial piety** (孝) be reverent toward one’s kin (以忠利於國，孝穆於親).
4. Let **orthodox faith** (正信) follow the Master’s instructions (以正信從師訓).
5. Let **rectitude** (正直) harmonize with one’s relatives and dependents (以正直和穆六親眷屬).
6. Let **orthodox discernment** (正絶) reject falsehood and avoid entanglement with evil (以正絶聽是非，邪不干正).
7. Let **honest transactions** (市價斗稱) be conducted with fairness and straightforwardness (平直交易).

Next, the **Six Prohibitions Against Listening to Crooked Speeches** (六不聽曲詞):
1. Do not accept petitions from those who harbor resentment, jealousy, or deceit, or whose motives are unclear (察有嗔妬奸濫不明者，不得受狀).
2. Do not accept petitions from people who deceive, steal, or engage in clandestine affairs (凡人欺詐奸竊，事屬暗昧，不得受狀).
3. Do not accept petitions from those who falsely accuse others to incite officials or soldiers, causing harm or injury to others (假以財物，求梼妄動吏兵，害物傷命，不得受狀).
4. Do not hear cases from envious monks who seek vengeance against others (為冤僧嫉妬，欲求報對者，不得受理).
5. Do not accept petitions regarding unclear property disputes or the pursuit of deceased individuals’ belongings through dubious means (財物不明，亡者往來追攝，似乎機變者，不得受理).
6. Do not hear cases from those who falsely sue officials, seeking punishment after a clear judgment has already been made (民有冤枉，已經明斷，妄訟官吏，欲求警報者，不得受理).

The decree is as stated above. I humbly pray to follow the **rituals and principles** (科式), without failing in propriety and decorum (毋失規儀).」

「Diligently cultivate and uphold the **precepts** (修持), laboring in the **sacred rites** (香火). Cherish the radiance of the Three Lights (味三光之焕景), and bear the talismans of the Six Heavenly Stems (佩六甲之符章). Safeguard life and protect the body, aiding Heaven and assisting the realm (佐天助国).

When calamities arise—whether locusts and caterpillars (螟蝗) wreak havoc, or floods and droughts (水旱) go unchecked—when malevolent spirits (精魅) act as demons (为妖), or when living beings suffer from sickness and woe (生灵疾苦), attend to all matters, great or small, and **exterminate demons and avert calamities** (按律诛禳) in accordance with the **Daoist laws** (律).

Do not **amass wealth** (殖货财), nor **favor flatterers** (私谄曲). Do not **betray trust** (勿背盟约), nor **leak sacred secrets** (泄慢枢机). May the **Dao** flourish in its practice (使教法以兴行), and may all beings turn toward faith (俾众生而向信). Heaven’s judgment is near—let this be your earnest admonition (天鉴不远，宜勉之).

Thus the decree (故牒).
**Great Year** (太岁) [of the] [Year] [Month] [Day] [Hour] [Decree] (年月日时牒).

**Recommended for promotion** (保举): Daoist Master [Name Redacted] (师具位), surname [Redacted] (姓某), seal [Redacted] (押).
**Overseen by the Daoist Patriarch** (监度): Daoist Master [Name Redacted] (师具位), surname [Redacted] (姓某), seal [Redacted] (押).
**Ordained by the Daoist Patriarch** (度师): [Name Redacted] (具法位), surname [Redacted] (姓某), seal [Redacted] (押).

**Supplementary Note** (补帖):
To the **Office of the Supreme Daoist Court of the Jade Purity** (玉清神霄大法司):

The said office, in accordance with native records (乡贯), having presented **pledges and credentials** (赍质信) to the door of [Name Redacted] (某君), should now transmit the **Sacred Secrets of the Highest Daoist Rite** (高上神霄保仙秘法). Beyond those already reported to the Three Masters (三师), this further supplements the **Highest Daoist Rite of the Great Peace** (高上神霄太平辅化), where the disciple [Name Redacted] (弟子) practices the **Supreme Daoist Rite** (神霄大法) and holds the **post of Right-Side Hall Military and Scriptural Affairs** (右殿军同会书府事法职), requiring issuance of this **certificate for verification** (出帖照会).

This decree (右牒) is hereby entrusted to [Name Redacted] (某) for safekeeping (收执).

The **Sacred Daoist Texts of the Jade Purity** (神霄玉文) and the **Secrets of the Pure Court** (琼台秘诀) encompass all things without exception, their scope unbounded. If one cherishes these **Sacred Treasures** (自宝) and upholds them faithfully, then in **stillness** (坐众妙) one attains the myriad wonders, and **arising** (立至万神) one reaches the ten thousand deities. In **serene repose** (寂然不动), one’s **Dao-qi** (感) flows naturally and **harmonizes** (遂通).

How could one not **strive with sincerity** (勉励精诚) and **supplicate the True One** (上祈真贶) for blessings?

If one **procrastinates after initial diligence** (初勤终怠) or **speaks falsely while claiming otherwise** (口是心非), the **Spiritual Officials of the Dao** (法中灵官) will record their **merits and demerits** (功过) without fail, even to the minutest detail (毫分无失). Then shall the Five Emperors (五帝) **declare their deeds** (言功), and the Three Officials (三官) shall **not dare to register them in their ledgers** (鼓笔).

Let there be no **grievance against the Master’s words** (无怨师言)—this is most earnestly admonished (切宜勉之).

Conform to this decree and carry it out accordingly (准此奉行).」

「太歲 年 月 日 帖。
**Presented by the Celestial Officials of the Dao-Year, Month, and Day:**
The **Dao-qi Master** (保舉師具位) of rank **某**, surnamed **某**.
The **Dao-qi Supervisor** (監度師具位) of rank **某**, surnamed **某**.
The **Dao-qi Degree Master** (度師具法位) of rank **某**, surnamed **某**.

**Official Notification to the Three Heavens (勑三天門下):**
According to the **Jade Sluice Petition** (玉闙奏下), there is a **Dao-qi adept** (元修真之士) of rank **某**, who has **complied with the Dao-qi regulations** (依科奉行).
In the year **某**, month **某**, day **某**, he **assisted the Celestial Powers in their transformations** (佐天行化) and **aided the state in saving its people** (助國救民).
**□□ arrived and □□ was protected** (□到□保明), and he **petitions to be transferred in rank** (乞依科遷), **to assume the title of certain Dao-qi rank** (補佩某品仙階), as **the one who executed this** (施行者).
**Rightly so, this official** (本官) of **certain rank** (品) **possesses a humble and harmonious nature** (禀性谦和), **and diligently practices the Dao-qi precepts** (精修奉戒).
His **universal salvation of the people** (普救人民) **earns him great merit and virtue** (功德甚重), and the **Heavenly Hosts rejoice** (諸天稱慶).
It is **proper to grant his request** (宜依拟補某官) and **to follow the Celestial Decree** (奉上帝勑命指揮), as stated above (奉如右).
**Upon receipt of the talisman, this shall be carried out** (符到奉行), **in strict accordance with the Highest Dao-qi Jade Purity True King’s statutes and decrees** (一如高上神霄玉清真王律令勑).

太歲 年 月 日。
**Presented by the Dao-qi Master** (具位) of rank **某**, surnamed **某**.

**Appeal for the Borrowed Soldiers of Mount Tai (申泰山借兵馬式):**
To the **Jade Purity Dao-qi Grand Office** (玉清神霄大法司):
This office **has already, in the current month on day certain, at hour certain** (已於今月某日某時), **submitted a petition to the Dao-qi Jade Purity Palace** (告下神霄玉清府劫命符文一道), **requesting the loan of soldiers from Mount Tai** (關借泰山兵馬若干), **to be dispatched to certain location** (就某處), **for a person afflicted by a prolonged illness** (為某人染患日久), **whose medicinal treatments have been ineffective** (服藥無效).
This office **has carefully examined the matter** (看詳委) and **determines that malevolent spirits are conspiring to cause harm** (是有邪神通同為禍).
**Together with this office’s soldiers and generals** (同共本司兵將), **they shall search out and capture these malevolent spirits** (搜捉邪祟) and **execute the proper Dao-qi remedies** (根治施行).
This shall be **reported upon completion** (須至申聞者).
**Rightly so, this office respectfully submits a statement** (右謹具狀), **to Mount Tai’s Eastern Peak Dao-qi Palace** (申 泰山東岳府), **humbly beseeching their instructions** (伏乞指揮).
**Selecting capable soldiers and generals** (選差得力兵馬), **heroic commanders and fierce leaders** (雄將猛帥), **with urgency, they shall proceed to the site** (火急前至地頭), **to jointly assist in the rescue** (同共救應).
Once the **meritorious Dao-qi work is accomplished** (善功畢日), **they shall promptly return and report** (即便回申), **in accordance with the Dao-qi regulations** (依法祇應).
**Daring to presume upon their authority** (干冒威聽), **this office awaits their gracious response** (伏候照報).
**Respectfully submitted statement** (謹狀).
**Presented by the Dao-qi Master** (具位) of rank **某**, surnamed **某**, on the **Celestial Year-Month-Day** (太歲 年 月 日).

To the **Jade Purity Dao-qi Grand Office** (玉清神霄大法司):
This office **yesterday, in month certain, day certain, at hour certain** (昨於某月某日某時), **submitted a petition to the Dao-qi Jade Purity King’s Palace** (告下神霄玉清王府勑命符文), **requesting the loan of soldiers from Mount Tai** (關借泰山兵馬若干), **who were dispatched to a certain household in a certain location** (於某處某家).

there is clearly a **male child registration (兒注)**—
the **calling and naming are distinct (相呼分明).**

「The offense deserves ten thousand deaths, yet I humbly present this memorial in supplication, awaiting Your divine decree.

I now submit this petition. The **Celestial Sovereign** (*Tàisuì*) of the year, month, and day, along with my surname, certain, hereby memorialize.

Furthermore, I memorialize the **Nine-Heaven Supreme Unity officials** (*Jiǔtiān Tàiyī Zàngrén*), whose ranks include:
- The **Supreme Unity Lord of True Virtue** (*Zàngrén Zhēnjūn*)
- The **Supreme Unity Lord of Ten Thousand Blessings** (*Wànfú Zhēnjūn*)
- The **Supreme Unity Lord of True Fate** (*Sīmìng Zhēnjūn*)
- The **Supreme Unity Lord of True Register** (*Zhǎngjí Zhēnjūn*)
- The **Supreme Unity Lord of True Plan** (*Zhǎngchóu Zhēnjūn*)
- The **Supreme Unity Lord of True Expiation** (*Quèxié Zhēnjūn*)
- The **Supreme Unity Lord of True Rectification** (*Dìngjí Zhēnjūn*)
- The **Supreme Unity Lord of True Benevolence** (*Zhùshàn Zhēnjūn*)
- The **Supreme Unity Lord of True Protection of Life** (*Hùshēng Zhēnjūn*)

Humbly, I await Your true compassion to review my memorial and grant me Your divine command. I beseech that the **Nine-Heaven Supreme Unity’s Officials of Expiation and Subjugation of Malevolence** (*Jiǔtiān Tàiyī Quèxié Guānjiāng Lìbīng*) be dispatched and descend (*chājiàng xiàfú*), uniting with those below to arrive at my home, specifically removing for this subject (*wǒ*) the following:
- The **Northern Dipper General of Fetal Death** (*Běidǒu Shā tāi Jiāngjūn*)
- The **Lord of Fetal Registration and Fetal Aversion** (*Tāizhù Tāiyàn Shénjūn*)
- The **Nine kinds of malevolent spirits** (*Huāgōng Huāmǔ, Huánghé Qiáonán, Qīnglóng, Báihǔ, Tiāngǒu, Fúmó, Shānguǐ, Fēitiān Jiǔ zhǒng xiélèi*), including:
  - The **Flower Father** and **Flower Mother** (*Huāgōng Huāmǔ*)
  - The **Yellow River Bridge Difficulty** (*Huánghé Qiáonán*)
  - The **Green Dragon** (*Qīnglóng*)
  - The **White Tiger** (*Báihǔ*)
  - The **Celestial Dog** (*Tiāngǒu*)
  - The **Non-Buddhist Demon** (*Fúmó*)
  - The **Mountain Ghost** (*Shānguǐ*)
  - The **Flying Demon** (*Fēitiān*)

To sever the male child registration’s calling and naming (*duànjué ér zhù xiàng hū*), and prevent future extinction of their lineage (*miǎnzhì rìhòu jué qí zhǒngyì*). I further pray that the **true *qi* (*zhēnqì*) of the Nine-Heaven Supreme Unity** be granted and infused into this subject (*wǒ*), and my wife, certain, to dissolve their existing fetal bonds (*xiàngqù tāiyùn chéngjié*) and permanently remove the suffering of male and female fetal registration (*yǒngwú nánnǚ chuánzhù zhī yōu*).

If my plea is granted (*guǒmóng zòuqǐng*), I shall be indebted to Your profound mercy (*yǎnghé xuānnén*). Though I dare to invoke Your true authority (*gànmào zhēnwēi*), my offense deserves ten thousand deaths, awaiting Your true decree (*fúkòu zhēnzhǐ*).」

**Translation:**

**Humble Petition**

In the year of the **Tai Sui**, on the **month** and **day**, a disciple of the Dao from [location], humble surname **[name]**, submits this petition for rain.

Your disciple, **[name]**, in deepest reverence, has heard that the **Dao** originates from **nature itself**, and its teachings unfold through **skillful means**. All who make devout supplications shall surely be answered.

According to the transmitted words of the local disciples, since **[specific time]** of this year, the **excessive yang** has wreaked havoc, and the rains have failed to arrive on time. Crops wither and dry, and the people live in dread. If this persists, next year’s harvest will fail, leaving us without sustenance. Even worse, we fear we shall be unable to meet the obligations of grain taxes. Without prayer and supplication, how can we hope for abundance?

This petition has been submitted to the local magistrate, who has ordered its implementation. Your disciple, having received this urgent plea, dare not refuse. Thus, in deepest humility, I record this petition and, risking my life, present it to the **Ancestral Teacher, the Jade Purity Emperor, and the Primordial Heavenly Venerable**.

With utmost reverence, I await **Heaven’s special decree**, that it may be issued to all concerned.

I pray that the **General of Thunder and Clouds Who Summons Rain**, the **Six Ding and Six Jia**, the **Five Thunder Marshals**, the **Thunder Department officials**, the **Wind Lord and Rain Master**, and the **Dragon Kings Who Walk the Rain**—all these assembled beings—be dispatched to the **rain-supplication altar** established by your disciple. May they unleash a **heavy downpour** to save the parched fields, that the crops may revive.

Your disciple has dared to transgress **Heaven’s authority**, deserving ten thousand deaths. In deepest terror and trembling, I prostrate myself, bowing my head to the ground, and humbly submit this petition, awaiting the **Dao’s decree**.

In the year of the **Celestial Stem**, on the **month** and **day**, your humble servant of rank **[Name]** submits this memorial.

From the **Jade Purity Supreme Clarity Great Law Bureau**,
To the **Office of the City Deity Governors of [Certain] Prefecture/State**.

Upon receiving the plea from **[Name of Petitioner]** to intervene in healing, after already issuing a **Heavenly Talisman** and **Sacred Water** to be ingested by the afflicted—with no effect yet observed—it is clear that this is a case of **malevolent spirits and rebellious demons**, requiring an official directive.

Upon receipt of this memorial, investigate the matter thoroughly and immediately summon **mighty officials and soldiers of the Dao’s might**, dispatching them to **[Name of Afflicted Family]**, to **subdue and expel the malevolent spirits**, ensuring they depart from **[Name of Afflicted Family]’s domain**.

Should they fail to comply with this directive, they shall be **formally reported to the Supreme Master of the Jade Purity**, and **standard penalties enforced**, awaiting retribution.

Respectfully memorialized.
In the year of the **Celestial Stem**, on the **month** and **day**, memorial submitted.
**Rank and Name** affixed.

Upon receiving **[Name of Petitioner]’s** persistent plea—with no signs of recovery—it is evident that **malevolent, lawless spirits** from the lower realms have gathered, **demanding blood and sustenance**, defying the Dao’s laws, **cunning and deceitful**, falsely accusing the living, **occupying their homes**, and causing **imminent harm**. **The Great General of the Thunder Array, Golden Bell, and Flowing Fire**,

**The Great General of Thunderfire**,

Should there be any delay, **standard disciplinary measures will be enforced**.

Respectfully summoned.

Further, they must **strictly command** the **Spirit of Destiny** (*司命*) and guardian deities of the household to **acknowledge their responsibility** (*各令知委*), and from this day onward, **show no leniency**, lest they **allow malevolent spirits to cause further harm** (*故纵邪祟，依前作祸*).

Additionally, they must **pursue and expel the afflicting *qi*** (*病气*) from the victim’s body, enabling them to **take medicine effectively**, **restore their spirit and vitality** (*精神附体*), and **settle their soul and calm their essence** (*魂魄安和*). **No deviation is permitted**; upon the **符’s arrival**, these orders must be **faithfully executed** (*奉行*).

**太歲　年　月　日　时下。**
**具位，姓某押。**

I command you to **extract and elevate the lost soul of the departed Certain** (*亡过某灵魂*), **swiftly remove their karmic records** (*疾除罪簿*), and **obliterate their evil roots** (*落灭恶根*). **No soul shall be detained**; they must ascend at once. **All gods must protect and guide** them, leading them directly to the **Realm of Humans and Deities** (*人天*).

According to their **karmic merit** (*随品*), they shall **receive transformation** (*受化*), be **reborn in a blessed land** (*更生福乡*). As decreed, **this command must be transmitted with urgency** (*一如告命，风火驿传*).

**太歲　年　月　日，吉时告下。**
**具法位，姓某。**

**发二符文关 玉清神霄大法司：**

This **Divine Command** (*大法司*) acts upon the **intention of the living** (*入意*), in accordance with established **doctrines** (*典*), to issue the **Sacred Daoist Talismans of the Jade Clarity** (*玉清神霄*) for **Shattering the Underworld and Extracting the Lost Soul** (*破地狱拔幽魂真符*), which must now be **urgently dispatched** (*须至关发者*).

**Rightly dispatched**, the **Divine Officer of the Earthly Dao** (*神霄地道功曹神君*) carries this **符’s decree** (*符命*), and **hastens to the Ten Directions and Three Realms** (*十方三界*), the **Boundless Divine Realm** (*无极神乡*), and the **prison overseers** (*诸狱主者*) of the **Northern Darkness of the Dark Principalities** (*北阴酆都*):

**Extract and elevate the lost soul of the departed Certain**, enabling them to **depart the Eternal Night** (*出离长夜*), **reach the Mysterious Hall** (*获诣玄坛*), and **partake in the merit** (*领沾功德*), thus **fulfilling their path to rebirth** (*充遂生方*).

**牒地府九幽都司 玉清神霄大法司：**

This **Divine Command** (*大法司*) acts upon the **supplication for the departed Certain** (*奉为某追荐*). I, Certain, **fear that their soul is detained** in the **Nine Dark Regions of the Underworld** (*九幽之境*). In accordance with this **符’s decree** (*准此符命*), I command that the **departed Certain be swiftly elevated** (*速得超生*), **cease their torment in the Cold Hall** (*罢对寒庭*), and **have their evil records expunged** (*削除恶簿*).

As per the **law of the Supreme Daoist Sovereign** (*神霄真王律令*).

**Dispatch awaiting arrival** (*牒候到*), I **humbly submit this decree** (*仰准前符命*) to the **Underworld’s Three Officials** (*地狱三官*), the **Nine Ministries** (*九府*), the **One Hundred and Twenty Departments** (*百二十曹*), the **Five Emperors’ Judges** (*五帝考官*), the **punishing deities of the Nine Dark Hells** (*九幽地狱执罚神兵*), the **prison wardens of the Bull-Head Prison** (*牛头狱卒*), the **Great Demons of the Three Realms** (*三界大魔*), and all **Underworld officials** (*地府一切冥官主者*):

**Receive this符’s decree**; the **Underworld’s torments must halt** (*地府停苦*), and upon the **符’s arrival**, these orders must be **faithfully executed** (*符到奉行*).

**Seal of the Dispatch** (*故牒*).
**太歲　年　月　日　时牒。**
**具法位，姓某押。**

---
**投简表式**

**具位，小兆，臣姓某，**
**诚惶诚恐，稽首顿首，再拜**

**上言:** I, Certain, **humble and reverent**, **prostrate myself twice** (*稽首顿首*), and **bow twice** (*再拜*), submitting this **petition** (*表式*):

I act upon the **intention of the living** (*入意*), **establishing a wish for life** (*建生*). I **humbly offer** to the **Supreme** (*上属*):

**The Certain Star of the Northern Dipper** (*北斗某星君*).

I, Certain, **have long harbored a devout aspiration** (*先有愿心*), to **pay homage to the Five Sacred Mountains and Four Great Marshes** (*朝礼五岳、四渎*), the **Heavenly Caverns of Blessed Lands** (*洞天福地*).

I **present this petition** (*献投简文*), **reporting to the Supreme Dao** (*大道*), **Heaven and Earth** (*天地*), and **the恩 of my parents** who nurtured me, as well as the **enlightening恩 of the Three Celestial Luminaries** (*三光*), the **enlightening恩 of the Sovereign, Water, and Land** (*国王、水土*), and the **enlightening恩 of my teachers, friends, and guides** (*师友传度*).

I **offer this prayer** (*上祝*): May the **current sovereign** (*当今*), **live as long as Heaven and Earth** (*寿同天地*), and **permanently govern the mountains and rivers** (*永镇山河*).

**Further Petition:**

I **also wish** that the **Way** may **remove my nine ancestral sins** (*九祖之愆*) from the past and **forgive my three lifetimes’ offenses** (*三世之罪*) in the future.

I **fortuitously encounter the holy age** (*圣代*), and **aspire to emulate the true Dao** (*真风*). Though my **coarse mortal body** (*俗骨*) and **ordinary life** (*凡胎*) are burdened with **long-standing remorse** (*尤悔*), my **practice of the Dao remains shallow** (*道行闻浅*), and I **fail to grasp ultimate truth** (*至真*).

Unworthy to **penetrate mysteries and attain profound insight** (*通幽洞彻*), I **cannot accumulate merit to repay** (*积功图报*).

With reverence, I **hear of the Five Sacred Mountains and Four Great Marshes**, the **Heavenly Caverns of Blessed Lands** (*洞天福地*), and the **Purple Palace of True Capital** (*紫府真都*), the **sole abode where Immortals descend to bless** (*神仙降佑之乡*).

Thus, I, a **seeker of the Dao** (*学道祈求之士*), **humble myself before the True Spirit** (*真灵*), beseeching **gracious discernment** (*洞鉴*).

May You **pardon all my transgressions** (*过咎*) and **cleanse my sins** (*愆尤*).

Grant that my **Daoist rites and talismans** (*法箓*) may **sever evil** (*斩邪*), so that I may **return to the True Immortals** (*归正仙*).

With **martial assistance** (*兵佐助*) to **guide my path** (*随行*), I shall **cultivate the Dao and refine my essence** (*修真*), **transcending the mundane to attain sainthood** (*超凡入圣*).

I am **utterly moved and earnest** (*无任激切*), my **devotion unshaken** (*屏营之至*).

Respectfully spoken:

**The Celestial Year** (*太岁*) of **Year**, **Month** of **Month**, **Day** of **Day**,
**Possessed by the Dao** (*法位*), **Small Seal** (*小兆*), **Subject** (*臣*) **Certain** (*姓某*) **petitions** (*表奏*).

**Petition to the Holy Mother** (*奏圣母式*)
**Possessed by the Dao** (*法位*), **Small Seal** (*小兆*), **Subject** (*臣*) **Certain** (*姓某*).

I **do not fear the punishment of the executioner’s axe** (*斧越之诛*), and **dare to seek audience with the Supreme Primordial** (*重玄之听*).

「I, your humble servant, was yesterday instructed by **Reverend Master** (*度师*) **Certain** (*某君*) of the Inner Mongolia region in the **Jade Purity, Divine Dawn** (*玉清神霄*) **Great Dao** (*大法*), including the **One Stage God-General** (*一阶神将*) **talismans and seals** (*符印*), vowing to **assist the Celestial True One** (*天真*) in **propagating the orthodox transformation** (*宣扬正化*), **relieving the people’s suffering** (*救民疾苦*), **curing illnesses and banishing malevolent spirits** (*治病除邪*), and **refining both body and mind** (*修炼身心*), with the aspiration to **ascend to the Jade Bureau** (*升玉府*).

In reflection, your servant is a **filthy mortal in a degenerate age** (*浊世行尸*), of **profane essence** (*凡间秽质*), yet by **fate’s grace** (*宿运*), I was placed among humanity, and through **fortune’s blessing** (*真荃*), I received the **Great Dao** (*大法*). I **rely on the lofty immortals** (*高真*) to **bestow mercy upon the world** (*俯垂济世*).

Though my **virtue is slight and my Dao shallow** (*功微道浅*), my **power is meager and my conduct weak** (*德薄行衰*), I have **recklessly advanced to the Immortal Stage** (*滥进仙阶*), yet no **meritorious deeds** (*有功可记*) are recorded in my **actions and retreats** (*行藏*).

Thus, I have **offended in both motion and stillness** (*致犯动静成愆*), and **my mouth, hands, heart, and body have violated the Dao’s prohibitions** (*口掌心身有违科禁*). With **ten thousand faults and myriad sins** (*千愆万罪*), exposed to **both light and dark punishments** (*阳过阴诛*), I **daily tremble in fear with no means to repent** (*夙夜竞惶无门忏谢*).

Fortunately, on this **auspicious day** (*吉日*), I **offer morning rites to the Primordial Lord** (*朝礼元君*), earnestly **praying for compassionate aid** (*特希哀佑*) and **merciful enlightenment** (*愍以愚蒙*).

Your servant **respectfully records this petition** (*谨录状奏*) to **those who hear** (*闻者*).

---
**Rightfully, your servant respectfully records this petition** (*右臣谨录状上奏*) and **submits it to the Primordial Dao Ancestor, Holy Mother Primordial Lord** (*元始开天道祖圣母元君御前*), humbly **hoping that the Dao’s benevolence will grant my petition** (*伏望道慈允臣所奏*), and **praying for a vigorous command** (*乞赐劲命*) to **forgive and absolve me, your servant Certain** (*赦宥臣某*), **clearing my guilt and misfortune** (*罪冤消释*), **and allowing me to attain serene peace** (*得获清宁*). Thus, your servant may **devoutly seek the Dao through the law** (*奉法求真*) and **swiftly receive the numinous response** (*速蒙灵应*), **granting my sincere prayers immediate communion** (*允臣虔祷立获感通*).

**Ever indebted to the boundless Dao’s grace** (*仰荷大道罔极之恩*), your servant is **utterly moved and earnest** (*无任激切*), **devotion unshaken** (*屏营之至*). I **respectfully submit this** (*谨具以闻*).

**Respectfully submitted** (*谨奏*).
**The Celestial Year** (*太岁*) of **Year**, **Month** of **Month**, **Day** of **Day**,
**Possessed by the Dao** (*具位*), **Small Seal** (*小兆*), **Subject** (*臣*) **Certain** (*姓某*) **petitions** (*状*).

**Submitted to the Three Teachers** (*奏三师*)
**Possessed by the Dao** (*具位*), **Small Seal** (*小兆*), **Subject** (*臣*) **Certain** (*姓某*).

Your servant **respectfully states that** (*臣谨据某*), yesterday on **Year, Month, Day** (*某年月日*), **I suffered from** (*得何病证*) **a certain illness** (*某病*), suddenly **assailed by mountain goblins and malevolent spirits** (*山魈鬼神*), causing me to **whirl in madness day and night** (*日夜颠狂*), **to act disorderly in speech and call out in chaos** (*作乱言语呼唤*), and **to invoke myriad evil spirits** (*口称邪祟不一*).

Though I **exhausted all means through priests, shamans, and medical treatments** (*累经师巫医药*), they **failed to subdue** (*制伏不下*) the affliction, and it remains **a stubborn and cunning malevolence** (*顽猾奸狡*).

I **still fear for my life** (*尚虑性命难存*) and **grieve for my kin** (*骨肉怀忧*), unable to **find cessation** (*得止*).

Thus, I **submit my case to you, my Lord** (*具状投臣*), **pleading for salvation and treatment** (*乞行救治*).

Your servant **sees the earnestness of the supplicant’s words** (*切见本人投词恳切*), **and dare not refuse** (*不敢抑绝*). Therefore, on **Month, Day** (*今月某日*), I **shall establish the Divine Dawn Water-Fire Tribunal** (*建置神霄水火狱*) at the **east-southeast corner of Certain’s home** (*某家东南方上*), **requesting the descent of the Three Offices and Five Thunder God-Generals** (*乞降三司五雷将吏*) to **the site’s entrance** (*诣地头*), **to apprehend the mountain goblins and malevolent spirits** (*收捉某身中为祸山魈等祟*) **that plague me** (*赴狱考治*), and **to rescue and aid the living** (*救济生人*).

**This shall be done upon your decree** (*须至奏闻者*).

---
**Rightfully, your servant respectfully records this petition** (*右臣谨录状*) and **submits it** (*上奏*).」

「The venerable Patriarch, the Most Exalted God of Divine Dawn, the Jade Purity True King of Eternal Life, the宗师 (Master of the Doctrine), the Most Exalted God of Divine Dawn, the Jade Purity King of Eastern Hua, and the真师 (True Master), the Nine-Heaven Beneficent Calculator, the Lord of Destiny and Benevolent Generations, the Good-Generating Han the Elder—**humbly implore** (*伏望*) **the Heavenly Mercy** (*天慈*) **to grant favor** (*俞允*), **specially descending a decree** (*特降勑命*), **to notify the Three Offices and Five Thunders** (*告下三司五雷*), **commanding the mighty divine generals** (*部领威猛神将*), **valiant soldiers, and prison officials** (*精兵狱吏*), **to swiftly proceed to the site** (*俓诣地头*), **and apprehend the aforementioned mountain goblins** (*收捉上件山魈*), **malevolent spirits and demons** (*邪妖等祟*), **corpse spirits** (*伏尸*), **serpent spirits** (*蛇精*), **and the Five Wayfarers** (*五通*), **to bring them to the Heavenly Prison for examination and punishment** (*赴狱考治*), **and reveal their traces** (*显现综迹*).

**Then, through their intervention**, **to escort and assist in the exorcism** (*转凭解送，佐助行持*), **to relieve suffering and cure illness, to expel evil** (*救济疾苦，治病驱邪*), **and to universally grant blessings of understanding** (*咸赐感通*), **thus demonstrating the Imperial Sovereign’s virtue of nurturing life** (*以彰上帝好生之德*). Your servant **dares to presume upon** (*冒渎*) **the Heavenly Authority** (*天威*), **and the guilt is punishable by ten thousand deaths** (*罪当万死*). **Humbly awaiting your decree** (*伏候勑旨*).

**In the Year of the Great Celestial Cycle** (*太岁*), **Month, Day** (*年 月 日*).
**Submitted by** (*具位*), **your servant of surname Certain** (*臣姓某状奏*).

**To the City Deity** (*牒城隍*) **and the Jade Purity Divine Dawn Grand Marshal** (*玉清神霄大法司*), **and to the City Deity of Certain’s Prefecture and State** (*牒某府州城隍司之神*):

**Regarding the matter at hand** (*当司据某事*), **your servant humbly petitions for salvation and treatment** (*乞行救治*). Beyond the **Heavenly Talisman already bestowed** (*除已给付天符*), **and the dispatch of Heavenly generals and officials to apprehend** (*差拨天将吏兵收捉外*), **this must be carried out immediately** (*须至行遣者*).

**Urgent notification** (*牒候到*): Upon arrival, **please promptly investigate the aforementioned matter** (*请详前件事理*) and **dispatch mighty and resolute divine generals** (*火急差拨威猛有心力神将*), **commanding officials and soldiers** (*部领吏兵*), **to proceed to the site** (*前至地头*), **and join with this office’s Heavenly generals** (*会合本司天将*), **to search and capture the malevolent spirits and demons afflicting the household** (*於患家核捉为祸邪祟鬼神*), **ensuring none escape** (*毋令走透*), **and all are seized** (*须要捕获*), **to be delivered to the Heavenly Prison for punishment** (*收赴天狱施行*). If any **fail to comply** (*稍有违*), **or deviate from the above instructions** (*不依前件*), **they shall be held accountable** (*的当具奏上帝*), **and severe retribution shall follow** (*重行典宪，立俟报应*).

**Respectfully submitted** (*谨牒*).
**In the Year of the Great Celestial Cycle** (*太岁*), **Month, Day** (*年 月 日*) **notification** (*牒*).

**Submitted by** (*具位*), **your servant of surname Certain** (*姓某押*).

**Official Seal Record** (*关式*): **Jade Purity Divine Dawn Grand Marshal** (*玉清神霄大法司*):

**This office, upon receiving the afflicted’s earnest petition** (*当司据某入意遂投本司救治*), **has verified** (*寻验得*) that **malevolent spirits are indeed present and clearly malevolent** (*委有不正邪祟分明*), **and must be dispatched immediately** (*须至行遣者*).

**Rightfully, in accordance with** (*右，关准*) **the True King’s decree** (*真王勑命*), **the following are hereby ordered**:
- **Total Supervision General** (*差总监大将军*)
- **Commanding General** (*统兵大将军*)
- **□ Black General** (*□黑大将军*) *(Note: The character is unclear; possible options include "Heavenly" or "Dark," but "Black" is retained for consistency with the context of thunder generals)*
- **Historical Black General** (*历黑大将军*)
**to join with the Lord of Demons** (*会合命魔*), **leading the assault to slay demons** (*前驱杀鬼*).

**The generals, officials, and talisman bearers** (*符中将吏、功曹、符使*), **must swiftly go to the site** (*疾速前去地头*) **and search for all malevolent spirits and demons within the afflicted person** (*搜捉患人身中一切为祸鬼邪*), **regardless of rank or relation** (*不问高下亲疏*), **immediately seizing them upon their appearance** (*即仰应时摄赴患体*), **and transmitting through the proper channels** (*借口通传*). If any **do not submit** (*不伏*), **they must be interrogated and examined on the spot** (*仰一面絣吊考问*), **with no delay or negligence** (*不得慢易*). **They must await this office’s arrival for final resolution and dispatch** (*切待本司到来，结绝解送*).

**Failure to follow the law shall not be pardoned** (*倘不遵依法律，罪无轻恕*). **This is to be executed with utmost urgency** (*火急奉行*).

**Thus sealed** (*故关*).」

**Name and Rank:** [Name], [Title] in charge.

**Summoning of Officials and Soldiers:** Urgently notify the **Highest God of the Celestial Palace, the Jade Clarity King** (*高上神霄玉清王*), that the **True King’s decree** (*真王勑命*) summons **my divine soldiers** (*某神兵*).

**Talisman:** The decree summons **my generals and officials** (*某将吏多少*), ordering them to assemble at the **sacred altar** (*灵坛*) of **[Location]**, for an urgent matter.

**Highest Celestial King’s Decree:** The **Highest Celestial King** (*高上神霄王*) summons **my deity** (*某神*), to investigate the **original cause** (*元因*), and to issue a proclamation upon arrival to execute the command.

**Acting on behalf of Heaven, enforcing the Dao:** Exterminate evil and annihilate malevolent spirits (*除邪灭精*). **Thousands shall be beheaded; ten-thousands shall be presented** (*千千截首，万万来呈*). **If one fails to appear, their brains shall be shattered and their bodies destroyed** (*一人不到，碎脑殒身*).

**True King’s Command:** Let **Dragon and Tiger generals** (*龙虎*) **rush forth in unison** (*交奔*). **Divine soldiers’ commanders** (*神兵主者*), upon receiving this talisman, must act swiftly (*速行*). If there is any resistance, report it to the **Imperial Sovereign** (*帝君*). **As per the decree, transmit by wind-fire courier** (*风火驿传*).
